KAZUNDA KASIKALILEKE
Kuli nzila zinjaanji zyikonzya kuletelezya bantu kuyambukilwa kazunda kasikalileke.
Zimwinzilanzeezyi:Masena munywidwa makoko, 
mwalo bantu mobakonzya kukolwa nkabela akuli jana munkwela zitali kabotu.
Amwi masena aatali kabotu akonzya kukwelelezya bantu
kuiyambukilwa kazunda ngaaya, madolopo ajanwa muminyinza, 
mukkala bazezi banswi, mumavwuka ciindi bantu nobalonga kuti bakapaile kubusena bumwi.
Bantu balacita nkwela iitakwabilidwe mumasena oomu.
mwakweebela zilengwa Leza calo eeci cipa kusunkwa akati kabantu, 
Kapati bakubusyi nkaambo inga babula cakucita akutalika kulijana muzilenqwa zibi mbuli zyankwela.
Kuli kuyungana akati kabakubusyi kupa kulijana munkwela litakwabilwidwe.
Bucete abwalo kapati bantu bakkala mudolopo bwaleta buyumuyumu mubantu,
Bucete bulazumanana akaambo kabantu balesegwa milimo nokuba kufwidwa
bayandwa babo babagwasya. Eeci caleta buyumuyumu kuli bacaala. 
Aaba bantu kuteqwa bacikonzye kupona balatalika kulijana muzyiyanza zibi mbuli kuvwuula
kutegwa bajane mali aakuzya nzyobayanda.
Akaambo kabukkale buyumu, bamwi bantu balijana mumakwebo akukosala minyinza.
Makwebo aaya alijisi mapenzi angawo mbuli kubbadelela mpasya
nzyobaula akubbadela mwa koona, Eeci cilapa bantu kutalika zyabumpelenge mbuli
kusambala mibili yabo kutegwa bacikonzya kucita makwebo aaya.
Bukapenta abwalo bwaleta mapenzi manji kujatikizya kazunda kasikalileke.
Bakapenta baleta mapenzi manji nkaambo bantu aaba zimwi zindi balalya nkwela
abantu banji-banji litakwabilidwe calo eeci cayindizya bulwazi.
Tunsiya-nsiya mbuli 'kusalazigwa, kupalulwa,
maali atumwi atwalo twaleta mapenzi manji kujatikizya kazunda.
Kusalazigwa ncilengwa cicitwa kusola kutanda zyeelo zyamufwu. 
Bamwi bantu munkwela. Eeyi nzila lakonzya kupa kazunda kuli umwi.
Kupalulwa akalo nkalengwa kacitwa amisyobo imwi music cesu. 
Eeyi nzila ilakonzya kutabukizya kazunda kwiinda mukubelesya mbeli yomwe 
kuti kakuli ujisi kazunda akati kabo.
Mali aalo nkalengwa kamwi kacitwa amisyobo yabantu bamwi mbuli Batonga.
Muntu ujisi maali kanji-kanji ulijana mucilijazyo cakujana kazunda kasikalileke.
Mubuzyo Kweendelanya acibalo, lemba nzila zili kkumi muntu mwakonzya kulijana akazunda kasikalileke.
Kosala mutwe wamakani omwe, wamana ulembe mulaso utaleli kumabala
myaanda yotatwe acisela 
Basitunzanyu banji balabeja. Kopandulula mbocili camasimpe eeci.
Ndyoona ndyopa ndelikulya. Lemba cano cikonzya kupandulula kaambyo aaka
Kolerba lugwalo kubayiminizyi bamunanda yamilawo ubaambile buyumu-yumu
mbojana mucooko mokkala wamana ulombe lugwasyo luliloonse.
Bulwazi bwasikalileke mbwamasimpe, 
nkobuli: uti nzi akaambo aaka? Lemba mboyeeya.
Koyingula mibuzyo yone, omwe-omwe kuzwa mukabbuku komwe-komwe.
Kalimanzila mulimi wa Cilimino ca Bbondo wakatalika kuya ansi mubulimi bwakwe. 
Kopa twaambo tosanwe twakapa kuti bulimi buye ansi.
"Me biya me twaambo tuli boobu tulandicima cime 
Nguni wakaamba majwi aaya?
Wakali Kwaambila ni?
Twaambo nzi twakali kumucima?
Cakali ciindi nzi cakumwaka naakakatazya muntu yu?
Ncinzi cimbi cakajanika?
KUZYALWA KWA MUTONGA (Nkamu ya Mukanzubo) 
Mukaintu ulaa da iyisi maumi obilo mumuntu omwe, 
buumi bwakwe mwini abuumi bwamwana ngwayumwide.
Aboobo kuli milawo njayelede kutobela kukwabilila maumi aaya obilo
Lemba zyintu zyosanwe nzyatayelede kucita mukaintu ulaa da.
Pandulula ncaamba mabala aaya kweendelana ambwaakabelesegwa mubbuku oomu:
"Akaambo kankamu ezi kutamvwana kwatalika banabokwabo wabasula
Nguni wakali kwaamba majwi aaya?
wakali kwaamba nkamu nzi?
Mbaani bakali kwaambwa?
Ncinzi cakaletelezya kuti mwaambi ooyu aambe boobu?
Ndulayo nzi sikwaamba ndwasola kutondezya kubantu babala bbuku eeli?
Muciindi caba nakalindu, milimo nzi basimbi njobakali kubelekela bamayi
kulikombelezya kwiiya? Kolemba yosanwe.
Tondezya kaambyo aaka mbokabelesedwe kweendelanya ambookabala bbuku eeli,
 "konabula mukowa koombe kokwete." 
Tondezya munzila zyotatwe eeci mbocilibonya boobu.
"Mboobu baacisya mbobaalupengela lubono.
Nguni wakaamba majwi aaya?
Wakali kwaambila ni?
Mbaani zyina baacisyanyina muntu ooyu?
Ino musamu walubono bakaujana kuli ni?
Mizeezo ya kachila yakazwidilila buti? Lemba cakacitika.
Kufwiinsya cibalo Bala cibalo citobela wamana ucifwiinsye kutaindilila mabala mwaanda.
'Mwanaangu ino busongo obu butola kuli? Swebo tobamwi inga twatalika
kuyoowa nkaambo meso esu akabona zyinji zyiyoosya. 
Aalo matwi akamvwa zyinji zyigambya." Mbwaakatalika kwaamba akutongooka munene Chigabwa
naakayeeya mbubakali kupona myaaka yainda. 
Wakali kkede amwanaakwe Cheelo kabalya musalo.
Munene ooyu wakasakana mumizeezo naakabona zyakali kucitika. 
Wakatalika kati, "Mwanaangu, kaindi bulimi bwakali kabotu kapati nkaambo kumakani abulimi, 
tiibwakali kupenzya mbuli mazuba ano. Imvwula yakali kuwa muciindi ceelede, 
kwakanyina cilanga mbuli ciba ano mazuba. Inyika yakajisi munzuka, kwakanina kuula camuntunzya.
Kwakanyina kuula mbuto zyacikuwa, ngamunya amubutala akali kubelesegwa amana kaabbala. 
Twakali kutebula kabotu kakunyina mapenzi.
Aano mazuba bulimi bwadula kuti naa toowula camutunzya ambuto yacikuwa.
Kutebula kuyooba kwamujanza. Kaindi kwaanyina misamu yansaku yalo yamana kujaya nyika.
Kaindi kwakali kuligwa myuungu, minsale, banamwino azyimwi zyisyango. 
Mazubaa sunu eezyi tazyicijanwi nkaambo azyalo zyabalwa kuti ninsaku kumisamu eeyo.
Mapenzi aamwi ngakuti imvwula taicitangi mbwiiyelede. 
Sunu aano mazuba itanga mumwezi wa Nalupale kakuli kaindi 
ngomwezi ngotwakali kupalila-palila zyisyango zyesu. 
Kusambala zyisyango kwakali kwabukkide. 
Twakajisi mabboodi akali kusambala zyisyango. 
Masimpe nocali kukonzeka, motwajokela buyo kumazubaa kaindi. 
Mbwaakagola munene kwaamba.
Mubuzyo Mabala ako ataindilili kumwaanda 
Cibalo cako citalike boobu:
Bubotu bwalulimi bwakaindi Kumvwisisisya kubala
Bala cibalo citobela kawilwi wamana wiingule mibuzyo litobela.
"Yawe musa! Babambe bana bako baya bobile mbookazyala musyokwe; 
Baya kukuvwuna muciindi ncotazyi." 
Mbwaakaamba oobu Ntaulu kuli Buumba nobakamana kubamba makani aamwanaa mupati wabo, 
Hamoonga, ngwaakazyede kuli Munalula - musimbi wacilozi.
Makai akacitika kuti Ntaulu wakazyede bana bobile, 
musimbi amusankwa kumwanaa bacindu, Mukampongo. 
Mukaintu wakwe Nchimunya ciindi eeci wakaunkide kumusyika kwalo nkwaakali kuya kuula kayanga. 
Buumba a Ntaulu nobakabona kuti bina Banji bapiluka kale, 
bakaunka alaale kuti bakaliibe kwaambaula.
Ntaulu wakazumanana kaambo nkaakatalikide. 
"Mukwabo , aaba bana mbotwakazyala kunze balavwuna". 
"Ino ncinzi cini ncoamba?" Wakabuzya Buumba. 
Musa mebo mwana nguwakandivwuna. 
Awono aano nindali mucuumbwe.
"Nindakasika ananda bumwi buzuba, ndakajana mukaintu wangu wajika kale cisusulo. 
Akaambo kakuti yakali kundifwusa mabwe, ndakanjila
munanda mbuli kuti ndakali kutonkwaa kambizyi. 
Ndakazyoobona kana kangu kasimbi nkokafwambaana 
kunjila akalo akuti "Bataata, mutalyi cakulya cili momuya mumitiba. 
Babaama babikka musamu uulya ngomwakali kusansaila magukusi. 
Ndali kulangilila nobabikka. Kabbodela bakabikka mukkabati nobamana kubikka mucisyu.
"Chimuka, ino wali kutyani noobabona yebo?" 
"Ndali kuyanda kubweza bbuku la nambala kiti nkaakulembe mulimo ngotwapegwa
kucikolo nindababona pesi balo tiibandibona pe."
Mukwabo mwana naakamana kundaambila boobu, ndakabweza mutiba wacisyu
akugusya cituli cankuku akufwusila kabwa kasyoonto kalo kakali munsi-munsi aakatebule. 
Mukaindi kasyoonto, kabwa kakazwa anzé akutalika kuzeenteka
mpoona kakaakuwa amalyatilo aakunjilila munanda akufwa mpoona.
Nindakacibona kacicitika eeci, ndakasyoma ncaakandaambila mwanaangu ooyu.
Akaambo kakuti kunyina uumbi wakacibona caacitika, ndakabweza cilyatilo luba. 
Masusu akandiima.Ndakalindila mukaintu kuti apiluke ooo nkwaakaunkide. 
Ndakali kuboneka mbuli kuti nkakuku kaugwa nkaambo ndakazyiba 
kuti dime ndakali kunga ndivwungaidwe ngubo.
Naakaboola mukaintu wang, ndakmwiitila munanda akumwaambila 
kuti ndakali kulindila nguwe kuti tulye limwi. 
Mukaintu wakakaka akuti walo ulikkutide nkaambo walilide kale naatakana unka nkwaakabede. 
Ndakamusinikizya kuti tulye pele naakabona kuti ndasinizya, 
wakasamba akusuna mukusu akuubuya buyo katasunsi mucisyu.
Nindaaboona boobu, ndakamwaambila kuti nkokuti nkalide buyo kuzyuli. 
Aawo ndakabweza mutiba mwakali nyama yankuku walo, 
ndakati kobweza mutiba wansima akuti kobwezelezya amenda akunywa. 
Naakanjila muzyuli, mebo ndakazwa akumukkila mukati. 
Mpoona ndakatuma mujwa wangu kuti akaite basazinyinaa mukaintu wang kuti baboole cakufwambana. 
Mukubaa coolwe, boonse bakaakujanika akuboola nkaambo bakayoowa njitilo mbuyakabede.
Nobakakkala boons munanda yakukkalila, ndakaunka kuzyuli akuyakumujulila
kwakali beenzu munanda nkabela wakajana basazinyina boonse mbaaba
abamukowa wangu botatwe balikkede. Ndakabayiila cano coonse mbocakabede
akuleta kabwa nkindakasiside mumaluba-luba kutegwa nditondezye bumboni,
Ndimane ndakabuzya mukaintu naa kuli cibi ncidakacita ncaakali kuyanda kundijaila. 
Ndakababuzya abalo basazinyina kuti ndiza kuli ncindakacita calo ncobazyi balo. 
Boonse bakaumuna wii! Kwakabula awiingula. Bakagambwa kapati.
Mukwabo, "Mabiya mbwaafwida kumubumbi, ndakati amurutoleezye muntu
weenu buyo-buyo inga nkeya kukalenga kapapa kanondo." 
Mboyakamana nanda abina Cheelo, ncindakakwata bina Mpimpa aba ibali kumusyika.
Ono mbookali kumakuwa kukwiiya, ndati nkuzyibye mukwesu. 
Bana bakuzyala musyokwe katubabamba nkaambo inga bakuvwuna. 
Balo bazyi nduwe buyo owisyi, kakuli baio bamunanda bavwula kusyoma nyina walo.
Buumba akamunyandya makani aaya pele wakaiya ciiyo.
Lino Koyingula mibuzyo itobela
Sala bwiinguzi bwelede kuzwa kuli bone bwapegwa kumubuzyo amubuzyo.
Ntaulu wakazyede bana bongaye?
Cintu cipati cakapa kuti Ntaulu balekane abakaintu
nkutacizyiba kujika mukaintu. nkuyanda kujaya mulumi.
mwana wakabejela bawisi. nkutamuyanda mukaintu,
Ba muka Ntaulu bakainkide kumusyika kuya
Bantu boonse bakaitwa bakaumuna wil. Eeci caamba kuti.
Wakakaka cakukakila limwi. Wakati, "Tandili ndime pe. 
Ngumwi wakakanana makani aankwela kuli Mutinta.
Akaambo kakuti boonse bakalibuzyi buumi bubotu bwa Mutinta, 
bakazyiba kuti Nchimunya ukaka buyo. 
Eelyo bayi bapati bakalaya Nchimunya kumbele aabazyali.
Bakati, "Nchimunya ulasunda. Kuti koyanda kuya kukkala buumi buyumu, 
kocita intu come aciindi comwe. Ecino ciindi kozumanana alwilyo Iwako. 
Watakucita ooku, uyakujana mapenzi." Kuli Mutinta bayi bapati bakati,
"Uli musimbi mubotu nikaambo ulibuzyi bubi bwamuzeezo wa Nchimunya. 
Basimbi bamwi balacengwa abasankwa, bamana bajana mapenzi mubuumi bwabo. 
Utakasoli kusunda, kucita cakanana Nchimunya," bakamunyemena mwanaabo.

Sena Iyakatanta, bazyali ba Mutinta bakazyiba kuti Ncimunya wakanana makani aankwela kuli Mutinta.

Bazyali ba Nchimunya bakamubuzya mwanaabo naa cakali masimpe kuti wakanana makai aankwela kuli Mutinta.

Bamane bazyali ba Mutinta bakazyibya bayi kapati ba Chinyama kucikolo makai aankwela aakakanana Nchimunya kuli Mutinta.

Bala cibalo citobela kaumuumu.
Mucisi ca Bbekumbe kwakali mwami wakazyede mwana musimbi mubotu. 
Mwari ooyu wakali kuyanda kuti mwanaakwe akakwatwe kumuntu sicamba alimwi wabulemu.
Mukuyanda kuzyiba muntu ooyu, mwami wakayanda kuti muntu ooyo weelede kusunkwa munzila zyaandeene. 
Aboobo wakaleta ngoma zyobile akuzyaanzika mumusamu
kutanta musamu coy akuyoowuma ngoma zyiya kukunyina kuwa. 
Mbanji bakasoleka pele boonse cakaala.

mucisi ca Bbekumbe tiwakali tivami wakazyede musimbi mubotu.

bakamwaambila ncakeelede kucita, kuti wakeelede kutanta musamu

akunma ngoma.

Taakasowa cindi pe wakaangungumwina oonse mbwaakajulilwa biyo acikko kalangililamwami.
Mwami waka mulumbaizya musankwa ooyu elyo wakamwaambila musunko wamamanino.

Kunyina naakayisamide kale ninga eeyi. Buce biyo wakayisama kukuboko kwalulyo.

waawo nkusanduka waba mukuba. Mwami wakalibonena eeci.

Mwami mukukkomana wakamupa lumwi lubazu iwakukkala.

MALWEZA  AATUNGA MULONGO
Kwakali kululelema mumwezi wa Kavwumbi kaniini.
Cakali ciindi cakumazuba, izuba nolyakasosoloka acilanga nkumo
Kalilondelela waalya mpolibonenwa ngulube.
Imvwula yakasibika cinyenaazya kulubazu Iwakunyika, 
cakunga kuti koli musyokwe, ticakali kwiindulukwa kulanga,
Nkaambo inga kayile kuloka yacizike; nkwiile kuti 'matako mpe lubilo'.
Kwakali kwiile kubee makumbi ayanda kukolomoka avwumbe nyika yoonse. 
Nokuba kuti zuba lyakacili mujulu, ansi kwakali kusiya mbuli kulubundubundu aalya aanjilila kakuku keenzu.
Kaluso kamulombwana kakadukumenye kulanga-langa mapepa muopesi lyako, 
tilkakacibwene cakali kucitika nkaambo maano oonse kakaabikkide kumulimo ngokakali kucita. 
Luwo lutontola lujisi akanunkilizi kabulongo, Inga kuya kusondela anze, wajana kujulu kwasyibingana. 
Eci cakamunyandya, nkaambo tanaakali kuyeeya kuti mumwezi wa Kavwumbi 
kaniini nkouli kumatalikilo inga kwaboola yasyikataka mbuli yakaimikide anze.
Wakafwambaana kujala mpulungwido akukwela tusani tuvwumbilila kutegwa naa yalaba kataibwene.
Mucibuye munjililwa kotana sika muopesi yakalombwana aaka, kwakali nakalindu waasamide dimpwilimpwi lituba akasot katuba.
Kuti mwazyi kwile kuumana nkumo mumusinze inga ulaile kulijaya kutija koti ndabona mukuwansi.
Aaka kaluso kamulombwana kakali nkaanga haabupampu mukusilika amicelo yacikuwa, 
Tee mbambabo baya mazuba aano bategwa 'Makuwa aakacaala'. 
Tanaakali kuyanda kubeleka muzibbadela zyamfwulumende kwategwa mali maniini. 
Mweena oomu mung' anda mwaakakkede cakali ncecibbadela mwaakali kusilikila. 
Aboobo uuyanda kusilikwa, nkubbadela mali. Ooyu musimbi waakkede mucibuye,
neuwaali kumugwasya kusilika. Newaakali kutuma kupa bantu misamu.
Ucikwela biyo cuuno kuti akkale naakamana kuwumba tusani mumpulungwido wakamvwa fwooni yalila,wakalikokola naya avwiile.
Ndijisi mulwazi uujisi bulwazi bukatazizye, aboobo uyanda kumubona ati ndiza inga mulamugwasya.
Wakali musimbi wakali kumugwasya kubeleka wakali kukanana.
Mulwazi ulaa bulwazi bukatazizye! wakavwiila cakunyandwa musilisi kumwi kaseka-seka, 
amane wakalanga ciindi akuboko, tulombyjana twaacileka kulanga mujulu.
Wakajana nkocili cakubona mulwazi omwe biyo. 'Kaboola ndimubone.
Amane wakalibamba biyo kukkala kulindila.Kakatana ba kaindi wakamvwa mulangu waamulyango walila. 
Katana vwiila, wakanjila musimbi mukubusi wakalaa ciimo cibotu. 
Musilisi wakaseka-seka kutondezya bulongwe, amane wakati, 'Vweyi! Mwalibizya kamwale.
Nceeco cuuno amukkale.' Wakatondeka cuuno cakali munsi-munsi atebule lyakwe.
"'Ndalibizya,' wakavwiila musimbi kumwi kakkala acuuno.Musilisi wakabona kuti musimbi ooyu tanaakali kuyanda kuti meso kabaswaana.
"Mwatweenda kumazuba nobacembele; ncinzi kayi cakatazya? Tee mpaawa muboneka biyo kabotu?' 
Wakaamba musilisi cakusobana. Musimbi wakaile biyo kumweta-mweta kumwi ameso kalibonya kuti kuli kapati kakali kumuziya.
Anze yakatalika kupwatamuna kuwa kayijisi amuwo munji. 'Ndili mulwazi,' wakatalika kukanana musimbi cakufwenyafwenya mbuli 
kuti kuli mbatayandi kuti bamvwe, alimwi kaluwide kutegwa meso ataswaani aamusilisi.
"Bulwazi bwangu nduwe musilisi ngondibikkide lusyomo kuti inga wabusilika olikke.' 
Cindi eeci ijwi lyakali kuzyangama. 'Ino mbulwazi nzi obo butaambwi? Langa cindi camana kopasaula kukanana,'
wakaamba musilisi kumwi kamwetamweta. "Kuti hekonzya kukugwasya ndakugwasya.'
'Ndilaa mbwebede,' wakatalika kukanana musimbi.
'Aboobo eeci nceyumude tandiciyandi amocinda.' Wakaintamuka, walanga kumusilisi alimwi wasintama mbuli kuti ukanana kumakwe.
'Vweyi! cabija kapati,' wakavwiila musilisi. 'Ino tumvwe kakunyina akudantaika kukanana; ncinzi cipati ncotaciyandili eco ncoyumwide?' 
Musilisi ooyu izyina lyakwe wakali Haatimba. Ooyu musilisi mulimo wakwe wakaluuzyi kutacengeezya.
Aboobo wakalizyi kuti balwazi bal mbuli yooyu wakamuswaya tababindilwi alimwi tabavwulumukilwi. 
Nkumuteteetela nkubomba kutegwa ulye malelo. Nkumupa cindi kutegwa aambe zyoonse zili kumoyo. 
Kuti wamwiinganina, inga zimwi zyafwidilila, zyaunka mucikuka. Kayi muntu ulaa mbwabede lyoonse ulakatazya. 
Nokuba kuti ooyu musimbi wakatola cindi kuti avwiile, musilisi avwiile,
wakamulindila kuti aambe. Boonse bakakkala kabaumwine mbuli kuti basikilwa aatakondi. 
Limwi musimbi wakazyiba kuti kuumuna taku ncicaali kunga cilamugwasya. 
Caaceede nkwaamba biyo toonse atwaali kucisya ncence. Ino kayi atyeni kayi uyanda kugwasyigwa. 
Muntu waakkede kumpela lyakwe ngomuntu alikke ngwaakali kusyoma kuti naa wamwaambila penzi lyakwe, 
ulakonzya kulimvwa aboobo inga wamugwasya.
'Ndazimininwa cakucita,' mbwakatalika kukanana musimbi, maano andimana, musankwa undisinkilide ulaboola
mwezi uuboola kuzyila ku Amelika nkwaakaunka kukwiiya.
Musankwa ooyu ndakamulindila kwamusanu wamyaka kuti amanizye Iwiiyo Iwakwe. 
Muntu ngundakali kusyoma ciindi coonse alimwi ndicimusyoma. Awalo kwiinda mumagwalo aatakali kumana waalijisi lusyomo mulindime. Kumane kwaile kuboola mucele wanditukka mukuli uulaa malweza. Naakamana kwaamba boobo wakaintamuka. 
Kumeso yakali kwiile kukulumbuka yacizike. Limwi wakapozomoka biya.
Musilisi' wakakkede biyo kaumwine kalindila kuti amanizye kwaamba zyoonse zyakali kumoyo nzyaakali kukonzya.

bakali kuciswa cilwazi eeci bakali kusika kwakwe kuyanda kugwasyigwa. Buzuba oobu mbubwena musimbi oyu wakali wasanu, 
aboobo boonse bakali kwiisinda mbubona bwakali kwiisinda musimbi oyu.
Niwakamukkala moyo, wakaleka kulila, wakasinda minsyonzyi kumeso akatambala nkaakafwumuna mubbeeke ndyaakajisi.

kayi bazyali bangu bakatala tabakonzyi kubamba mwanaa muntu kakuli andenyina baali kupenga nindaali mpwitamamina. 
Baakatala sunu, walampisya musinzo nkubaazyila, kuyigwa kwafwiimpa. 
Zyoonse ezvi kuti ndazyi kuzivwoomeka, inga ndamvwâ mutwe uyanda kundilekelezya.

Wakatalika alimwi kulila, amane wakazumanana akuti
"Ndizyi kuti eeci cilanyandya alimwi cilakatazya kusyoma.
Simizyeesu ooyu muntu ngundali kuyanda kuzwa bunini bwangu, 
alimwi Lwando simizyeesu nguwena ooyu awalo wali kundiyanda lyoonse. 
Nkaambo kaluyando ndulwena oolu, cakandipa kuti ndizwe kwesu, kuya kukkala anguwe.
Ndakatalikila kwakwe cikolo kusika limwi ndamanizya. Wali kunduulila zyoonse zyaali kuyandika kucikolo.
Mpaawo inga baali kumugwasya biya bazyali bangu. 
Kuti kabaumwine, taku naakali kutongooka waali kundicitila zyoonse.
Nindakamanizya cikolo ku Chivuna, wakandibbadelela kuti ndikazumanane mulwijyo lwangu ku Evelyn Hone.
Coonse eeci cindi ndakali kukkala anguwe amukwasyi wakwe woonse ku Woodlands muno mu Lusaka. 
Nindakatalika kubeleka, ndakaba aakaanda kangu ku Olympia Park.
Pele nokuba kuti ndakali aang'anda yangu ticakandilesya kuunka kubona acisya,
awalo tanaakali kuyuminina kung Panda yangu. Ooyu acisya Lwando nkakeela da lyomwe abamaama.

alimwi bakali bankutwe kumilimo. Alimwi abalo bana basimbi bakali kuzyila mumaanda maniini bakakwetwe kale,
nguwakabayandauda balumi. Abalo maanda aabo akali kusuka busi.

Oyu musankwa wakali mubwene kuti wakali lomene alimwi wakalijisi mulemyo.

kuti bakakwatane. Nibakamana kuzuminana boobo, makani bakaatola kubazyali babo aumwi.

makani aaya nkaambo wakazyi mbuli moyo wamusankwa wakali kuyanda kukwata mwanaakwe mbuwakabede.

Mwakali mumwaka wa 1966, Caalama naakamanizya bbuku lya Grade 7. Cindi eeco, 
Lwando wakali kunga azyikumulanga muntu wakwe, walimvwa bubi. Wali kusola
kulijata-jata pesi caali kumwaalila. Kubota biya boona limwi amuntu wakwe. 
Wakali kunga talimvwi kabotu kuti Caalama
Kali kuli bausy. Wakali kuboola lyoonse kung'onzi. 
Eeci cindi tanaa kaninga kwata. Kwakali kasankwa nkaakauma
naakajana balamyontana milaka balaa Caalama mukkoce lyang'anda yakwe bumwi busiku.
"Kumane nkokuboola cindi naakali kweezyanyika. bakaintu bakwe kuli Caalama. 
Kwaboola koongelezegwa kwa Caalama kuti balendeleiwa kwabula ubajikila, 
kakubee uyanda kuti aboole munsi lyakwe. Lwando waamutanda biya
mukaintu akaambo kamoyo ngwaakamvwide wali kubbubba kuyanda kuti awone aamuntu wakwe. 
Kuti kakanana munsi-munsi aamuntu wakwe, wali kunga mpaawo wafwundilila koonse akwaambaula. 
Zimwi zindi inga waali kubee tamvwide limwi mujwa nkuya kutilimuna biya naya kubuzya
alimwi kuti ino wali kwaamba nzi. Coonse eeci walo Caalama tanaakali kucibona kuti acisyanyina wali kumumenena.
Kumane kwaboola kusekelela kwakuzyalwa kwa Lwando. Eeci cakali nceciindi cibotu cakumukozya bukoko Caalama.
Lwando wakaula makoko aandeene. Wamukombelezya kunywa bwakali kulweela-lweela. 
Naakanywa, wakakkomana kapati, wakalizyi kuti sunu ulacijana camupenzenzye mazuba oonse.
Haamwaandwe wakaityokezya mizeezo yokwa Lwando naakati, 
'Ndiyanda kubona masimpe kuti ndacityokezya Wakakuna bukoko Aakati zyuba bala;
tacisekeki nkwaambile Lwando mwana. Coonse cindi eeci ndakali kwiile kulicenga,' waazumanana kukanana. 
'Ndakali kumuyanda ulya musimbi kwinda mabala mbwaamba,
Ndakaunka ku Amelika, ooko kwalo nkundakaakujana basimbi. 
Kuli basimbi ooku kacende kwakunga walanga biya kuti Leza kulenga ulicizyi. 
Nindakasobana kapati ku Amelika nikwatakali mujwa wako. 
Luyando ndundakajisi kuli nguwe, Iwakali lumbilumbi biya cakunga lyoonse ndakali kweenda acifwanikiso cakwe munkomwi.
Coonse cindi kuti ndasunkwa koona aamusimbi waku Amelika, ndakali
kulimvwa mbuli kuti Caalama ulindibwene cibi ncendicita, aboobo ndakali kuleka. 
Coonse cakali kundipa kuleka twamusyobo ndundakajisi ali Caalama. 
Wacibona on ncindakali okuno? Ncinzi ono cicili cibotu kuponena atala aanyika? Taata biya ziyume zitete.
MudaalaLwaanzilwanyikatanaakabuyandamwanaakwe Haatimba mbwaakali kulunduka mukukwata kwakwe.
Haatimba tanaakaninga salazigwa. Ono ngoôyu mudolopo wabwezela musimbi. 
Eeci ciya kuleta kukanana kupati, Tanaakakkomana mudaala naaba anjini.
Mbwaakamana kulubala lugwalo Iwakazyila kuli Haatimba, mudaala wakatanta bbaasi lyakali kufwuma kwiinda.
Mubbasi wakajana mung' anga wabang' anganyina, Haanyendo, ooyo walo wakamwaambila twaambo
Tumwi twatakamukkazika kabotu, tujatikizya mukwasyi ookwabo mukaintu ngwaakali kuyanda kukwata Haatimba.
Ono mbwaakasikila wakabona cimbi cintu cakaindilila kumunyonganya. 
Wakacibona mukaintu mbwaakaboolela kumwaanzya.
'"Eeli da ndyamyezi yongaye mukaintu wako Haatimba?' '"Uuno ngwatatu. Ino mwazyiba buti kuti ulimitide?'
'Cilalibonya,' bakavwiila bausyi, 'nokuba kuti inga nd'ati ulaa mubili mubotu. 
Kuli meso biya aakonzya kumubona. Mudaala wakaumuna kwakaindi kaniini amane wakabuzya;
"'Hena eeci ncicakapa kuti ufwambaane obuya kukwata?' "Inzya ncecico.
"Wandaambila kuti bausyi bakamukasya kuti mucite mucato. Sena masimpe?*
'Eeco nciindi cabausyi,' wakavwiila Haatimba. Mebo tandikombi naa twacita mucato naa tatuciti.
Ambeyo nciindi cangu cakuti ndizyibe Haatimba, Bazyali bamusimbi baakuba aambobayeeya, 
baya kuboola kuli dime kutali nduwe.' 'Inga mwabatumina kuli ndime, " wakavwiila Haatimba. 
Tindazyi kuti mboyeeya obo, wakaamba mudaala ijwi kalili ansi. 
'Nokuba kuti pesi kuli nzindakatimywe bantu kabaambaamba.'
Haatimba wakali kokola amane walibamba biya kukkala, Aa zinzi zyimwakamywa tumywe?'
Ndakamvwa kuti bausyi mukaintu wako bakanyema kapati 
mwanaabo mbwaakalilemeka kakaambo kakukwatana kwanu. Wakaamba majwi aamwi mbuli 
aakuti musimbi wako oyu kuli musankwangwaakaleka ngubakamusalide bausyi. 
Alimwi tumwi twaambo ntwakuti bausyi bakamutakata akumusinganya. 
Sena kuli ncozyi aceeci?' 'Mebo kwiina ancindakamvwa,
wakaywiila Haatimba kumwi kayeeme kumupando. 'Kuli yooyo musankwa wakali
kuyanda kumukwata inga ndati ndausa. Musimbi wakayanda ncaakayanda.

Autegwa batalike kweeba, wakakwatwa kumusilisi Haatimba.
Eci cakandinyandya akusyoma cakasoka kundaalila. Cakali mbuli ciloto kuli ndime. 
Cakandicima kapati nkaambo musanu wamyaka poonse eyi njindakali ku Amelia, laku
nindakoona amusimbi umbi, nkaambo kaluyando naundakajisi kuli Caalama. Inga mwayeeya bio mbundakalimywa
anyasebo nobabetesi. Kumane, Lwando, oyo walo uulingusimizyaabo ca Caalama wakaboola kuli dime. 
Wakandibona buyanga. Wakandikombelezya kuti ndibbadele kuniini, kumuntu ngutwakaambila kuti ajaye Caalama.
Ndalomba kulekelelwa kujulu aansi tiindakazyi. Taku nindakazyiba kusika cindi ncicatakali kugwasyika. 
Kwiinda mukutazyiba kwangu, ndakaile kuunkila mukasuko kakambizyi. Mulandu wakujaya Lwando, 
ndazumina nkaambo wakandimisizya musimbi wangu Caalama, amane wamupanganina kumujaya kusisikizya cibi ncaakacita. 
Alimwi ndajava a Dakuungila, uutegwa Mutelampondo, mujayi uuluulwa nkaaambo nguwanyonyaula Caalama
lulijisi twaambo tweelede, ntomunga mwabelesya kujana masimpe.
Ndime wanu sikwaazwa, Haamwaandwe mbwaakamanina biyo kulemba, wakamvwa ükonkomona acijazyo. 
Wakavwiila akumwitila mukati, kumwi kapenuna bbuku lyaavwumbide katobolo akasando.
Mutelampondo wakanjila akujala cijazyo naakamanina kunjila. Haamwaandwe wakabona mbuli 
kuti wakaba bumbi kuzwa cindi ncaakamubwene Mutelampondo.
Wakali samide kabotu-kabotu jekete likonzyanya abuluke.
Wakasamide acibaki cituba, atayi uusiya munsingo.
Kumaulu, wakali samide mabbusu aasiya aakali kutaimataima, a masookesi aasubila. 
Kuti oolanga inga wati ndajana aali bantu ncobeni, ani ncigwebenga.
Wabonwa Mutelampondo, nceeco. cuuno kkala cilombwana,' 
wakaanzya Haamwaandwe kumwi kabajatana mumanza. "
Ndabonwa,' wakavwiila Mutelampondo kumwi kakkala acuuno cakali kumpela aatebule lyokwa Haamwaandwe.
Wakauonda mulimo wako kabotu-kabotu, kalombwana. wakaamba Haamwaandwe.
"Tindakazyi kuti uliisi basankwa bajisi busongo bunji bakonzya kulicengeezya kuti
mbasilisi babanyama baamunzi "Twakaile kuzyibila biya sunu, kayi mpotulida. 
Cakaile kuba ceenzya mubili,' wakaamba Mutelampondo cakutwanga amulimo ngwacita. 
Lyoonse notucita mulimo wesu, kuli zintu zyobilo nzyotubona 
Kuti zyabelekwa. Cakusaanguna mulimo oyo uuyandika kucitwa, cabili tweelede kubona kuti
bamapulisa tabatuyeeyeli naaba aniini. Zyoonse ezyi zyobilo tulazicita kabota-kabotu.
Inzya yawe mulimo wako uluuzyi,' wakaamba Haamwaandwe kumwi kaseka-seka.
"Aboobo nkaambo kamulimo ngookoonda, ndilakupa cipego nconakundiyeeya kusika
limwi Haatwakwe akahoole ansi ano. Cipego cako nceeci.'
Haamwaandwe wakabweza katobolo akudubula Mutelampondo anselelo aakkombo. 
Wakabweza kasando kakwe akuunka aakalede mubili ookwa Mutelampondo wakaloka mbuli ciyuni caumw a malekani kuzwa acuuno. 
Wakamulyata amutwe. Mutelampondo wakajalula meso. Haamwaandwe wakaseka-seka amane cakufwubaazya wakati:
"Kwaamba kalombwana alimvwide buti? Tee kayi inkulu yantobolo ilanoneezya? 
Ooku nkuvwulizya biyo majwi aakaamba Mwami Jesu kuli umwi sikwilya wakwe naakati,
"Uufwumuna panga lyakwe akujaya umwi, awalo uya kufwa panga." 
Aboobo ncencico eci nocovwola, mumilimo njooli kucita yoonse. 
Muzimo wako ukasangane amizimo yakatandwa kubusyu bwa Leza. 
Katuya ndilakweenzya kukamvwu kasubila, Lwando ulalindila!"
Haamwaandwe wakainyuka akumuumputa kansondo mumutwe canguzu. 
Kakanjila mbuli kuti wauma atala aacitende cakabola. 
amane, wakabbatika lugwalo ndwaakali kulemba acamba cokwa Mutelampondo.
Anze, kwakali kulimvwisya kulila kwamyootokala yakali kusika mulubuwa. 
Haamwaandwe kumwi kavwungide mulomo wakaunka ampulungwido akusondela anze.
Myootokala yobilo yabamapulisa yakaliimvwi anze.
Bamapulisa bakazwa akuzinguluka ng'anda kumwi kabajisi antobolo mbuli 
kuti bamvwa kuti kwanjila bakalukuza mung'anda. 
Umwi wabo wakaima amulyango. Haamwaandwe wakayeeya kuti atabakatazyi kapati. 
Wakaunka acuuno cakwe wakkala. Wakanyamuna katobolo akoonzolola mbuli mbwakonzya,
Kamuboola munditole ono ndalibambila!' Kaseka-seka, wakaaka mululi wantobolo mukanwa akulebula.
Tee ncicaalila muyuni lukumba wakati,"Avwuuka ansi taalebelelwa?'
Mudolopo lya Nairobi, kulamfu aminzi kwakali kabunga kabana basankwa balo ibatakajisi nkobazulilwa.  . 																									
Bakapona buumi bwabo mbubona mbuli mazuba mbwaakali kutobelana.																									
Bumwi buzuba mafumofumo bakalongela miseme yabo nibakazwa kubuka mumigelo yamuloodi aawo aakali mpeyo kapati.																									
Bakalikunga bayasya makwiisyilili kutegwa batande mpeyo																									
Akati kabasankwa aaba kwakali kujanika umwi ooyo wiitwa kuti Magozwe.																									
Ooyu nguwakali mwana alimbabo boonse.																									
Iciindi bazyali ba Magozwe nibakafwa wakali biyo amyaka yosanwe. Aboobo wakaunka kuyakukkala abaacisyanyina ibakali kumutundulula. Kunyina nibakamubikkila maanu Magozwe.    Acibe cakulya nyaanya, kwiina nibakali kumupa pesi kakuli bakalikumubelesya ncito zilema mbuli mbubakalikuyanda.																									
Mateyo 19:14 Jesu wakati, “amubaleke bana bashoonto baboole kulindime, mutabakashi pe, nkaambo Ubwami Bwakujulu mbubwabo baliboobu.”																									
Bbaibbele lya banalilajanika akucita kuti Jesu azibwe kubana kwiinda mukupa twaano tusandulwide mubbaibbele azikozyanyo ziyandika zyandeene akubantu,																									
antomwe azisi zyoonse a webu, foni yakumanza/PDA\’s,tubbuku tupentedwe amabbuku, mumishobo yoonse mwana ngwakonzya kwambaula.																									
Magozwe kunyina naakalikuzumizigwa kuti ape butongoosi nokuba kubuzya mubuzyo uuli woonse. Kwalikunga kuti naa wabuzya, baacisyanyina nkumuuma. Wakalikunga ababuzya kujatikizya makani akuya kucikolo bamwaambila kuti, “buyanga bwakaindilila mulinduwe tokozi kwiiya.”    Nikwakainda myaka yotatwe yakulelwa mukupenga, Magozwe wakatija, wakazwa ang’anda alibaacisyanyina akutalika kukkala mumazila.																									
"Ootu twaano mubbaibbele twelede kupegwa anyika yonse kubana bali 1.8 mabilyoni nakacikozyeka.

"																									
Leza mbwaakalenga zintu zyoonse																									
Kumatalikilo Leza wakalenga ijulu anyika. Lino nyika yakalipilingene akubula zintu,																									
Buumi bwakukkala mumazila bwakalikukatazya. Bana basankwa banji-banji cakaliciyumu-yumu kujana cakulya. Nkaambo kakuzoompola zintu zyabantu kumaanza kutegwa ujane cakulya bamwi bakali kwaangwa mpoonya bamwi bakalikuumwa. Iciindi umwi naajanika muciimo cakuciswa, kujana cakulya nokuba muntu wakugwasililizya cakali cintu nciyumu. Mali ngubakali kuyaa kulombelela alimwi akuulisya tupulasitiki ngongayo ngubakali kulisiminina kuti kabaligwasya.																									
nkabela kauli mudima atala lyamaanzi malamfu. Alakwe Muuya wa-Leza wakali kukumba-kumba atala lyamaanzi.																									
Lino Leza wakaamba kuti, Akube mumuni. Mpoonya awo mumuni wakaba.																									
Nkabela Leza wakabona mumuni kuti mubotu, alimwi Leza wakaanzaanya mumuni amudima.																									
Lino mumuni Leza wakauulika kuti ndisikati, awalo mudima wakauulika kuti masiku.																									
Bumwi buzuba Magozwe naakali kumvunyungula mumadooti, muzingungulu, wakabona kabbuku kamanide-manide. Wakakabweza akukabikka musaka lyakwe. Abuzuba wakalikunga ulakabweza akulanga-langa zifwanikiso mbokuli taakacizyi akubala noliba bbala lyomwe.																									
Aboobo kwakaba igoko, alimwi kwakaba cifumo, buzuba bomwe.																									
Lino Leza wakaamba kuti, Akube mulengalenga akatikati kamaanzi, uanzaanye maanzi amaanzinyina.																									
Eezi zifwanikiso zyakalikutondezya caano camwana musankwa wakaba simweenzya ndeke. Magozwe wakakozya kuliyeeyela kuba simweezya ndeke. Zimwi ziindi wakalikulimvwa kuti ngonguwe ngobakanana mukati mubbuku.																									
Elyo Leza wakacita mulengalenga oyo, waanzaanya maanzi aali ansi lyamulengalenga amaanzi aali kujulu lyamulengalenga. 																									
Mbuboobo mbukwakaba. Lino oyo mulengalenga Leza wakauulika kuti ndijulu.																									
Bumwi buzuba Kwakali kutontola nkabela Magozwe wakaimikila munzila kalombelela. Eelyo umwi mudaala wakaswena munsi lyakwe. “Kwaamba, mebo ndime Tomaasi. Ndibeleka biyo munsi-munsi awaano kwalo oko nkokozya kujana cakuti inga walya,” wakakanana mudaala kumwi katondeka kung’anda yamusyobo wa mungunga waji iijisi alimwi aciluli cacikambwe. “Ndasyoma inga waunka okuya ukabweze cakulya.” Magozwe wakamulamga mudaalo ooyu, wailanga ng’anda. “Ndiza,” wakamvwiila Magozwe kumwi keenda akweenda akuzwa wazwa ngooyo waunka.																									
Aboobo kwakaba igoko alimwi kwakaba cifumo, buzuba bwabili.																									
Lino Leza wakaamba kuti, Maanzi oonse aali ansi lyajulu ayoboloke antoomwe,																									
kuti intundubwi iboneke, Nkabela kwakaba obo.																									
Lino intundubwi Leza wakaiulika kuti ninyika, aalo maanzi mpaakayobolokela wakaaulika kuti ndwizi.																									
Nkabela Leza wakabona kuti ncintu cibotu. 11Lino Leza wakaamba kuti, nyika isyusye mweemvwe,																									
azisyu zizyala imbuto, amisamu iizyala micelo, umwi aumwi mbuli musyobo wawo,																									
Mbuli myezi mbuli mbuyakali kuya akwiinda kaitobelena, banabasankwa aaba limwi bakaya kkoyabazyibilina alimwi aba Tomaasi. Tomaasi wakalimuntu uyandisisya kwaambaula abantu, kapati aabo batakajisi kwakukkala kunze biyo amumazila. Tomaasii muntu wakateelela bube bwabuumi bwabantu bakkala mumaanda alimwi amumazila.																									
iijisi imbuto mukati, atala anyika, Nkabela kwakaba obo.																									
Nyika yakasyusya mweemvwe, azisyu zizyala imbuto cimwi acimwi mbuli musyobo waco,																									
Magozwe wakali kkede mumbembelekwa a loodi kalanga cifwanikiso mukabbuku kakwe ciindi eeco Tomaasi naakasika akukkala munsi lyakwe. “Mbuti? Ino kaambanzi kabbuku aaka?” wakabuzya Tomaasii. “Cibalo caamba umwi musankwa weenzya ndeke, “ wakamvwiila Magozwe. “Nguni zina musankwa oyo?” wakabuzya Tomaasii. “Chita, tandicizi kubala,” wakamvwiila Magozwe.																									
amisamu iizyala micelo iijisi imbuto mukati, umwi aumwi mbuli musyobo wawo.																									
Nkabela Leza wakabona kuti ncintu cibotu. Aboobo kwakaba igoko, alimwi kwakaba cifumo, buzuba bwatatu.																									
Lino Leza wakamba kuti, Akube mimuni mumwenya wakujulu, kuti ianzaanye isikati amasiku,																									
alimwi ibe zitondezyo akubamba ziindi zyeelede zyamazuba azyamyaka.																									
Nibakaswangaana, Magozwe wakamwaambila Tomaasii caano cabuumi bwake. Wakamwaambila mbuli mbwaakatija kuzwa kuli baacisyanyina. Tomaasii kunyina zinji zyaakaumbaula alimwi kunyina ncaakatodeya Magozwe kuti acite pele wakamupa kuteelela kweelede. Zimwi ziindi bakakanana kabalya cakulya mung’nda yamasenke acikambwe.																									
Ibe malampi mumwenya wakujulu aakumunisya ansi. Nkabela kwakaba obo.																									
Leza wakacita mimuni yobile mipati, mumuni mupati wakweendelezya isikati amumuni muniini wakweendelezya masiku;																									
azyalo inyenyeezi wakazicita. Nkabela Leza wakazibika mumweenya wakujulu, kuti zimunike ansi,																									
Eelyo Magozwe naakaceede biyo asyoonto kuti akkwanye myaka iilikkumi, Tomaasii wakamupa kambi kabbuku. Aaka kabbuku kapandulula musankwa umwi wakumunzi mbuli mbwaakaba ampuwo yamusobano wabbola. Tomaasi wakamubalila caano eeci ziindi zinji kusikila limwi bumwi buzuba wakati, “Ndilombozya kuti uunke kucikolo kutegwa ukaiye kubala bumwi buzuba.” Tomaasi wakapandulwida Magozwe kuti kulibusena bumwi ooko kwalo bana nkobaiya.																									
Wakeezyeezya makani aaya abusena oobo alimwi akubikkilizya amakani akuya kucikolo. Ino kuti naa kacili ncamasimpe kuti baacisyanyina bakaliluleme nibakalikumwaambila kuti wakali cikopo kapati cakuti takozyi akwiiya.    Ino kuti bakamuume kubusena bwaceenzu ooko. Ndiza cilainda Kubota kuti ndacaala biyo nkweena okuno.																									
Wakazumuna kulya musalo antoomwe a Tomaasi aboobo kakunyina akusowa ciindi wakaunka.																									
Kumane waawo Magozwe wakatalika kukkala mung’nda oomu. Wakalikoona abeenzinyina bobilo. Antoomwe bana bakalikukkala moomu mung’anda bakali kkumi antoomwe aba Cissy alimwi abalumi babo, babwa botatwe, kakkiti alimwi, kaaze alimwi ampongo yomwe ncembele.																									
Magozwe wakatalika kwiiya cikolo akujana buyumuyumu. Zinji zyakalikuyandika kuti akozye kweelana abenzinyina. Zimwi ziindi wakali kulimvwa kutyompokelwa alimwi akuyanda kucileka. Pele wakaayeeyela makani ngaakajana mubbuku lyakwe mumakwiisyilili.																									
Magozwe wakalikkede anze ang’anda iilaaciluli canyanzabili, kabala kabbuku. Tomaasi wakasika alimwi akukkala munsi lyakwe. “Kaambanzi kabbuku aaka?” wakabuzya Tomaasi.    “Kabbuku kaambaula musankwa wakaba mwiiyi,” wakamvwiila Magozwe.    “Ino nguni zina lyakwe?” wakabuzya Tomaasi.    “Izina lyakwe ngu Magozwe,” wakamvwiila Magozwe kumwi kamwetula-mwetula.																									
ziendelezye isikati amasiku akwaanzaanya mumuni amudima, Nkabela Leza wakabona kuti ncintu cibotu.																									
Aboobo kwakaba igoko, alimwi kwakaba cifumo, buzuba bwane.																									
Lino Leza wakaamba kuti, Maanzi avuzye makamu makamu aazintu zyuumi																									
abalo bayuni bauluke atala lyanyika mumweenya wakujulu.																									
Nkabela Leza wakalenga banyama bapati bamulwizi azintu zyoonse zyuumi ziputauka,																									
maanzi nzyaakavuzya cimwi acimwi mbuli musyobo waco,																									
abayuni boonse bauluka umwi aumwi mbuli musyobo wakwe.																									
Nkabela Leza wakabona kuti ncintu cibotu.																									
Elyo Leza wakazilongezya, wati, Amuzyalisye, muvule, muzuzye maanzi aamulwizi,																									
abalo bayuni bavule munyika. Aboobo kwakaba igoko, alimwi kwakaba cifumo, buzuba bwasanu.																									
Lino Leza wakaamba kuti, Amwalo munyika muzwe zintu zyuumi,																									
cimwi acimwi mbuli musyobo waco. Muzwe iŋombe abauka abanyama baansi,																									
umwi aumwi mbuli musyobo wakwe. Nkabela kwakaba obo. Leza wakacita banyama baansi,																									
umwi aumwi mbuli musyobo wakwe, aŋombe zyamisyobo misyobo, abauka boonse baansi bamisyobo misyobo, Nkabela Leza wakabona kuti ncintu cibotu.																									
Elyo Leza wakaamba kuti, Atupange muntu mucinkozya cesu, abe mbubonya mbuli ndiswe.																									
Baendelezye inswi zyamumaanzi, abayuni bakujulu, aŋombe, anyika yoonse, abauka boonse bayavula ansi.																									
Nkabela Leza wakalenga muntu mucinkozya cakwe, Wakamulenga mucinkozya caLeza.																									
Wakabalenga baalumi abanakazi. Lino Leza wakabalongezya, Leza wakabaambila kuti,																									
Amuzyalisye, muvule, muzuzye nyika akwiibombya. Amweendelezye inswi zyamulwizi																									
abayuni bakujulu abanyama boonse baputauka ansi. Alimwi Leza wakati, Amubone! Zisyu																									
zyoonse zizyala imbuto ziboneke ansi, amisamu yoonse iili amicelo yamisamu iizyala																									
imbuto, zyoonse buyo ndamupa, zibe zilyo zyanu. Aboobo banyama boonse baansi abayuni																									
boonse bakujulu abauka boonse baansi bajisi muuya wabuumi, ndabapa zisyu zyoonse																									
zisyuuka, zibe zyakulya zyabo. Nkabela kwakaba obo. Elyo Leza naakabona zintu zyoonse																									
nzyaakacita, wakabona kuti zyoonse zyabota loko. Aboobo kwakaba igoko,																									
alimwi kwakaba cifumo, buzuba bwamusanu abumwi.																									
Leza mbwaakalyokezya buzuba bwamusanu aabili																									
Lino ijulu anyika zyakamana, azyoonse zili mumo. Nkabela mubuzuba bwamusanu aabili																									
Leza wakaleka milimo yakwe njaakacitide. Mubuzuba obo bwamusanu aabili wakalyokezya																									
kuzwa kumilimo yakwe yoonse njaakacita. Aboobo Leza wakakondezya buzuba bwamusanu																									
aabili akubusalazya, nkaambo mulimbubo wakalyokezya kuzwa kumilimo yakwe yoonse																									
Leza njaakalenga akucita. Muunda wa-Edeni																									
Ngaaya makani aajulu anyika mbuzyakatalika nizyakalengwa, Mubuzuba obuya Jehova Leza																									
naakacita nyika ajulu, ziziki zyamusokwe zyoonse nizyatakalina kuboneka munyika,																									
amisamu yamusokwe niyatakalina kumena, (nkaambo Jehova Leza katana kuwisya imvula																									
anyika, alimwi katakwe muntu wakupanda nyika, pele mwakazwa izambangulwe munyika,																									
lyakali kutetya nyika yoonse), Jehova Leza wakabumba muntu, Wakamubumbya bulongo																									
bwaansi, wamufulida mumpemu zyakwe muuya wabuumi, nkabela mpawo muntu wakaba muumi.																									
Lino Jehova Leza wakalima muunda kujwe ku-Edeni, nkabela mpempawo mpaakabika oyo muntu ngwaakabumba.																									
Elyo Jehova Leza wakameneka mpoonya awo anyika misamu yoonse iiebeka kumeso																									
amisamu mibotu yakulya. Awalo musamu wabuumi wakaumeneka akati kamuunda, amusamu wakuziba bubotu abubi.																									
Nkabela mumonya mu-Edeni mwakazwa mulonga wakuteteesya muunda, elyo																									
wakapambukanya, waba zipanzi zyone. Izina lyacitaanzi ngu-Pisoni, ncencico cizyunguluka																									
nyika yoonse ya-Havila, ingolida nkwiibede. Ingolida yanyika eyo nimbotu, alimwi																									
nkukonya oko kuli mundaalila amabwe mayandisi aaonukisi. Azina lyamulonga wabili																									
																									
ngu-Gihoni, ngonguwo uuzyunguluka nyika yoonse ya-Kusi. Azina lyamulonga watatu																									
ngu-Hidekeli, ngonguwo uutola kujwe ku-Asuri. Amulonga wane ngu-Firate. Lino Jehova																									
Leza wakabweza oyo muntu, wamubika mumuunda wa-Edeni kuti aulime akuubamba.																									
Nkabela Jehova Leza wakalailila muntu kuti, Misamu yoonse yamumuunda ncobeni																									
uyooilya, cita musamu wakuziba bubotu abubi. Toelede kulya kulinguwo pe, nkaambo																									
mubuzuba obo mboyoolya kulinguwo ncobeni uyoofwa.																									
Lino Jehova Leza wakati, Tacili cibotu kuti muntu akale alike pe, Atumucitile sikumugwasya																									
uumweelede. Mpawo Jehova Leza wakabumba bulongo, wacita banyama boonse																									
bamusokwe, abayuni boonse bakujulu, wabaleta kumuntu, abone na ulabaulika buti. Nkabela																									
banyama boonse, kufumbwa mazina muntu ngaakabaulika, bakaulikwa mbubonya. Aboobo																									
muntu wakaulika iŋombe zyoonse abayuni bakujulu abanyama boonse bamusokwe mazina.																									
Nekubaboobo teekwakajaninwa muntu sikugwasya uumweelede. Elyo Jehova Leza																									
wakaoneka muntu iŋonzi impati, Nkabela naakacili mukoona, wakabweza kamwi																									
katumpango twakwe, wasinka cipulo cako. Lino ako kampango nkaakagwisya mumuntu,																									
Jehova Leza wakakabumbya mwanakazi, wamuleta kumuntu. Mpawo muntu wakaamba kuti,																									
Ma! Ncobeni oyu ulijisi zifuwa mbubonya mbuli zifuwa zyangu anyama mbubonya mbuli																									
nyama yangu. Uleelede kuulikwa mukaintu, nkaambo wazwa mumuntu. Nkaambo kako																									
mwaalumi uleelede kusia wisi abanyina akukakatila kumwanakazi wakwe, babe nyama																									
yomwe buyo. Nkabela boonse bobile bakali basizinswe, mwaalumi abanakwe, pele																									
kabatakwe insoni. Adamu a-Eva mbubakabisya																									
Lino inzoka kiijisi maanu kwiinda banyama boonse bamusokwe Jehova Leza mbaakalenga.																									
Nkabela yakaambila mwanakazi kuti, Sa ncobeni Leza wakaamba kuti, Tamweelede kulya																									
misamu yoonse yamumuunda? Elyo mwanakazi wakaambila inzoka kuti, Micelo yamisamu																									
yamumuunda tulailya, pele micelo yamusamu oyo uuli mukati kamuunda, Leza waamba																									
kuti, Tamweelede kulya njiyo pe, alimwi tamweelede kwiiguma, kuti mutafwi. Mpawo																									
inzoka yakaambila mwanakazi kuti, Ne! Tamukonzyi kufwa pe. Nkaambo Leza ulizi kuti																									
mubuzuba obo mbubonya mbomuyooulya, meso aanu ayoojuka, lino muyooba mbuli Leza,																									
muyooziba bubotu abubi mbububede. Lino mwanakazi wakabona kuti musamu mubotu																									
kukuulya, alimwi ulabotezya meso, alimwi ulayandika kukupa muntu busongo. Nkabela																									
mpawo wakabweza micelo yawo, walya. Alakwe mulumaakwe, wakamupa, alakwe wakalya.																									
Mpoonya awo meso aabo boonse bobile akajaluka, nkabela bakaziba kuti bali azinswe, Lino bakatalika kusuma matu aamukuyu akulicitila zilivumbilizyo.																									
Lino bakamvwa ijwi lya-Jehova Leza uleendeenda mumuunda izuba nelyakatalika kubomba, nkabela oyo muntu Adamu abanakwe bakayuba akati kamisamu yamumuunda kuti																									
bataboneki kumeso aa-Jehova Leza. Elyo Jehova Leza wakaita Adamu, wati, Uli kuli? Wakavuwa kuti, Ndamvwa ijwi lyako mumuunda, lino ndafwa bweeme nkaambo kakuti																									
ndisicinswe, aboobo ndayuba. Wakati, Ino ngwani wakakulwiida kuti uli sicinswe? Sa walya																									
micelo yamusamu oyo ngundakakulailila kuti, Utalyi kulinguwo? Mpawo Adamu wakati,																									
Oyo mwanakazi nguwakandipa kuti tube awe nguwandipa micelo yamusamu, elyo ndalya.																									
Lino Jehova Leza wakaambila mwanakazi kuti, Ino ncinzi eci ncowacita? Mwanakazi wakati,																									
Inzoka njiyakandoongelezya, aboobo ndalya. Mpawo Jehova Leza wakaambila inzoka kuti,																									
Mbowacita obo, ulitukidwe kwiinda iŋombe zyoonse abanyama boonse bamusokwe.																									
Uyooenda abula bwako, abulongo buyooba zilyo zyako, mazuba oonse aabuponi bwako.																									
Nkabela njoobusya inkondo akati kanduwe amwanakazi, akati kalunyungu lwako alunyungu																									
lwakwe. Walo uyookuuma amutwe, ayebo uyoomuluma kukasinde. Lino mwanakazi																									
wakamwaambila kuti, Njookuvuzizya macise aako akuminta kwako, uyoozyala bana																									
amacise, alimwi uyoosukama mulumaako, ngonguwe uuti kakweendelezye. Alakwe Adamu																									
wakamwaambila kuti, Mbowaswiilila ijwi lyamukaako akulya micelo njindakulailila kuti																									
toelede kwiilya, nyika ilitukidwe nkaambo kanduwe, Uyoolya micelo yayo mumacise																									
mazuba oonse aabuponi bwako. Iyookuzyalila mamvwa amitubetube. Uyoolya zisyu																									
zyamusokwe. Uyoolya insima cakufwa mitukuta mane ukapiluke kunyika, nkaambo																									
mulinjiyo mowakagwisigwa, nkaambo uli bulongo buyo, akooko kubulongo nkoelede																									
kupiluka. Lino Adamu wakaulika izina lyamukaakwe kuti ngu-Eva, nkaambo mbebanyina																									
baumi boonse. Nkabela Jehova Leza wakacitila Adamu amukaakwe zibaki zyazikanda, wabasamika nzizyo.																									
Lino Jehova Leza wakati, Bona! Muntu waba mbubonya mbuli ndiswe. Ulizi bubotu abubi																									
mbuzibede, Lino atucenjele, kuti atatandabiki ijanza lyakwe akucela micelo yamusamu																									
wabuumi, atalyi njiyo, ataponi mane kukabe kutamani. Elyo Jehova Leza wakamutanda																									
kuzwa kumuunda wa-Edeni kuti akalime nyika eyo njiyonya njaakagwisigwa mulinjiyo.																									
Wakatanda muntu, alimwi kulubazu lwakujwe lwa-Edeni wakabika baangelo bakerebimu																									
apanga lyamabekabeka ilyakali kuyumbana koonse koonse kusinkila inzila yamusamu wabuumi.																									
Kaini mbwaakajaya Abelo. Lino Adamu wakaswanana a-Eva banakwe, nkabela wakaminta, wazyala Kaini, wati, Ndajana muntu kuli-Jehova.																									
Alimwi wakazyala lwabili, wazyala munyina Abelo. Nkabela Abelo wakaba sikweembela																									
imbelele, pele Kaini wakaba sikupanda nyika. Lino necakaba ciindi, Kaini wakaletela Jehova																									
cituuzyo camicelo yanyika. Alakwe Abelo wakaleta kabalwebalwe wambelele amafuta aazyo. Lino Jehova wakabotelwa Abelo acituuzyo cakwe, pele Kaini acituuzyo cakwe																									
takwakamubotelwa pe. Nkabela Kaini wakakalala loko, abusyu bwakwe bwakasyulungana.																									
Mpawo Jehova wakaambila Kaini kuti, Ino wakalalilanzi? Nkaambonzi busyu bwako																									
bulisyulungene? Na wacita kabotu, sa tokooyoonyampuzigwa na? Pele na tociti kabotu, zibi																									
zilakubutilila kumulyango, Lino uyoosukama nduwe, nkabela uyoomweendelezya.																									
Lino Kaini wakaambila munyina Abelo kuti, Atweende musokwe. Nkabela nebakali																									
musokwe, Kaini wakanyampukila Abelo munyina, wamujaya. Elyo Jehova wakabuzya Kaini																									
kuti, Uli kuli Abelo mwanike wako? Wakaamba kuti, Nsimubwene pe. Sa ndime sikulela																									
mwanike wangu? Lino wakati, Ma! Wacitanzi? Ijwi lyabulowa bwamwanike wako																									
lilandikwiilila kuzwa muvu. Lino sunu wajana lutuko kuvu elyo ndilyonya ilyanywa bulowa																									
bwamwanike wako buzwa kujanza lyako. Nozoolima ivu, talikooyookupa limbi inguzu																									
zyalyo. Uyooba sikweendeenda asimutuntuli ansi. Mpawo Kaini wakaambila Jehova kuti,																									
Kuumwa kwangu nkunjumwide nkupati kampatila. Ncobeni buzuba obuno wanditanda																									
kuzwa kunyika, aboobo njoosiswa kumeso aako, Njooba sikweendeenda asimutuntuli																									
munyika, nkabela kufumbwa muntu uundijana uyoondijaya. Mpawo Jehova wakamwaambila																									
kuti, Mbubo, Kufumbwa muntu uujaya Kaini uyooindulwidwa kupegwa mulandu ziindi zili																									
musanu azibili, Nkabela Jehova wakabikila Kaini citondezyo, kuti umwi aumwi uumujana atamujayi.																									
Mizukulu ya-Kaini. Lino Kaini wakazwa kubusyu bwa-Jehova, waakukala munyika yaNodi																									
iili kujwe lya-Edeni.																									
Elyo Kaini wakaswanana amukaakwe, nkabela wakaminta, wazyala Enoki. Alimwi																									
wakayaka munzi, lino oyo munzi wakauulika izina lya-Enoki mbubonya mbuli izina																									
lyamwaanakwe. Lino Enoki alakwe wakazyalilwa Iradi, alakwe Iradi wakazyala Mehujaeli,																									
alakwe Mehujaeli wakazyala Metusaeli, alakwe Metusaeli wakazyala Lameki. Lino Lameki																									
wakakwata banakazi bobile; izina lya umwi kali Ada, azina lyawabili kali Zila. Nkabela Ada																									
ngowakazyala jabali, ngonguwe wisaabo boonse bakala mumatente akweembela iŋombe.																									
Azina lyamwanike wakwe kali Jubali, ngonguwe wisaabo boonse balizya kantimbwa																									
anyeele. Alakwe Zila wakazyala Tubala-Kaini, ngonguwe iwakali kufula zibelesyo zyoonse																									
zyamukuba azyabutale. Amucizi wa-Tubela-Kaini kali Naama.																									
Lino Lameki wakaambila banakazi bakwe kuti, Ada a-Zila, amuswiilile ijwi lyangu.																									
Nubanakazi ba-Lameki amuteelele majwi angu.Nkaambo ndajaya muntu iwakandiyasa,																									
Ndanyonyoona mulombe nkaambo kakunduuma. Kaini ulatemwa mulandu ziindi zili musanu azibili.																									
Sa Lameki takooyootemwa ziindi zili makumi aali musanu aabili amusanu azibili na?																									
Seti mbwaakazyalwa. Lino Adamu wakaswanana alimwi abanakwe, nkabela wakazyala mwana mulombe. Lino wakamuulika izina lya-Seti, nkaambo wakati, Leza wandipa mwana umbi mucibaka ca-Abelo, Kaini ngwaakajaya. Alakwe Seti wakazyalilwa mwana, nkabela wakamuulika izina lya-Enosi. Mpoonya awo bantu bakatalika kukomba muzina lya-Jehova.																									
Mazyalano aabantu kuzwa kuli-Adamu kusikila kuli-Nowa																									
Ndeeli ibbuku lyamazyalano aa-Adamu. Mubuzuba obo Leza naakalenga muntu,																									
wakamulenga mucinkozya ca-Leza. Wakabalenga boonse, mwaalumi amwanakazi, alimwi																									
wakabalongezya akubaulika izina lyaAdamu mubuzuba obo nibakalengwa. Lino Adamu,																									
naakamana kupona myaka iili mwanda amakumi otatwe, wakazyala mwana mucinkezya																									
cakwe, iwakali mbubonya mbuli nguwe, wamuulika izina lya-Seti. Lino mazuba Adamu																									
ngaakapona naakamana kuzyala Seti akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aitatu, alimwi																									
wakazyala bana balombe abasimbi. Aboobo mazuba oonse Adamu ngaakapona akasika																									
kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aine amakumi otatwe, elyo wakafwa.																									
Nkabela Seti, naakamana kupona myaka iili mwanda amusanu, wakazyala Enosi. Lino myaka																									
Seti njaakapona naakamana kuzyala Enosi yakasika kumyanda iili musanu aitatu amyaka iili																									
musanu aibili. Aboobo mazuba oonse Seti ngaakapona akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili																									
musana aine akumi aibili, elyo wakafwa.																									
Nkabela Enosi, naakamana kupona myaka iili makumi aali musanu aane, wakazyala Kenani.																									
Alimwi mazuba Enosi ngaakapona naakamana kuzyala Kenani akasika kumyaka iili myanda																									
iili musanu aitatu amyaka iili ikumi aisanu, nkabela wakazyala bana balombe abasimbi.																									
Aboobo mazuba oonse Enosi ngaakapona akasika kumyanda iili musanu aine amyaka yosanwe, elyo wakafwa.																									
Nkabela Kenani, naakamana kupona myaka iili makumi aali musanu aabili, wakazyala Mahalalele. Alimwi mazuba Kenani ngaakapona naakamana kuzyala Mahalalele akasika																									
kumyanda iili musanu aitatu amakumi one, nkabela wakazyala bana balombe abasimbi.																									
Aboobo mazuba oonse Kenani ngaakapona akasika kumyanda iili musanu aine akumi, elyo wakafwa.																									
Alakwe Mahalalele, naakamana kupona myaka iili makumi aali musanu alimwi amyaka																									
yosanwe, wakazyala jaredi. Lino mazuba Mahalalele ngaakapona naakamana kuzyala																									
Jaredi, akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aitatu amakumi otatwe; alimwi wakazyala																									
bana balombe abasimbi. Aboobo mazuba oonse Mahalalele ngaakapona akasika kumyaka																									
iili myanda iili musanu aitatu amakumi aali musanu aane amyaka yosanwe, elyo wakafwa,																									
Lino Jaredi, naakamana kupona myaka iili mwanda amakumi aali musanu alimwi aibili wakazyala Enoki. Nkabela mazuba Jaredi ngaakapona naakamana kuzyala Enoki akasika																									
kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aitatu, alimwi wakazyala bana balombe abasimbi.																									
Aboobo mazuba oonse Jaredi ngaakapona akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aine																									
amakumi aali musanu alimwi aibili, elyo wakafwa.																									
Lino Enoki, naakamana kupona myaka iili makumi aali musanu alimwi amyaka yosanwe,																									
wakazyala Metusela. Nkabela naakamana kuzyala Metusela, Enoki wakali kweenda a-Leza																									
myaka iili myanda yotatwe, alimwi wakazyala bana balombe abasimbi. Aboobo mazuba																									
oonse aa-Enoki akasika kumyaka iili myanda yotatwe amakumi aali musanu alimwi																									
amusanu. Nkabela Enoki wakali kweenda a-Leza mane lumwi kataciwo, nkaambo Leza wakamutola.																									
Lino Metusela, naakamana kupona myaka iili mwanda amakumi aali musanu aatatu amusanu																									
aibili, wakazyala Lameki. Alimwi mazuba Metusela ngaakapona naakamana kuzyala																									
Lameki akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aibili amakumi aali musanu aatatu amyaka																									
yobile, nkabela wakazyala bana balombe abasimbi. Aboobo mazuba oonse Metusela																									
ngaakapona akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aine amakumi aali musanu alimwi amusanu aine; elyo wakafwa.																									
Lino Lameki, naakamana kupona myaka iili mwanda amakumi aali musanu aatatu amyaka																									
yobile, wakazyala mwana mulombe. Nkabela wakamuulika izina lya-Nowa, nkaambo																									
wakati, Oyu mwana nguukonzya kutuumbulizya mumilimo yesu akutulemununa makataazyo																									
ngaajana maanza esu nkaambo kanyika Jehova njaatukide. Nkabela mazuba Lameki																									
ngaakapona naakamana kuzyala Nowa akasika kumyaka iili myanda yosanwe amakumi aali																									
musanu aane amusanu, alimwi wakazyala bana balombe abasimbi. Aboobo mazuba oonse																									
Lameki ngaakapona akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aibili amakumi aali musanu																									
aabili amyaka iili musanu aibili, elyo wakafwa.																									
Lino Nowa naakaba amyaka iili myanda yosanwe, wakazyala Semu a-Hamu a-Jafeti.																									
Nowa mbwaakali mululami akati kabantu basizibi																									
Lino bantu nibakatalika kuvula ansi, alimwi nibakali kuzyala bana basimbi, bana ba-Leza																									
bakabona bana basimbi babantu kuti mbabotu, nkabela bakakwata kufumbwa mbobakali																									
kuyanda akati kabo. Mpawo Jehova wakaamba kuti, Muuya wangu tuukooyookazyanya																									
lyoonse amuntu pe, nkaambo ninyama buyo. Mazuba aakwe ayooba myaka iili mwaanda																									
amakumi obile. Mumazuba alya kakuli babbabbani ansi. Nkabela kusule lyayaaya, bana																									
ba-Leza nibakaswanana abana basimbi babantu, bakabazyalila bana, mbombabo bakaba basinguzu baciindi, bantu basimpuwo.																									
Lino Jehova wakabona kuti bubi bwabantu baansi bulayoosya, amiyeeyo yoonse bantu njibayeeya mumyoyo yabo mibi luzutu mazuba oonse, aboobo­ Jehova wakausa nkaambo																									
kakulenga muntu, wakapenga mumoyo wakwe. Nkabela Jehova wakaamba kuti, Bantu																									
mbondakalenga, nzoobaziminganya ansi. Nzooziminganya bantu abanyama, bauka abayuni																									
bakujulu boonse, nkaambo nda usa kuti ndakabalenga. Pele Nowa wakafwidwa luzyalo mumeso aa-Jehova.																									
Njeeyi mizukulu ya-Nowa. Nowa kali muntu uululeme, katajisi kampenda, akati																									
kabasaanyina. Nowa wakali kweenda a-Leza. Nkabela Nowa wakazyala bana botatwe, Semu, Hamu a-Jafeti.																									
Lino nyika yakabija kumeso aa-Leza, alimwi nyika yakazula luuni. Lino Leza wakabona																									
kuti nyika yabija, nkaambo bantu boonse bakalibisizye inzila zyabo ansi, nkabela Leza																									
wakaambila Nowa kuti, Ndakanza kumanisya bantu boonse, nkaambo nyika ilizwide luuni																									
nkaambo kabo. Ncobeni njoobanyonyoona anyika yoonse. Kolipangila bwaato bwazisamu																									
zyagofa. Obu bwaato ubucite azimpetu, alimwi uleelede kubuziluluzya mukati aanze insakizi.																									
Mbuboobu mboelede kubucita. Bulamfu bwabwaato buleelede kuba tukokola tuli myanda																									
yotatwe, bwaamba bwabo bube tukokola tuli makumi osanwe, abwiime bwabo bube tukokola																									
tuli makumi otatwe. Ucite impulunguzyo mubwaato, zibe kakokola komwe kuzwa																									
kulululi, Awalo mulyango wabwaato uubike mulubazu lwabo. Alimwi yaka zimpetu zyaansi,																									
azimwi zyabili zyakujulu, azimwi zyatatu kujulu lyazeezyo. Lino mebo ndaleta																									
izambangulwe lyamaanzi ansi lyakunyonyoozya nyama yoonse yabaumi baputa ansi, Boonse																									
buyo bali munyika bayoozanga. Pele webo tuyootangana cizuminano ayebo, aboobo																									
uyoonjila mubwaato, webo abana bako amukaako abamukabana bako. Alimwi akati																									
kabanyama bamisyobo yoonse, uyoonjizya bobile bobile mubwaato kuti baponesegwe																									
anduwe, Bayooba mweenze amuzyazi. Abalo bayuni bamisyobo misyobo, abanyama																									
bamisyobo misyobo, abauka bamisyobo misyobo bayavula ansi bobile bobile baleelede kuba																									
ayebo kuti baponesegwe. Alimwi bweza zilyo zyamisyobo yoonse, kufumbwa ziligwa,																									
ukazilondole, kuti zibe bulilu bwako abulilu bwabo. Lino Nowa wakacita obo. Wakacita																									
mbubonya mbuli Leza mbwakamulailila.																									
Izambangulwe mbulyakayuminina																									
Lino Leza wakaibaluka Nowa abaumi boonse abanyama mbaakali abo mubwaato. Mpawo																									
Leza wakaungya muuwo anyika, nkabela maanzi akatalika kuyosa. Tusensa toonse																									
twamatoolo azipulo zyakujulu zyoonse zyakasinkwa, awalo mucobocobo wakalesegwa.																									
Maanzi akali kuya buunguluka ansi, mane lumwi kumamanino aamazuba aali mwanda																									
amakumi osanwe maanzi akaceya. Lino mumwezi wamusanu aibili, mubuzuba bwakumi amusanu aabili bwamumwezi, bwaato bwakacuta azilundu zyaArarati. Nkabela maanzi																									
akacili kuya buceya mane kusikila kumwezi wakumi, lino mumwezi wakumi, mubuzuba																									
butaanzi bwamumwezi, mitwe yazilundu yakaboneka.																									
Amane buyo mazuba aali makumi one, Nowa wakajalula cipulo ncakacitide mubwaato,																									
watuma cikwangala. Nkabela wakauluka-uluka koonse koonse mane maanzi akayuminina																									
ansi. Alimwi wakatuma inziba, kuti abone na maanzi atalika kuceya ansi. Pele inziba																									
teeyakajana mpiikonzya kukalila amyeendo yayo, aboobo yakapiluka kulinguwe mubwaato,																									
nkaambo maanzi akacili manji atala anyika. Mpawo wakatandabika ijanza lyakwe, waijata,																									
waiboozya mubwaato mwaakabede. Lino wakalindila alimwi mazuba aali musanu aabili,																									
watuma inziba lwabili kuzwa mubwaato. Elyo kuciindi cakumazuba inziba yakaboola																									
kulinguwe, amumulomo wayo kiijisi itu lyaolifa ndeyakaakucela. Mpawo Nowa wakaziba																									
kuti maanzi atalika kuceya ansi. Lino wakalindila alimwi mazuba aali musanu aabili,																									
watuma inziba, pele tiikwe neyakaboola limbi pe.																									
Lino mumwaka wamyanda iili musanu aumwi amwaka omwe, mumwezi mutaanzi,																									
mubuzuba butaanzi bwamumwezi, maanzi akayuminina ansi. Mpawo Nowa wakavumbula																									
lululi lwabwaato, wasondela, wabona kuti nyika yayuma. Nkabela mumwezi wabili,																									
mubuzuba bwakumi amusanu aibili bwamumwezi, nyika yakayuma ntantalu. Lino Leza																									
wakaambila Nowa kuti, Kamuzwa mubwaato, yebo abanako, abana bako abamukabana																									
bako boonse. Banyama boonse mboli abo bamisyobo misyobo, bayuni aŋombe abauka																									
boonse bayavula ansi, uzwe abo, kuti babe isaula ansi, bazyalisye akuvula ansi. Mpawo																									
Nowa wakazwa abana bakwe abanakwe abamukabana bakwe boonse. Banyama boonse,																									
abauka boonse abayuni boonse, boonse baumi bamisyobo misyobo bayavula ansi, boonse biyo bakazwa mubwaato.																									
Lino Nowa wakayakila Jehova cipaililo, nkabela wakabweza bamwi banyama basalala																									
bamisyobo yoonse abayuni basalala bamisyobo yoonse, watuulila zituuzyo mpoonya awo																									
acipaililo. Mpawo Jehova naakamvwa bweema bubotu, Jehova wakaamba mumoyo																									
wakwe kuti, Nsikooyootuka limbi nyika nkaambo kabantu pe, nkaambo miyeeyo yamoyo																									
wamuntu mibi lyoonse kuzwa kubwanike bwakwe, alimwi nsikooyoouma limbi baumi																									
boonse mbuli mbondakacita. Nyika niiciliwo, ciindi cakubyala aciindi cakutebula, impeyo																									
ankasaalo, cilimo amainza, isikati amasiku, zyoonse tazikooyooleka.																									
Cizuminano Leza ncaakatangana anyika																									
Lino Leza wakalongezya Nowa abana bakwe, wabaambila kuti, Amuzyalisye, muvule,																									
muzuzye nyika. Banyama boonse baansi abayuni boonse bakujulu bamuyoowe akukankama																									
kubusyu bwanu. Boonse biyo, abauka bayavula ansi answi zyamulwizi, baabwa mumaanza																									
aanu. Baumi boonse bayavula ansi bayoomubeda zilyo, mbubonya mbuli zisyu zisia-sia. Zyoonse biyo ndamupa nzizyo. Pele tamweelede kulya nyama antoomwe abuumi bwayo,																									
nkokuti bulowa bwayo. Ncobeni bulowa bwanu, bulowa bwabuumi bwanu,																									
njoobuyandaula. Kumaanza aabanyama boonse njoobuyandaula, akumaanza aamuntu																									
njoobuyandaula. Muntu umwi aumwi, kumaanza aamweenzinyina njooyandaula buumi																									
bwakwe. Kufumbwa muntu uutila bulowa bwamuntunyina, bulowa bwakwe alakwe																									
buyootilwa kumaanza aamuntu, nkaambo muntu wakalengwa mucinkozya ca-Leza.																									
Lino nywebo amuzyalisye akuvula, mube banji munyika akuvula mulinjiyo.																									
Elyo Leza wakaambila Nowa abana bakwe mbaakali abo kuti, Amubone! Mebo ndatangana																									
anywe cizuminano cangu, nywebo alunyungu lwanu luciza, abanyama boonse mbomuli																									
abo, bayuni bakujulu abanyama baansi aboonse mbomuli abo mubwaato, banyama boonse																									
biyo baansi. Njootangana anywe cizuminano, nkabela bantu boonse																									
tabakooyoonyonyoonwa limbi mumaanzi aazambangulwe. Takukooyooba limbi																									
izambangulwe lyakuvwinyauna nyika. Alimwi Leza wakaamba kuti, Nceeci citondezyo																									
cacizuminano cangu ncitutangene anywe, inywe abaumi boonse mbomuli abo mumazyalani																									
oonse. Ndabika fulicoongo wangu mujoba, abe citondezyo cacizuminano cangu																									
ncitutangene anyika. Kuyooba kuti, na ndabusya ijoba ajulu lyanyika, fulicoongo wangu																									
uyooboneka mujoba, elyo njooyeeya cizuminano ncitutangene anywe, inywe abaumi																									
boonse bamisyobo yoonse, Takukooyoosika limbi maanzi aazambangulwe kuzoovwinyauna																									
bantu boonse. Fulicoongo uyooba mukati kajoba, lino njoomulanga akuyeeya cizuminano																									
citeeli ca-Leza ncatangene abaumi boonse bamisyobo yoonse yaansi. Leza wakaambila																									
Nowa kuti, Nceeci citondezyo cacizuminano cangu ncintangene abaumi boonse baansi.																									
Hamu mbwaakasampaula wisi. Lino bana ba-Nowa ibakazwa mubwaato mbaaba:																									
Semu a-Hamu a-Jafeti. Hamu nguwakazyala Kanana. Aba botatwe bakali bana baNowa,																									
nkabela mbembabo ibakazuzya nyika yoonse.																									
Lino Nowa wakatalika kulima nyika. Wakalima muunda wamasaansa Lino naakanywa																									
waini, wakakolwa, walivumbulula mucilao cakwe. Nkabela Hamu wisi Kanana wakabona																									
cinswe cawisi, walwiida babunyina bakwe bobile ibakali anze. Lino Semu a-Jafeti																									
bakabweza cikobela, bacibika amakuko aabo bobile, beenda cibundasule, bavumba cinswe																									
cawisaabo. Masyu aabo akali futete, aboobo teebakabona cinswe cawisaabo. Elyo Nowa																									
naakasinsimuka kuzwa kukukolwa kwakwe, wakaziba mwanaakwe muniini ncaakamucitila, nkabela wakati,																									
Aombolozekwe Kanana! Uzooba muzike wabazike akati kabanyina!																									
Alimwi wakati, Alumbwe Jehova Leza wa-Semu, Kanana abe muzike wakwe.																									
Leza akomezye lunyungu lwa-Jafeti, Akale muzilao zya-Semu. Alakwe Kanana abe muzikewakwe.																									
Nkabela izambangulwe nilyakamana, Nowa wakacili kupona myaka iili myanda yotatwe amakumi osanwe. Aboobo mazuba oonse aa-Nowa akasika kumyaka iili myanda iili musanu aine amakumi osanwe, elyo wakafwa.																									
Mazyalani aabana ba-Nowa. Ngaaya mazyalani aabana ba-Nowa, Semu,																									
Hamu a-Jafeti. Izambangulwe nilyakamana, bakazyalilwa bana.																									
Bana ba-Jafeti mbaaba: Gomeri a-Magogi a-Madai a-Javani a-Tubali a-Meseki a-Tirasi.																									
Abana ba-Gomeri mbaaba: Asikenazi a-Rifati a-Togarima. Abana ba-Javani mbaaba:																									
Elisa a-Tarisisi, Kitimu a-­Dodanimu. Inyungu zyabaaba nzezyakaabana nyika zyabamasi																									
zili kunkomwe yalwizi, umwi aumwi mbuli mwaambo wakwe aluzubo lwakwe akati kabamasi,																									
Abana ba-Hamu mbaaba: Kusi a-Mizraimu a-Puti a-Kanana. Abana ba-Kusi mbaaba: Seba																									
a-Havila a-Sabeta a-Raama a-Sabeteka. Abana ba-Raama mbaaba: Seba a-Dedani.																									
Nkabela Kusi wakazyala Nimrodi, ngonguwe iwakataanguna kuba mwaalumi sintaze ansi.																									
Kali muvwimi singuzu kumeso aa-Jehova. Nciceeco ncicaambilwa kuti, Mbuli Nimrodi																									
muvwimi singuzu kumeso aa-Jehova. Kumatalikilo bwami bwakwe bwakali Babuloni																									
a-Ereki a-Akadi a-Kalene munyika ya-Sinara. Kuzwa kunyika eyo wakainka ku-Asuri,																									
waakuyaka Nineve a-Rehoboti-Iri a-Kala, a-Reseni akatikati ka-Nineve a-Kala, ngonguwo munzi mupati. Alakwe Mizraimu wakazyala Ludi a-Anamimu a-Lehabimu																									
a-Nafituhimu, a-Paturusimu a-Kasiluhimu (mulunyungu lwakwe mobakazwa ba-Filisti) a-Kafitorimu.																									
Alakwe Kanana wakazyala Zidoni mwanaakwe mutaanzi, a-Heti, aba-Jebusi, aba-Amori,																									
aba-Girigasi, aba-Hivi aba-Ariki aba-Sini, 18aba-Arivadi, aba-Zemari, aba-Hamati.																									
Nkabela nicakaba ciindi inzubo zyaba-Kanana zyakapalangana. Mugaano waba-Kanana																									
wakali kuzwa ku-Zidoni kuya kulubbazu lwaku-Gerari kusikila ku-Gaza, alimwi kuya																									
ku-Sodoma a-Gomora a-Adima a-Zeboimu, kusikila ku-Lasa. Mbaabo bana ba-Hamu,																									
munzubo zyabo amyambo yabo azisi zyabo amisyobo yabo.																									
Alakwe Semu, wisi bana ba-Eberi, munyina jafeti mupati, wakazyalilwa bana. Bana																									
ba-Semu mbaaba: Elamu a-Asuri a-Arifakisidi a-Ludi a-Aramu. Abana ba-Aramu																									
mbaaba: Uzi a-Huli a-Geteri a-Masi. Nkabela Arifakisidi wakazyala Sela, alakwe Sela wakazyala Eberi. Lino Eberi wakazyalilwa bana bobile. Izina lyaumwi kali Pelegi,																									
nkaambo mumazuba aakwe nyika yakaandaanisigwa, azina lyaumunyina kali Jokitani.																									
Abo boonse bakali bana ba-Jokitani. Nkabela nyika njebakakala njeeyi: kuzwa ku-Mesa kuya ku-Sefari cilundu cakujwe. Mbaaba bana ba-Semu munzubo zyabo amyaambo yabo anyika zyabo azisi zyabo.																									
Nzeezyo inzubo zyabana ba-Nowa mumazyalani aabo amuzisi zyabo. Munyungu zyabo																									
misyobo yabantu moyakapalanganina ansi kusule lyazambangulwe.																									
Abramu mbwaakalonga kuzwa ku-Harani kuya ku-Kanana																									
Lino Jehova wakaambila Abramu kuti, Kozwa munyika yako akucisi cabuzyale bwako																									
akuluzubo lwauso, ukainke kucisi ncenti kutondezye, Njoocita kuti ube musyobo mupati.																									
Njookupa coolwe akulemya izina lyako, ube coolwe. Kufumbwa muntu uukulongezya																									
njoomulongezya, ayooyo uukusampaula Njoomusampaula. Alimwi mulinduwe misyobo yoonse yabantu iyoojana coolwe.																									
Lino Abramu wakainka, mbubonya mbuli Jehova mbwaakamwaambila. Alakwe Loti																									
wakainka awe. Nkabela Abramu kajisi myaka iili makumi aali musanu aabili amyaka																									
yosanwe naakazwa ku-Harani. Nkabela Abramu wakatolelela Sarai banakwe, a-Loti																									
mwana wamwanike wakwe, ambono zyabo zyoonse nzibakavubide, abasiŋanda boonse																									
mbobakajene ku-Harani, Bakainka kuya kunyika ya-Kanana, nkabela bakasika nkukonya																									
oko kunyika ya-Kanana. Lino Abramu wakainda akati kanyika mane wasika kuSekemu,																									
kumubanga waku-More. Nkabela ba-Kanana bakacili munyika. Lino Jehova wakalibonya																									
kuli-Abramu, wakati, Nyika eyi njooipa lunyungu lwako. Elyo wakayakila Jehova cipaililo																									
mpoonya awo Jehova mpaakalibonenya kulinguwe. Nkabela kuzwa oko wakalongela																									
kucilundu cakujwe lya-Beteli, wayaka cilao cakwe nkuko, akatikati kaminzi yobile, Beteli																									
kuuli kububbila, Ai kuuli kubuzwezuba. Aalo awo wakayakila Jehova cipaililo, wakomba																									
muzina lya-Jehova. Pele Abramu kaciya bweenda, kaciya buya kumusanza.																									
Abramu mbwaakaya ku-Egepita. Lino kwakaba ipamba munyika,																									
nkabela Abramu wakainka ku-Egepita kuyookala-kala nkuko, nkaambo ipamba lyakabija																									
munyika. Lino naakasika afwaafwi kumugaano wa-Egepita, wakaambila Sarai mukaakwe																									
kuti, Bona! Ndizi kuti uli mwanakazi mubotu uuebeka loko. Ncobeni ba-Egepita,																									
bakubona biyo, balaamba kuti, Ngooyu mwanakazi wakwe, Lino balandijaya, pele uwe																									
balakusia. Amba kuti, Ndime mucizi wakwe; aboobo makani alabota kulindime nkaambo																									
kako. Muuya wangu upone nkaambo kanduwe. Lino Abramu naakasika ku-Egepita,																									
ba-Egepita bakabona mwanakazi, babona kuti mubotu loko. Nkabela bapati baFarao																									
nebakamubona, bakamutembaula kubusyu bwa-Farao, aboobo mwanakazi wakatolwa																									
kuŋanda ya-Farao. Alakwe Abramu wakacitilwa kabotu nkaambo kakwe, nkabela																									
wakajana imbelele aŋombe ambongolo abazike abalanda banakazi ambongolo inzyazi ankamele.																									
Mpawo Jehova wakapenzya Farao abeŋanda yakwe mapenzi mapati nkaambo ka-Sarai																									
muka-Abramu. Lino Farao wakaita Abramu, wati, Ino ncinzi eci ncowandicitila?																									
Nkaambonzi tokwe kundaambila kuti ngumukaintu wangu? Nkaambonzi nowakaamba																									
kuti mucizi wangu? mane ndakamutola kulindime kuti abe mwanakazi wangu. Ncobeni																									
ngumukaintu wako. Umutole, uinke awe. Nkabela Farao wakalailila bantu bakwe, nkabela																									
bakamusindikizya, walo abanakwe aboonse mbaakali abo.																									
Abramu a-Loti mbubakaanzaana																									
Lino Abramu wakazwa ku-Egepita, walo abanakwe aboonse mbaakali abo a-Loti, wasika																									
ku-Negebi. Nkabela Abramu kali muvubi loko, kajisi iŋombe ansiliva angolida. Lino																									
wakali kweendeenda kuzwa kuNegebi mane wakasika ku-Beteli, oko nkukonya																									
nkwaakataanguna kuyaka zilao zyakwe, akatikati ka-Beteli a-Ai, nkucakabede cipaililo																									
ncaakayaka akutaanguna. Oko Abramu wakakomba muzina lya-Jehova. Alakwe Loti																									
iwakali kweenda a-Abramu kajisi imbelele aŋombe amatente. Nkabela nyika yakaceya;																									
teebakakonzya kukala antoomwe pe, nkaambo kabajisi imbono zinji, aboobo bakakacilwa																									
kukala antoomwe. Lino kwakabuka inkondo akati kabasikweembela iŋombe zya-Abramu																									
abasikweembela iŋombe zya-Loti. Kuciindi eco ba-Kanana aba-Perizi kabacikede munyika.																									
Elyo Abramu wakaambila Loti kuti, Wence kutabi inkondo akati kesu, yebo ambebo,																									
abeembeli bako abeembeli bangu, nkaambo tuli bamukowa omwe. Sa nyika yoonse tiili																									
kubusyu bwako na? Atupambukane ambebo, Na ulayanda kuya kucimwesi, mebo ndaya																									
kululyo; na ulayanda kuya kululyo, mebo ndaya kucimwesi. Mpawo Loti wakatambya																									
meso aakwe, wabona nkwaalale yoonse ya-Jordano, wabona kuti, koonse koonse ili amaanzi. Kuciindi eco, Jehova natakalina kunyonyoona Sodoma a-Gomora, yakali																									
mbubonya mbuli muunda wa-Jehova, mbuli nyika ya-Egepita noya ku-Zoari. Lino Loti																									
wakalisalila inkwaalale yoonse ya-Jordano, watozya kujwe. Mbuboobo mbubakaanzaana																									
amweenzinyina. Abramu kakede munyika ya-Kanana; Loti kakede muminzi yankwaalale,																									
kaya buyakayaka zilao zyakwe mane wakasika ku-Sodoma. Pele bantu ba-Sodoma bakali																									
basizibi, bakali babi loko kumeso aa-Jehova,																									
Lino Jehova wakaambila Abramu, naakamana kwaanzaana a-Loti, wati, Tambya meso aako,																									
ubone koonse koonse kuzwa mpobede, kunyika akumusanza, kujwe akumbo, nkaambo																									
nyika yoonse njowabona, njoipa nduwe alunyungu lwako, mane kukabe kutamani.																									
Njoovuzya lunyungu lwako, lube mbuli lusuko lwaansi. Na muntu ulakonzya kubala lusuko																									
lwaansi, lino lunyungu lwako alwalo luyoobalika. Buka, koya bweendeenda mubulumfu																									
boonse bwanyika akubwaamba bwayo boonse, nkaambo njooipa nduwe. Mpawo Abramu																									
wakalonzya itente lyakwe, wiinka, waakukala kumibanga ya-Mamre iili ku-Hebroni, nkabela																									
wakayakila Jehova cipaililo mpoonya awo.																									
Abramu mbwaakavuna Loti kumaanza aabami bakujwe																									
Lino mumazuba aa-Amarafele mwami wa-Sinara, Arioki mwami wa-Elasara, Kedorelaomere																									
mwami wa-Elamu, a-Tidala mwami wa-Goimu, bakacita inkondo a-Bera mwami																									
wa-Sodoma, a-Birasa mwami wa-Gomora, a-Sinabi mwami wa-Adima a-Semebere mwami																									
wa-Zeboimu, amwami wa-Bela. Aba boonse bakalibungene mukuti																									
lya-Sidimu (ndondulo Lwizi lwa-Munyo). Myaka iili ikumi aibili bakali bazike																									
ba-Kedorelaomere, pele mumwaka wakumi aitatu bakapapila. Lino mumwaka wakumi aine																									
bakeza ba-Kedorelaomere abami mbaakali abo, bazunda ba-Refaimu mu-Aseterote-kamaimu,																									
aba-Zuzi mu-Hamu, aba-Emi mu-Savekiriyataimu, 6aba-Hori mucilundu cabo caku-Seiri,																									
akusikila ku-Eliparana uuli munkanda. Lino kuzwa oko bakaboola, basika ku-Eni-Misipati																									
(ngonguwo Kadesi), bazunda cisi coonse cabaAmaleki, abalo ba-Amori ibakakede																									
mu-Hazezoni-tamara. Mpawo kwakazwa mwami wa-Sodoma, amwami wa-Gomora,																									
amwami wa-Adima, amwami wa-Zeboimu, amwami wa-Bela (ngonguwo Zoari), baswanana																									
akubamba mindando yabo yakulwisya mukuti lya-Sidimu, balwisye Kedorelaomere mwami																									
wa-Elamu, a-Tidala mwami wa-Goimu, a-Amarafele mwami wa-Sinara, a-Arioki mwami																									
wa-Elasara, Bami bone bakalwisya bami bosanwe. Nkabela ikuti lya-Sidimu kalizwide																									
migodi yamulambo. Lino bami ba-Sodoma a-Gomora bakacija, bawida mumonya, abaabo																									
ibakacisyeede bakacijila kucilundu. Elyo bakatola imbono zyoonse zyaku-Sodoma																									
azyaku-Gomora, azilyo zyabo zyoonse, bainka. Alakwe Loti mwana wamunyina Abramu,																									
iwakakede ku-Sodoma, bakamutolelela ambono zyakwe, bainka.																									
Mpawo kwakasika mulobosi, walwiida Abramu mu-Hebrayo, iwakakede kumibanga																									
ya-Mamre mu-Amori munyina Esikoli, munyina Anere, nkaambo abo kabatangene																									
buzwalani a-Abramu. Nkabela Abramu naakamvwa kuti mwanaakwabo watolwa																									
mubuzike, wakayobolola basilumamba bakwe bazyale muŋanda yakwe, bantu bali myanda																									
yotatwe akumi amusanu abatatu, wabatobela mane kusikila ku-Dani. Lino ciindi camasiku																									
bakalipambukanya tukamu tukamu akubalwisya, walo abalanda bakwe, babauma, babatobela																									
mane kusikila ku-Hoba uuli kulubazu lwalumwesi lwaDamasko. Nkabela wakaboozya																									
imbono zyoonse, alakwe Loti munyina wakamuboozya ambono zyakwe abanakazi abantu boonse.
