Aalo malende wakaaulika izina lya-Mizipa, nkaambo wakati, Jehova alange akati kangu ayebo netunoozooandeene.																									
Na wapenzya bana bangu basimbi, nanka kukwata banakazi abamwi atala abana bangu,																									
nekuba kuti taakwe muntu uuli aswebo, bona! Leza ngukamboni akati kesu.																									
Mpawo Labani wakaambila Jakobo kuti, Bona citantaala eci amalende aya ngendabika akati kesu.																									
Citantaala eci ngukamboni, aalo malende ngukamboni, wakuti mebo ncobeni nsikooyooinda																									
kucitantaala eci kuza kulinduwe, ayebo tokooyooinda kucitantaala eci kuza kulindime, kuzoocita bubi.																									
Leza wa-Abrahamu, a-Leza wa-Nahori, Leza wawisaabo, abeteke akati kesu.																									
Elyo Jakobo wakakonkezya muzina lya-Mulemu wa-Izaka wisi.																									
Nkabela Jakobo wakatuula cipaizyo mpoonya awo acilundu, waita babunyina kuzoolya insima. Bamane kulya insima, bakoona awo acilundu.																									
Nibwakaca, Labani wakafuma, wamyonta bana bakwe balombe abasimbi, wabalongezya, wanyamuka, wapiluka kulinguwe.																									
Alakwe Jakobo wakacili kuya butola lweendo lwakwe, nkabela baangelo ba-Leza bakaswanana awe.																									
Ababone buyo, Jakobo wakati, Njeeyi impi ya-Leza. Aboobo kuntu oko wakakuulika izina lya-Mahanaimu.																									
Jakobo mbwaakalibamba kuswanaana a-Esau.																									
Lino Jakobo wakatuma batumwa kuti bamuzulwide kuyooswanaana a-Esau mukulana wakwe munyika ya-Seiri, cisi ca-Edomu.																									
Nkabela wakabalailila kuti, Mbuboobu mbumweelede kwaambila Esau simalelaangu.																									
Mbuboobu mbwaamba mulanda wako Jakobo. Ndakakala-kala kuliLabani. Nkondakabede akusikila sunu.																									
Ndijisi iŋombe, imbongolo, imbelele, balanda abalanda basimbi. Lino ndatuma kukulwiida mupati wangu kuti nkafwidwe luzyalo kulinguwe.																									
Elyo batumwa bakaboola kuli-Jakobo, bati, Twakasika kumukulana wako Esau.																									
Lino uleza kuzookuswanaana, uli abantu bali myanda yone. Mpawo Jakobo wakayoowa loko akupenga.																									
Nkabela bantu mbaakali abo, ambelele aŋombe ankamele zyoonse, wakababamba mumakoka obile,																									
Esau wasika kukoka lyomwe akulilwisya ikoka lisyeede liyoofutuka.																									
Lino Jakobo wakati, O Leza wa-Abrahamu taata, Leza wa-Izaka taata, Jehova iwakandaambila kuti,																									
Bweeda kunyika yako akumukowa wako nkabela njookubamba kabotu,																									
mebo nsielede abuniini milimo yako yaluzyalo ayalusyomo njowandicitila ndemulanda wako.																									
Nkaambo ndazubuka oyu Jordano amufunko wangu buyo, lino sunu ndaba makoka obile.																									
Wence kondivuna kuzwa kumaanza aamukulana wangu, kuzwa kumaanza aa-Esau, nkaambo ndamuyoowa.																									
Ndayoowa kuti ambweni uleza kutuuma abana abamanyina babo boonse.																									
Pele webo wakaamba kuti, Ncobeni njookubamba kabotu akuvuzya lunyungu lwako lube																									
mbuli musenga wakunkomwe yalwizi uutabaliki nkaambo kakuvula kwawo.																									
Elyo wakoona mpoonya awo masiku ayo, nkabela wakabweza zimwi zyambono nzyaakali azyo zibe cipo cakupa Esau munyina.																									
Wakabweza impongo zili myanda yobile abagutu bali makumi obile, imbelele zili myanda yobile abasijembwe bali makumi obile,																									
inkamele zinyonsya zili makumi otatwe abana bazyo, impwizi zili makumi one abacende bali ikumi, imbongolo impwizi zili makumi obile ambongolo incende zili ikumi,																									
elyo ezi zyoonse wakazibika mumaanza aabalanda bakwe, itanga limwi alimwi alilike,																									
nkabela wakaambila balanda bakwe kuti, Amuzulule kunembo lyangu, alimwi amutalamukane itanga limwi atanganyina.																									
Nkabela wakalailila sitanga mutaanzi kuti, Akuswana Esau mukulana wangu, akubuzya kuti, Uli wani? Uya kuli? Azeezi nzojisi nzizyani?																									
Uleelede kwaamba kuti, Nzyamulanda wako Jakobo. Ncipo catumwa kuli-Esau simalelaangu. Alakwe mwali musule.																									
Awabili awatatu abasimatanga bakali musule, boonse buyo wakabalailila kuti, Mbuboobu mbumweelede kwaambila Esau, mwamujana.																									
Alimwi kamwaamba kuti, Alakwe Jakobo mulanda wako mwali musule. Nkaambo wakali kuyeeya kuti, Nkamutontozye acipo eci ncendatuma.																									
Musule aceeci tuyoobonana kubusyu. Ambweni ulanditambula.																									
Aboobo cipo cakatumwa kunembo, pele walo mwini wakoona masiku ayo mpoonya awo amalabba,																									
Jakobo mbwaakasinana a-Leza																									
Lino masiku ayo ngaonya wakanyampuka, wabweza banakazi bakwe bobile abalanda bakwe																									
basimbi bobile abana bakwe bali ikumi aumwi, wazubuka kucito ca-Jaboki.																									
Wakabatola, wabazubusya kalonga, azyalo zintu zyoonse nzyaakali azyo.																									
Elyo Jakobo wakasyaala alike, nkabela kwakeza muntu kuzoosinana awe masiku oonse mane kubucedo.																									
Nkabela naakabona kuti tamuzundi, wakaampa intelebelo yacibelo cakwe, aboobo intelebelo yacibelo ca-Jakobo yakakwiduka mukusinana kwabo.																									
Elyo wakati, Undileke njiinke, nkaambo bwaamba kuca. Pele wakavuwa kuti, Nsikookuleka pe, cita utaangune kundilongezya.																									
Wakamubuzya kuti, Nduweni izina lyako? Wakati, Ndime Jakobo.																									
Wakati, Izina lyako talikooyooambwa limbi kuti nduwe Jakobo, pe, izina lyako liyooba Israyeli, nkaambo wazundana a-Leza abantu, alimwi wazunda.																									
Mpawo Jakobo wakamubuzya kuti, Wence undilwiide izina lyako. Wakati, Ino nkaambonzi wabuzya izina lyangu?																									
Elyo wakamulongezya mpoonya awo. Elyo Jakobo wakaulika oko kuntu izina lya-Penueli, nkaambo wakati,																									
Ndabona Leza busyu kubusyu, nekubaboobo buumi bwangu mpobucili.																									
Lino izuba lyakapasula naakazubuka ku-Penueli, nkabela wakali kuya busunkuta nkaambo kacibelo cakwe.																									
Nciceeco bana ba-Israyeli ncibatalidi mulambi wakasolo uubambene antelebelo yacibelo mane kusikila sunu,																									
nkaambo kakuti wakaampa intelebelo yacibelo ca-Jakobo kumulambi wakasolo.																									
Jakobo mbwaakaswanaana a-Esau. Lino Jakobo wakatambya meso aakwe,																									
wabona kuti Esau uleza abantu bali myanda yone. Abone obo, wakapambukanya bana a-Leya a-Rakele abalanda basimbi bobile.																									
Nkabela balanda basimbi abana babo wakababika kunembo, musule lyabo wakabika Leya abana bakwe, musule lyabaabo wakabika Rakele a-Josefa.																									
Lino walo mwini wakainda kunembo, wakali kuya bukotama ansi ziindi zili musanu azibili mane wakasika kumukulana wakwe.																									
Pele Esau wakazuzaana kukumuswanganya, wamukumbata, wawida ansingo yakwe, wamumyonta. Nkabela balila.																									
Lino Esau naakatambya meso aakwe, wakabona banakazi abana, nkabela wakabuzya kuti, Ino mbobani aba mboli abo?																									
Wakavuwa kuti, Mbaaba bana Leza siluzyalo mbaakapa mulanda wako.																									
Mpawo balanda basimbi abana babo bakaswena afwaafwi, bakotama.																									
Alakwe Leya wakaswena abana bakwe, bakotama. Kumanizya, bakaswena Josefa a-Rakele, bakotama.																									
Elyo Esau wakabuzya kuti, Nkokutyeni aya makamu makamu ngendakaswana? Wakavuwa kuti, Nkokujana buuya mumeso aamwami wangu.																									
Esau wakuti, Ndijisi kale zinji, mwanike; kolibambila nzojisi.																									
Pele Jakobo wakati, Akaka! Na ndijene luzyalo mumeso aako, wence tambula cipo cizwa kumaanza aangu,																									
nkaambo kubona busyu bwako kuli mbubonya mbuli kubona busyu bwa-Leza. Wanditambula kabotu.																									
Wence tambula cilumbyo cangu ncowaletelwa, nkaambo Leza wandifwida luzyalo, alimwi ndijisi zinji. Aboobo wakamukombelezya mane wakatambula.																									
Mpawo Esau wakati, Atweende, ndakuzulwida. Pele wakamuvwiila kuti, Mwami wangu ulizi																									
kuti bana mbaniini, alimwi ndijisi imbelele atjombe zinyonsya, Na bazibingisya buzuba bomwe, imbelele zyoonse zilafwa.																									
Mwami wangu aye kunembo lyamulanda wakwe, Mebo nooza bweenda kabotu kabotu,																									
mbuli mbuzikonzya kweenda iŋombe, ambuli mbubakonzya kweenda bana, mane nkasike kumwami wangu ku-Seiri.																									
Lino Esau wakati, Nkusiile bamwi babantu mbondi abo, Pele wakati, Nkaambonzi? Nkajane buuya mumeso aasimalelaangu.																									
Mpawo Esau wakanyampuka mubuzuba obo mbubonya kuti apiluke ku-Seiri.																									
Pele Jakobo wakaya ku-Sukoti, waakuliyakila iŋanda. Azyalo iŋombe zyakwe wakaziyakila zibaya. Nciceeco oku kuntu ncikuulikidwe izina lya-Sukoti.																									
Nkabela Jakobo wakasika kabotu kumuni wa-Sekemu munyika yaKanana, naakazwa ku-Padanaramu. Wakayaka zilao zyakwe kunembo lyamunzi.																									
Nkabela cipanzi canyika mpaakayakide zilao zyakwe wakacuula kubana ba-Hamori wisi Sekemu. Wakaula amali aakesita aali mwanda.																									
Elyo wakayaka cipaililo mpoonya awo, wacuulika izina lyaElelohe-Israyeli. Sekemu mbwaakabisizya Dina																									
Lino Dina, mwana musimbi wa-Leya ngwaakazyalila Jakobo, wakaya kuswaya-swaya kubanakazi bacisi eco.																									
Nkabela Sekemu mwana wa-Hamori mu-Hiti mwami wacisi, naakamubona, wakamutizya, woona awe, wamubisizya.																									
Moyo wakwe wakasukama Dina mwana musimbi wa-Jakobo nkabela wakayandisya musimbi akumwaambila cakumoongelezya.																									
Elyo Sekemu wakaambila Hamori wisi kuti, Kondeendela oyo musimbi, nkamukwate. 5																									
Lino Jakobo wakamvwa kuti wasofwaazya Dina mwanaakwe musimbi, pele bana bakwe																									
balombe bakali mukweembela iŋombe musokwe, aboobo Jakobo wakaumuna buyo mane bakasika.																									
Nkabela Hamori wisi Sekemu wakainka kuli-Jakobo kuyooambaula awe.																									
Abalo bana balombe ba-Jakobo, nibakamvwa makani, bakaboola kuzwa musokwe,																									
nkabela abo basankwa bakabijilwa akukalala loko nkaambo kabufubafuba obo																									
mbwaakacitide mumukowa wa-Israyeli mukulalika mwana musimbi waJakobo, nkaambo cilatondwa kucita obo.																									
Pele Hamori wakabaambila kuti, Moyo wa-Sekemu mwanaangu ulisukeme mwanaanu musimbi. Wence mumupe nguwe, amukwate.																									
Alimwi atutangane buzwalani bwalukwatano, kuti mutupe bana banu basimbi, anywebo mutole bana besu basimbi.																									
Lino amukale kulindiswe; nyika yoonse iyoomujalukila, kuti mukale, musambale, mube ambono mulinjiyo.																									
Alakwe Sekemu wakaambila wisi musimbi abakulana bakwe kuti, Mfwidwe buuya kulindinywe, elyo kufumbwa ncomwaamba ndamupa ncico.																									
Amwaambe luselo lunji azipo zinji mbubonya mbuli mbumuyanda, njoomupa ncomwaamba, pele amundipe musimbi, mukwate.																									
Mpoonya awo bana ba-Jakobo bakavwiila Sekemu a-Hamori wisi cakweena, nkaambo kakuti wakasofwaazya mucizi wabo Dina.																									
Bakabaambila kuti, Tatukonzyi kucita obo pe. Tatukonzyi kupa mucizi wesu kuti akwatwe kumwaalumi uutapalwidwe, nkaambo kucita obo kulatuusya bweeme.																									
Tatukonzyi kumuzuminina cita mutaangune kucita cintu comwe, Muleelede kuba mbubonya mbuli ndiswe, nkukuti baalumi boonse akati kanu baleelede kupalulwa.																									
Na mwazumina obo, tulamupa bana besu basimbi akukwata bana banu basimbi, alimwi tulakala antoomwe, tube musyobo omwe.																									
Pele na mwakaka kutuswiilila, na mwakaka kupalulwa, tulatola buyo mwana musimbi wesu, twiinke,																									
Lino majwi aabo akabota mumeso aa-Hamori amumeso aa-Sekemu mwana wa-Hamori.																									
Nkabela mulombe takwaakamuka kucita obo, nkaambo kayandisya mwana musimbi wa-Jakobo.																									
Kali mulemu kwiinda basiŋanda boonse bawisi. Aboobo Hamori amwanaakwe Sekemu bakasika kumulyango wamunzi wabo, bakaambila bantu bamumunzi wabo kuti,																									
Aba bantu mbasiluumuno; bakale omuno munyika akusambala mumonya, nkaambo nyika nimpati, ilazulila;																									
bakwate bana besu basimbi, aswebo tubape bana besu basimbi.																									
Nekubaboobo bantu tabakonzyi kuzumina kukala aswebo akuba musyobo omwe, cita																									
tuzumine kucita cintu comwe, nkukuti tuleelede kuzumina kuti baalumi boonse akati kesu bapalulwe, mbubonya mbuli mbubapalwidwe balo.																									
Iŋombe zyabo ambono zyabo abanyama babo, sa zyoonse buyo tazikooyooba zyesu? Atuzumine, lino balakala aswebo.																									
Mpoonya awo boonse ibakali kunjila mumulyango wamunzi wakwe bakaswiilila Hamori a-Sekemu mwanaakwe.																									
Baalumi boonse bakapalulwa, boonse buyo ibakali kunjila mumulyango wamunzi wakwe.																									
Lino buzuba bwatatu nibwakaca, nibakali kuciswa, bana bobile baJakobo, nkukuti Simeoni a-Levi bakulana ba-Dina,																									
bakatola umwi aumwi ipanga lyakwe, boongomokela munzi, bajaya baalumi boonse.																									
Alakwe Hamori amwanaakwe Sekemu, boonse bakabajaya apanga, elyo bakagwisya Dina muŋanda ya-Sekemu, bamutola.																									
Bana ba-Jakobo bakasika kuli bajayidwe, akusaala munzi, nkaambo kakuti mucizi wabo kasofwaazidwe.																									
Bakatola imbelele zyabo aŋombe zyabo ambongolo zyabo, azintu zyoonse zyamumunzi azyamumyuunda,																									
imbono zyabo zyoonse, atwana twabo toonse abanakazi babo boonse, zyoonse buyo zyamuŋanda bakazisaala akuzitola.																									
Mpawo Jakobo wakaambila Simeoni a-Levi kuti, Mwandifwabya, nkaambo mwandinunsya akati kabantu bakede munyika, ba-Kanana aba-Perizi, Mebo, tuli bace buyo.																									
Balayoboloka akundilwisya, lino njoonyonyooka, mebo aluzubo lwangu.																									
Pele bakati, Sa uleelede kucitila mucizi wesu mbuli sibwaamu mbwacitilwa?																									
Jakobo mbwaakayaka cipaililo caku-Beteli. Lino Leza wakaambila Jakobo kuti,																									
Nyampuka, uye ku-Beteli, ukale nkuko, uyake cipaililo ca-Leza oyo nguwenya iwakalibonya kulinduwe ciindi eciya nowakacija kubusyu bwa-Esau mukulana wako.																									
Mpawo Jakobo wakaambila luzubo lwakwe aboonse mbaakali abo kuti, Amusowe baleza beenzu bali akati kanu, alimwi amulisalazye akuvundununa zyakusama zyanu.																									
Atunyamuke, tuye ku-Beteli, nkayake cipaililo, cibe ca-Leza oyo iwakandivuwa mubuzuba bwamafwabi aangu, iwakandisindikila mukweenda kwangu koonse.																									
Mpawo bakapa Jakobo baleza beenzu boonse ibakali mumaanza aabo amacoco aamumatwi aabo, nkabela Jakobo wakazisisa kunsi lyamubanga waku-Sekemu.																									
Elyo mukweenda kwabo, buyoofu buzwa kuli-Leza bwakajata minzi iyakeengelede, aboobo teebakatobela bana ba-Jakobo.																									
Lino Jakobo wakasika ku-Luzi (ngonguwo Beteli) munyika ya-Kanana, walo abantu boonse mbaakali abo.																									
Nkabela wakayaka cipaililo mpoonya awo, waulika kuntu oko izina lya-El Beteli, nkaambo																									
kakuti nkukonya oko Leza nkwaakamubonekela ciindi eco naakacija kubusyu bwamukulana wakwe.																									
Lino Debora muleli wa-Rebeka wakafwa, nkabela wakazikwa kunsi lyamubanga oko ku-Beteli, aboobo oyo musamu wakaulikwa izina lya-Aloni-Bakuti.																									
Lino Leza wakabonekela Jakobo alimwi naakamana kuzwa ku-Padanaramu, wamulongezya.																									
Nkabela Leza wakamwaambila kuti, Izina lyako nduwe Jakobo, pele tokooyooambwa limbi kuti nduwe Jakobo pe, izina lyako liyooba Israyeli.																									
Mbuboobo mbwaakaulikwa izina lya-Israyeli. Alimwi Leza wakamwaambila kuti,																									
Ndime Leza Singuzuzyoonse, Zyalisya, ukavule; mulinduwe mulazwa musyobo ankamu yamisyobo, amucikungu cako muyoozwa bami.																									
Alimwi nyika eyo njindakapa Abrahamu a-Izaka, ndaipa nduwe, alwalo lunyungu lwako luciza njoolupa nyika eyo.																									
Mpawo Leza wakapiluka kujulu, wamusia nkukonya oko nkwaakaambaula awe.																									
Nkabela Jakobo wakaimika malende, nkokuti malende aamabwe, nkukonya oko nkwaakaambaula awe,																									
Nkabela wakatila cipaizyo cakunywa alingawo, alimwi wakatila insazi yamafuta.																									
Mbuboobo Jakobo mbwaakaulika oko kuntu Leza nkwaakaambaula awe izina lya-Beteli.																									
Rakele mbwaakafwa naakazyala Benjamini. Elyo bakalonga kuzwa ku-Beteli,																									
nkabela nekwakacisyeede kasinzo kusika ku-Efrata, Rakele wakatumbuka, pele wakapenga mukutumbuka kwakwe.																									
Lino naakacili kusunda mukutumbuka kwakwe, sikumutumbusya wakamwambila kuti, Utayoowi, nkaambo sunu ulazyala mwana mulombe aumwi.																									
Nkabela muuya wakwe nowakaamba kumusia (nkaambo wakafwa) wakamuulika izina lya-Benoni, pele wisi wakamuulika izina lya-Benjamini.																									
Aboobo Rakele wakafwa, nkabela wakazikwa munzila yaku-Efrata (ngonguwo Betelehemu).																									
Lino Jakobo wakaimikizya malende atala lyakabanda kakwe. Ngengao malende aakabanda ka-Rakele mbwaacibede asunu.																									
Amwi makani aa-Jakobo abana bakwe, Izaka mbwaakafwa																									
Lino Israyeli wakalonga, waakuyaka cilao cakwe kunembo lyaŋanda indamfu ya-Ederi.																									
Nkabela Israyeli naakacikede mucisi eco, Rubeni wakalala a-Biliha simamambe wawisi, nkabela Israyeli wakamvwa makani.																									
Lino bana ba-Jakobo bakali ikumi ababili. 23Bana ba-Leya mbaaba: Rubeni (mwana mutaanzi wa-Jakobo),																									
Abana ba-Biliha mulanda musimbi wa-Rakele mbaaba: Dani a-Nafitali.																									
Abana ba-Zilipa mulanda musimbi wa-Leya mbaaba: Gadi a-Aseri, Mbaabo bana ba-Jakobo mbaakazyala ku-Padanaramu.																									
Mpawo Jakobo wakasika kuli-Izaka wisi ku-Mamre, ku-Kiriyati-ariba (ngonguwo Hebroni), Abrahamu a-Izaka nkubakali kukala-kala.																									
Nkabela mazuba aabuumi bwa-Izaka akasika kumwanda amakumi aali musanu aatatu.																									
Elyo Izaka wakazanga, wafwa, wainka kulibasinsiku bakwe naakacembaala Bucembele buzwide, nkabela Esau a-Jakobo bana bakwe bakamuzika.																									
Misukulu ya-Esau. Lino njeeyi mizukulu ya-Esau, ngonguwe Edomu.																									
Esau wakakwata banakazi bamucisi ca-Kanana, Ada mwana musimbi wa-Eloni mu­ Hiti, a-Aholibama mwana musimbi wa-Ana mwana wa-Zibeoni mu-Hivi,																									
a-Basemati mwana musimbi wa-Ismayeli mucizi wa-Nebayoti.																									
Nkabela Ada wakazyalila Esau Elifazi, alakwe Basemati wakazyala Reueli,																									
alakwe Aholibama wakazyala Jeusi a-Jalamu a-Kora, Mbaabo bana ba-Esau mbaakazyala munyika ya-Kanana.																									
Esau wakatola banakazi bakwe, bana bakwe balombe, bana bakwe basimbi, abasiŋanda bakwe boonse,																									
aŋombe zyakwe amatanga aakwe, aŋombe zyakwe zyoonse nzyaakavubide munyika ya-Kanana,																									
wakalongela kunyika imbi cakwaanzaana amwanike wakwe Jakebo.																									
Nkaambo imbono zyabo zyakavula, aboobo bakakacilwa kukala amwe. Nyika yabweenzu bwabo yakakacilwa kubalela nkaambo kaŋombe zyabo.																									
Aboobo Esau wakaakukala munyika yazilundu zya-Seiri, Esau ngonguwe Edomu.																									
Njeeyi mizukulu ya-Esau wisi waba-Edomu bakuzilundu zya-Seiri.																									
Josefa mbwaakaba muzike mucisi ca-Egepita. Lino Jakobo kakede munyika yabweenzu bwabamawisi,																									
nkokuti munyika ya-Kanana. Ngaaya makani aamazyalani aa-Jakobo, Josefa naakajisi myaka iili ikumi amusani aibili, wakali kweembela imbelele abakulana bakwe,																									
Kali mulombe antoomwe abana ba-Biliha abana baZilipa banakazi bawisi, nkabela Josefa wakaletela wisi makani aabo mabi.																									
Israyeli kayandisya Josefa kwiinda bana bakwe boonse nkaambo kali mwana wabucembele bwakwe, nkabela wakamucitila ijansi lili amaboko.																									
Pele bakulana bakwe, nebakabona kuti wisi ulamuyandisya kwiinda beenzinyina, bakamusula, kabataamba caluumuno kulinguwe.																									
Lino Josefa wakalota ciloto, walwiida bakulana bakwe, nkabela bakaindilila kumusula.																									
Wakabaambila kuti, Amuswiilile eci ciloto ncindalota. Ndakabona kuti twakali kwaanga																									
misunta yamaila mukati kamuunda, elyo musunta wangu wakabuka, waimikila, amisunta yanu yakuuzyunguluka, yaukotamina.																									
Mpawo bakulana bakwe bakamwaambila kuti, Ma! Sa uyooba mwami wesu? Sa uyootweendelezya swebo?																									
Nkabela bakaindilila loko kumusula nkaambo kaziloto zyakwe amajwi aakwe.																									
Mpoonya awo wakalota ciloto acimwi, walwiida bakulana bakwe, wati, Amuswiilile!																									
Ndalota cilota acimwi. Ndalota kuti izuba amwezi anyenyeezi zili ikumi aimwi zyoonse zyandikotamina.																									
Wakalwiida wisi abakulana bakwe, nkabela wisi wakamutapatila, wati, Ma! Ncilotonzi eci ncowalota?																									
Sa ncobeni tuzoosika, mebo abanyoko abakulana bako, kukukotama ansi kunembo lyako?																									
Lino bakulana bakwe bakali kumufwida ibbivwe, pele wisi wakajata majwi mumoyo wakwe.																									
Lino baku la na bakwe bakainka kuyooembela imbelele zyawisaabo ku-Sekemu.																									
Nkabela Israyeli wakaambila Josefa kuti, Bona! Sa bakulana bako tabali mukweembela ku-Sekemu?																									
Koza, nkutume kulimbabo. Wakavuwa kuti, Ndaya. Wakamwaambila kuti, Mbubo, koya,																									
ukabone bakulana bako na bali kabotu, azyalo imbelele na zili kabotu, uzoondaambile makani,																									
Aboobo wakamutuma kuzwa kukuti lya-Hebroni, nkabela wakasika ku-Sekemu.																									
Lino umwi muntu wakamujana ulaingaila musokwe, nkabela oyo muntu wakamubuzya kuti, Uyandaulanzi?																									
Wakavuwa kuti, Ndayandaula bakulana bangu, Wence undaambile na baleembelelai?																									
Wakati, Bazwa okuno, nkaambo ndakamvwa majwi aabo aakuti, Katuya ku-Dotani. Amvwe obo Josefa wakatobela bakulana bakwe, wabajana ku-Dotani.																									
Pele naakacili kule, bakamubona, nkabela naatakaina kusika, bakamuvwiya kuti bamujaye.																									
Bakaambilana umwi aumwi kumweenzinyina kuti, Ngooyo siziloto wasika.																									
Atweende, tumujaye, tumuwaale muli limwi lyamalindi, lino tulaamba kuti, Cinyama cibi camujaya. Tulabona na ziloto zyakwe zilaba buti.																									
Pele Rubeni naakamvwa, wakamuvuna mumaanza aabo, wati, Tutamujayi pe.																									
Rubeni wakabaambila kuti, Mutatili bulowa pe; amumutumpukisye omo mudindi elyo lyamubbuwa,																									
pele mutamubikili maanza aanu, Wakaamba obo kuti amuvune kumaanza aabo akumupilusya kuliwisi.																									
Elyo Josefa naakasika kufwaafwi kubakulana bakwe, bakamusamununa ijansi lyakwe, ijansi idamfu lili amaboko ndyaakasamide,																									
elyo bakamujata, bamutumpukizya mudindi. Idindi lyakali maya, kamutakwe maanzi mulindilyo.																									
Lino bakakala kulya insima, nkabela nibakatambya meso aabo bakabona inkamu yabasinyenda ba-Ismayeli balazwa ku-Gileadi,																									
bali ankamele zyabo ziyumwide zilisyo amisamu atununkilizyo, balaya kuzisambala ku-Egepita.																									
Mpawo Juda wakaambila beenzinyina kuti, Cilatugwasyanzi na twajaya mwanike wesu akuvumba bulowa bwakwe?																									
Atweende, tumusambale kuba-Ismayeli, pele tutamutambiki maanza esu, nkaambo ngumwanike wesu, ninyama yesu, Nkabela beenzinyina bakamuswiilila.																									
Elyo basambazi ba-Midyani nibakainda, bakagwisya Josefa kuzwa mudindi,																									
bamuulisya kuba-Ismayeli mali aansiliva aali makumi obile, aboobo bakasisya Josefa ku-Egepita.																									
Mpawo Rubeni naakaboola kudindi akujana kuti Josefa tacimo, wakadeluula zyakusama zyakwe,																									
wapiluka kubeenzinyina, wati, Mwana taciwo. Lino mebo, njiinke kuli?																									
Elyo bakabweza ijansi lya-Josefa, bajaya mujembwe wampongo, bajovweka ijansi mubulowa.																									
Nkabela bakatuma ijansi lili amaboko kuliwisaabo, bati, Twajana eci. Langa, ubone na ndendilyo ijansi lyamwanaako na pe.																									
Mpoonya awo wakaliziba, wati, Ndejansi lyamwanaangu. Cinyama cibi camulya. Ncobeni Josefa wadeIuulwa.																									
Lino Jakobo wakadeluula zyakusama zyakwe, wasama zisani zyamasaka mucikungu cakwe, walila mwanaakwe mazuba manji.																									
Nkabela bana bakwe balombe abana bakwe basimbi boonse bakabuka kuti bamuumbulizye, pele wakakaka kuumbulizigwa.																									
Wakati, Ncobeni njooselukila mukabanda mwaabede mwanaangu cakulila. Mbuboobo wisi mbwaakamulila.																									
Pele ba-Midyani bakamuulisya mu-Egepita, Bakamuulisya kuli-Potifara, umwi wabasilutwe wa-Farao, sikulanga wabasikutabilila.																									
Makani aa-Tamara. Mbwaakazyala Perezi a-Zera. Lino kuciindi eco Juda wakazwa kubakulana bakwe,																									
waakuswaya umwi muntu waku-Adulamu, izina lyakwe kali Hira.																									
Nkabela nkukonya oko Juda wakabona musimbi mwana wa-Suwa umwi muntu mu-Kanana, elyo wakamukwata, waswanaana awe.																									
Lino wakaminta, wazyala mwana mulombe, wamuulika izina lya-Eri.																									
Wakaminta alimwi, wazyala mwana mulombe, wamuulika izina lya-Onani.																									
Alimwi lwatatu wakazyala mwana mulombe, wamuulika izina lya-Sela. Kali ku-Kezibi naakamuzyala.																									
Nkabela Juda wakajanina Eri mwanaakwe mutaanzi mwanakazi, izina lyakwe kali Tamara.																									
Pele Eri mwana mutaanzi wa-Juda, kali mubi mumeso aa-Jehova, aboobo Jehova wakamujaya.																									
Mpawo Juda wakaambila Onani kuti, Unjilile mwanakazi wamukulana wako, ucite mbweelede mulamu wako, ukabusizye mukulana wako lunyungu.																									
Pele Onani wakaziba kuti lunyungu talukooyooba lwakwe, aboobo naakaswanaana amukamukulana wakwe wakasowela anyika kuti atapi mukulana wakwe lunyungu.																									
Lino eco ncaakacita cakabija mumeso aa-Jehova, aboobo wakamujaya alakwe.																									
Elyo Juda wakaambila Tamara mukamwana wakwe kuti, Kosyaala mbuli nabutema muŋanda yauso mane mwanaangu Sela akomene.																									
Nkaambo wakali kuyeeya kuti, Ambweni ulafwa alakwe mbubonya mbuli bakulana bakwe.																									
Aboobo Tamara wakainka kuyookala muŋanda yawisi,																									
Lino necakaba ciindi, mwana wa-Suwa (ngonguwe muka-Juda) wakafwa.																									
Nkabela Juda, naakaleka kulila, wakainka ku-Timna, nkobakali kuyunda imbelele zyakwe, antoomwe amuzwalani wakwe Hira mu-Adulamu.																									
Elyo Tamara wakalwiidwa kuti, Bona, usozyala wainka ku-Timna kuyooyunda imbelele zyakwe.																									
Amvwe obo, wakasamununa zyakusama zyabunabutema bwakwe, waliputilila intambala kubusyu bwakwe, walyeenyeenya,																									
waakukala kumulyango waku-Enaimu munzila iiya ku-Timna, Nkaambo wakabona kuti Sela wakomena kale, nekubaboobo tana kumupegwa kuti amukwate.																									
Lino Juda naakabona, wakayeeya kuti ngusimamambe, nkaambo kavumbide busyu bwakwe.																									
Mpawo wakaleya munzila mwaakabede, wamwaambila kuti, Wence tuswanaane ayebo,																									
Nkaambo takwakaziba kuti ngumukamwana wakwe. Wakati, Ulandipanzi kuti uswanaane ambebo?																									
Wakavuwa kuti, Ndakutumina mwana wampongo kuzwa kutanga, Wakati, Sa tokonzyi																									
kundipa citondezyo calusyomo mane ukatume? 18Wakabuzya kuti, Nkupe citondezyonzi?																									
Wakati, Kondipa cinamatizyo cako antambo yako amusako uuli mujanza lyako.																									
Wakamupa, waswanaana awe, nkabela wakaminta kuzwa kulinguwe.																									
Lino wakanyampuka, waya kulinguwe, wasamununa intambala njakasamide, wasama zyakusama zyabunabutema bwakwe,																									
Lino Juda wakatuma mwana wampongo kujanza lyamuzwalani wakwe mu-Adulamu,																									
kuti aboozye citondezyo kuzwa kumaanza aamwanakazi, pele takwe naakamujana pe. Nkabela wakabuzya bantu bakooko kuti, Uli kuli simamambe iwakali kumbali anzila ku-Enaimu? Bakavuwa kuti, Katakwe simamambe okuno pe.																									
Mpawo wakapiluka kuli-Juda, wati, Nsikwe kumujana pe. Abalo bantu bakooko bakati, Katakwe simamambe okuno.																									
Lino Juda wakati, Atole biyo zintu, kuti tutasekwi. Wabona kuti ndalitumide oyu mwana wampongo, pele tokwe kumujana.																									
Lino ciindi cili mbuli myezi yotatwe necakamana, Juda wakalwiidwa kuti, Bona! Tamara mukamwana wako wacita bwaamu, wamintila mubwaamu,																									
Mpawo Juda wakaamba kuti, Amumugwisye, aumpwe. Pele naakali mukugwisigwa,																									
wakatumina wisizyala mulazyo wakuti, Muntu uuli azintu ezi nguwakandiminsya.																									
Alimwi wakati, Bona, uzibe na nzizyani zintu ezi-cinamatizyo antambo amusako.																									
Mpawo Juda wakaziziba, wati, Uliluleme kwiinda ndime, nkaambo ndakabula kumupa Sela mwanaangu. Elyo takwe naakaindulula kumuziba.																									
Lino ciindi cakwe cakutumbuka necakasika, mwakajanwa mayanga muzyalilo lyakwe.																									
Nkabela mukuzyala kwakwe umwi mwana wakazuluzya ijanza lyakwe, Lino sikutumbusya wakajata ijanza lyakwe,																									
walyaanga akatambo kasalala pyu, wati, Ngooyu mutaanzi kuzyalwa.																									
Pele naakapilusya ijanza lyakwe, mweenzinyina wakazwa. Elyo wakati, Ma! Wapola buti yebo? Nciceeco izina lyakwe ncaakaulikwa kuti ngu-Perezi.																									
Musule lyakwe mwakazyalwa mweenzinyina iwakajisi katambo kasalala ajanza lyakwe, nkabela wakaulikwa izina lya-Zera.																									
Josefa mbwaakabeleka kuli-Potifara. Lino Josefa wakatolwa ku-Egepita,																									
nkabela Potifara, umwi wabasilutwe ba-Farao, sikulanga wabasikutabilila, muntu mu-Egepita, wakamuula kuzwa kumaanza aaba-Ismayeli ibakamuletede nkuko.																									
Lino Jehova wakali a-Josefa, aboobo wakajana coolwe muŋanda yasimalelo wakwe mu-Egepita.																									
Nkabela simalelo wakwe wakabona kuti Jehova uli awe, alimwi zyoonse nzyaakali kucita Jehova wakazikondezya mujanza lyakwe.																									
Elyo Josefa wakafwidwa buuya mumeso aakwe. Wakamumanina milimo,																									
wakamubika kuti abe mupati waŋanda yakwe, azyoonse zintu nzyaakajisi wakazyaaba mumaanza aakwe.																									
Lino kuzwa kuciindi eco naakamubika kuti abe silutwe waŋanda yakwe, awazintu zyoonse nzyaakajisi,																									
Jehova wakalongezya iŋanda yamu-Egepita nkaambo ka-Josefa, Lulongezyo lwaJehova lwakalikede ambono zyakwe zyoonse, neziba zyamuŋanda neziba zyamumuunda.																									
Nkabela zyoonse biyo nzyakajisi wakazisia mumaanza aa-Josefa. Walo mwini takwakaziba cintu neciba comwe ncaakali aco cita insima njaakali kulya.																									
Josefa mbwaakabikwa muntotongo. Lino Josefa kali aciwa cibotu, keebeka loko.																									
Nkabela kusule lyayaaya, mukasimalelo wakwe wakavundula meso aakwe kuli-Josefa, wati, Atweende ayebo.																									
Pele wakakaka. Wakaambila mukasimalelo wakwe kuti, Bona! Simalelaangu talikataazyi																									
kucintu neciba comwe muŋanda; zyoonse buyo nzyaajisi wazyaaba mumaanza aangu.																									
Taakwe mupati kwiinda ndime muŋanda ino. Tana kundikasizye cintu neciba comwe, cita nduwe luzutu nkaambo uli banakwe. Nkacite buti bubi bupati buli boobu akubisizya Leza?																									
Nkabela mazuba oonse, nekuba kuti wakacili kwaambila Josefa, taakwe naakazumina abuniini koona awe nanka kuba awe.																									
Pele buzuba bumwi naakanjila muŋanda kukubeleka milimo yakwe, katakwe naba omwe wabasiŋanda bamwi omo muŋanda,																									
nkabela wakajata cikobela cakwe, wati, Atulale ayebo. Mpawo wakasia cikobela cakwe mujanza lyakwe, wacija, waya anze.																									
Abone buyo kuti wasia cikobela cakwe mujanza lyakwe, wacija, waya anze,																									
wakaita basiŋanda bakwe, wabaambila kuti, Amubone! Watuletela mu-Hebrayo kuti atusampaule.																									
Weza kulindime kuti alale ambebo, elyo ndalila ajwi ipati. Amvwe kuti ndongololesya akulila, wasia cikobela cakwe kulindime, wacija, waya anze.																									
Mpawo wakabamba cikobela cakwe kulinguwe mane simalelo wakwe asike kuŋanda.																									
Asike, wakamwaambila alakwe mbubonya. Wakati, Mulanda muHebrayo nguwakatuletela weza kulindime kuzoondisabwida.																									
Pele nendoongololesya akulila wasia cikobela cakwe kulindime, wacija, waya anze.																									
Lino simalelo wakwe naakamvwa majwi aamukaakwe ngaakamwaambila aakuti, Mbuboobo mulanda wako mbwandicitila, bukali bwakwe bwakabuka.																									
Mpawo simalelo wa-Josefa wakamujata, wamubika muntolongo, baange bamwami mobakaangidwe, nkabela wakakala mumonya muntolongo.																									
Pele Jehova kali a-Josefa, wamufwida luzyalo, wamupa buuya mumeso aamulangi wantolongo.																									
Nkabela mulangi wantolongo wakabika baange boonse buyo bamuntolongo mumaanza aa-Josefa, aboobo kufumbwa cintu cakacitwa oko, ngonguwe wakali kucicita.																									
Mulangi wantolongo takakali kulikataazya kucita neciba comwe icakali mumaanza aakwe,																									
nkaambo Jehova wakali awe, azintu zyoonse nzyaakacita, Jehova wakazibotezya.																									
Josefa mbwaakapandulwida balanda ba-Farao ziloto																									
Kabe kaindi, sikukutaukila mwami wa-Egepita amujiki wakwe bakabisizya simalelaabo mwami wa-Egepita.																									
Mpawo Farao wakakalalila abo balanda bakwe bobile, simutwe wabakutausi asimutwe wabajisi,																									
wabaanga muŋanda yamulangi wabatabilizi, muntolongo Josefa mwaakaangilidwe­.																									
Lino mulangi wabatabilizi wakababika mumaanza aa-Josefa, kuti abakutaukile, nkabela bakakala mazuba manji muntolongo.																									
Elyo oyo sikukutaukila mwami wa-Egepita amujisi wakwe bakaleta ziloto.																									
Boonse bobile bakalota, umwi aumwi ciloto cakwe, mubusiku bomwe. Ciloto cimwi acimwi kacijisi kupandulula kwaco.																									
Nkabela nebwakaca Josefa wakeza kulimbabo, wajana kuti baluusene.																									
Lino wakabuzya abo basilutwe ba-Farao mbaakali abo balaangidwe muŋanda yasimalelaakwe kuti, Nkaambonzi masyu aanu abija sunu?																									
Bakamuvwiila kuti, Twalota ziloto, alimwi taakwe uukonzya kuzipandulula. Josefa																									
wakabaambila kuti, Sa teensi Leza uukonzya kupandulula! Amundilwiide.																									
Mpoonya awo silutwe wabakutausi wakalwiida Josefa ciloto cakwe. Wakati, Muciloto cangu ndakabona musaansa kunembo lyangu.																									
Mumusaansa kamuli mitabi yotatwe, Usyuuke biyo, wafulula malubaluba, elyo masankinya aamasaansa akabizwa ndilyonya.																									
Alimwi inkomeki ya-Farao yakali mujanza lyangu, nkabela ndakacela masaansa, ndakasinina munkomeki ya-Farao, ndapa mujanza lya-Farao.																									
Lino Josefa wakamwaambila kuti, Mbuboobo mbocipandululwa. Mitabi yotatwe nkokuti mazuba otatwe.																									
Amana mazuba otatwe Farao uyoobusya mutwe wako akukuboozya kumilimo yako,																									
nkabela uyoopa inkomeki mujanza lyakwe mbubonya mbowakali kucita lyoonse nowakacili mukutausi wakwe.																									
Pele kwabota kulinguwe, wence kondiyeeya mebo akundifwida luzyalo, ukaambe makani aangu mumatwi aa-Farao akundigwisya omuno muŋanda.																									
Nkaambo ncobeni ndakabbigwa munyika yaba-Hebrayo, alimwi okuno taakwe ncendakabisya kuti bandi bike muntolongo.																									
Elyo simutwe wabajisi, naakabona kuti ciloto cakapandululwa kabotu, wakaambila Josefa																									
kuti, Ambebo ndalota, Muciloto cangu ndakali azisewe zyotatwe zyazibunge amutwe wangu.																									
Mucisewe caatala kamuli zilyo zyamisyobo misyobo nzyajika mujisi, zyajikilwa Farao. Nkabela bayuni bakali kuzilida, mucisewe cakali atala amutwe wangu.																									
Mpawo Josefa wakavuwa, wati, Mbuboobu mbucipandululwa. Zisewe zyotatwe nkukuti mazuba otatwe.																									
Amana mazuba otatwe, Farao uyookosola mutwe wako akukwaanzika amusamu, elyo bayuni bayoolya nyama yamubili wako,																									
Lino buzuba bwatatu nibwakaca, bwakali buzuba bwakuzyalwa kwa-­Farao, nkabela wakacitila balanda bakwe boonse ipobwe.																									
Mpawo wakabusya mutwe wamukutausi mupati amujisi mupati akati kabalanda bakwe. Mukutausi mupati wakamuboozya mubukutausi bwakwe, aboobo wakapa inkomeki mujanza lya-Farao.																									
Pele mujisi mupati wakamwaanzika, mbubonya mbuli Josefa mbwaakapandulula.																									
Nekubaboobo mukutausi mupati takwakayeeya Josefa pe, wakamuluba buyo.																									
Josefa mbwaakapandulula ziloto zya-Farao. Lino niyakamana myaka yobile iizwide, Farao wakalota.																									
Muciloto cakwe kaimvwi kumbali lyalwizi. Nkabela omo mulwizi mwakazwa iŋombe impwizi zili musanu azibili.																									
Zyakali kweebeka, amibili yazyo yakalineneede. Nkabela kazicela akati kamatete.																									
Lino kusule lyazeezyo mwakazwa mulwizi azimwi zili musanu azibili. Zyakali zibi, amibili yazyo yakalikotede.																									
Nkabela kaziimvwi kumbali lyazitaanzi kunkomwe yalwizi.																									
Elyo iŋombe ezyo zili musanu azibili zibi zikotede zyakalya iŋombenyina zili musanu azibili izyakeebeka akuneneya.																									
Mpawo Farao wakasinsimuka. Alimwi wakoona, walota lwabili, wabona makunka aamaila aali musanu aabili aasyuuka akuba lyomwe, alisikide, mabotu.																									
Nkabela kusule lyayaayo kwakamena aamwi makunka aali musanu aabili, aapuputide, aajayidwe muuwo wakujwe.																									
Lino makunka aapuputide akalya makunka aasikide mabotu. Mpawo Farao wakasinsimuka, wajana kuti nciloto.																									
Lino nibwakaca, moyo wakwe wakapenga, aboobo wakatuma, waita boonse bacape ba-Egepita abasongo boonse.																									
Basike, Farao wakabalwiida ciloto cakwe, pele katakwe naba omwe iwakakonzya kucipandulula.																									
Mpawo mupati wabakutausi wakaambila Farao kuti, Sunu ndaibaluka kubisya kwangu.																									
Ciindi eciya Farao naakakalalila balanda bakwe akutwaanga muntolongo muŋanda yasilutwe wabatabilizi, mebo amupati wabajisi,																									
twakalota ziloto toonse tobile mubusiku bomwe. Umwi aumwi wakalota ciloto cipandululwa bumbi.																									
Lino oko nkutwakabede kakuli umwi mulombe mu-Hebrayo, mulanda wasilutwe wabatabilizi.																									
Ngonguwe wakatupandulwida ziloto zyesu akutwaambila umwi aumwi mbucaamba ciloto cakwe.																									
Nkabela makani akaba ncobeni mbubonya mbwaakatupandulwida. Mebo ndakaboozegwa mumilimo yangu pele mweenzuma wakaanzikwa.																									
Mpawo Farao wakatuma mulazyo wakwiita Josefa, nkabela bakafwambaana kumugwisya muntolongo, Naakamana kulinyoola akusama zimbi, wakeza kuli-Farao.																									
Elyo Farao wakaambila Josefa kuti, Ndalota ciloto, pele taakwe uukonzya kundipandulwida. Lino ndamvwa aanduwe kuti, wamvwa buyo ciloto, ulakonzya kucipandulula.																									
Mpawo Josefa wakavwiila Farao kuti, Teensi ndime pe, pele Leza nguuyoopandulwida Farao kabotu.																									
Lino Farao wakaambila Josefa kuti, Muciloto cangu ndakaliimvwi ankomwe yalwizi.																									
Omo mulwizi mwakazwa iŋombe impwizi zili musanu azibili, zineneede, zili aziwa zibotu, zyaakucela akati kamatete.																									
Lino kusule lyazeezyo mwakazwa impwizi azimwi zili musanu azibili, zikotede, zili aziwa zibi, ziyuminide loko amibili yazyo.																									
Nsikwe nendakabona iŋombe zibi zili boobu munyika yoonse ya-Egepita.																									
Mpawo iŋombe zikotede zibi zyakalya iŋombe zitaanzi zili musanu azibili zineneede.																									
Nekubaboobo zimane biyo kuzilya, teekwakazibwa kuti zyazilya pe, nkaambo ziwa zyezyo zyakacili zibi mbubonya mbozyakabede akutaanguna, Elyo ndakasinsimuka.																									
Ndakalota ci lo to acimwi, ndabona makunka aamaila aali musanu aabili akuba lyomwe. Akalisikide, mabotu.																									
Alimwi kusule lyayaayo kwakawayula makunka aali musanu aabili aapuseme, aaputide, aajayidwe amuuwo wakujwe.																									
Nkabela makunka aapuputide akalya makunka aali musanu aabili mabotu, Lino ndakalwiida bamucape, pele katakwe iwakakonzya kundipandulwida.																									
Mpawo Josefa wakaambila Farao kuti, Ciloto ca-Farao ncimwi buyo. Leza watondezya Farao ncayoocita.																									
Iŋombe zili musanu azibili zibotu nkukuti myaka iili musanu aibili, aalo makunka aali musanu aabili nkukuti myaka iili musanu aibili, nkaambo ciloto ncimwi buyo.																									
Alimwi iŋombe zili musanu azibili zikotede zibi izyakasyaalila kuzwa nkukuti myaka iili musanu aibili,																									
aalo makunka aali musanu aabili aapuputide aabijide kumuuwo wakujwe nkukuti myaka iili musanu aibili yanzala.																									
Mbubonya mbundaambila Farao kale, Leza watondezya Farao ncayoocita.																									
Kuyoosika myaka iili musanu aibili yaceo cipati munyika yoonse ya-Egepita,																									
elyo kusule lyayeeyo kuyoosika myaka iili musanu aibili yanzala; ceo coonse ciyoolubwa munyika ya-Egepira, nkaambo inzala iyoomanisya nyika.																									
Ceo taci-kooyooyeeyegwa limbi munyika nkaambo kanzala iiyoosyaalila, nkaambo iyoobija loko.																									
Alimwi ciloto mbucakaindululwa tobile kuli-Farao, nkukuti makani abambwa kuli-Leza, nkabela Leza ulafwambaana kwaacita.																									
Nkaambo kako Farao alangaule muntu musongo uucenjede, amubike kuti aendelezye nyika ya-Egepita.																									
Alimwi Farao abike basilutwe moonse munyika, kuti batole cipanzi casanu camicelo yanyika ya-Egepita mumyaka iili musanu aibili yaceo.																									
Babungike zilyo zyoonse zyamyaka eyi mibotu iiti sike, balondole maila mumaanza aa-Farao kuti kube zilyo muminzi, babike kumbali.																									
Zilyo ezyo ziyoobeda nyika ciyobozyo, ciligwe mumyaka iili musanu aibili yanzala iiyoosika kucisi ca-Egepita, kuti nyika itafwidilili kunzala.																									
Josefa mbwaakaba mweendelezi wa-Egepita. Lino aya majwi akabota mumeso aa-Farao amu meso aabalanda bakwe boonse.																									
Nkabela Farao wakaambila balanda bakwe kuti, Sa cilakonzeka kujana muntu aumwi uli mbuli oyu uuli a-Muuya wa-Leza?																									
Farao wakaambila Josefa kuti, Mbuli Leza mbwaakuzibya aya makani oonse, ncobeni taakwe musongo uucenjede mbuli nduwe.																									
Uyooendelezya iŋanda yangu abantu bangu boonse baleelede kulibamba mbubonya mboamba. Mubwami luzutu njooba mupati kwiinda nduwe.																									
Alimwi Farao wakaambila Josefa kuti, Bona! Ndakubika kuti ube mweendelezi wanyika yoonse ya-Egepita.																									
Mpawo Farao wakagwisya kanwenwe kakujanza lyakwe akukasamika ajanza lya-Josefa,																									
alimwi wakamusamika zyakusama zyabuluba akubika munkonde wangolida munsingo yakwe.																									
Nkabela wakamutansika munkalaki yabili njaakajisi, nkabela bakali koongolola kubusyu bwakwe kuti, Amukotame!																									
Mbuboobo mbwaakamubika kuti aendelezye nyika yoonse ya-Egepita.																									
Alimwi Farao wakaambila Josefa kuti, Ndime Farao. Ncobeni taakwe muntu uuyoonyampula																									
ijanza lyakwe nanka kuulu kwakwe munyika yoonse ya-Egepita cita wazumina yebo.																									
Nkabela Farao wakaulika Josefa izina lya-Zafenati-Panea, alimwi wakamupa Asenati mwana musimbi wa-Potifera mupaizi waku-Oni kuti amukwate.																									
Aboobo Josefa wakali kuya bweendeenda munyika yoonse ya-Egepita,																									
Josefa kali amyaka iili makumi otatwe naakanjila mumilimo kuli-Farao mwami wa-Egepita.																									
Elyo Josefa naakazwa kuli-Farao wakali kuya bweendeenda munyika yoonse ya-Egepita.																									
Lino mumyaka iili musanu aibili yaceo nyika yakapa zilyo zinji loko.																									
Nkabela wakabungika zilyo zyoonse zyamyaka iili musanu aibili yaceo munyika ya-Egepita, walondola zilyo muminzi.																									
Kuminzi yoonse zilyo zyamyuunda iiengelede munzi wakazilondola mulinguwo.																									
Josefa wakalondola maila manji loko mbuli musenga wakunkomwe yalwizi, mane lumwi wakaleka kwaabala, nkaambo kaatacibaliki.																									
Lino mwaka wanzala nowatakaina kusika, Josefa wakazyalilwa bana bobile balombe mbaakamuzyalila Asenati mwana musimbi wa-Potifera mupaizi wa-Oni.																									
Nkabela mwana mutaanzi Josefa wakamuulika izina lya-Manase, nkaambo wakati, Leza wandilubya mafwabi aangu oonse aluzubo loonse lwataata.																									
Amwana wabili wakamuulika izina lya-Efraimu, nkaambo wakati, Leza wandizyazya munyika yakufwaba kwangu.																									
Cibe ciindi, myaka iili musanu aibili yaceo camu nyika ya-Egepita yakamana, amyaka iili musanu aibili yanzala yakatalika, mbubonya mbuli Josefa mbwaakaamba.																									
Lino kakuli inzala muzisi zyoonse, pele munyika yoonse ya-Egepita kakuli zilyo.																									
Bantu boonse ba-Egepita nibakafwa inzala, bantu bakalilila zilyo kuli-Farao, nkabela Farao wakaambila baEgepita boonse kuti, Kamuya kuli-Josefa; kufumbwa ncaamba amucicite.																									
Elyo inzala niyakaba koonse koonse kunyika, Josefa wakajalula mavuko oonse, waabila ba-Egepita zilyo. Inzala yakakataazya loko munyika yaEgepita.																									
Alimwi bantu bakuzisi zyoonse bakasika ku-Egepita kuzoosunza kuli-Josefa, nkaambo inzala yakakomena munyika yoonse.																									
Lweendo lutaanzi lwababunyina Josefa lwakusunza ku-Egepita																									
Lino Jakobo naakamvwa kuti maila nkwaali ku-Egepita, Jakobo wakabuzya bana bakwe kuti, Ino nkaambonzi mulalangana buyo.																									
Wakaamba kuti, Amuswiilile! Ndamvwa kuti maila nkwaali ku-Egepita, Amwiinke nkuko, mukatuulile, kuti tupone, tutafwi.																									
Aboobo babunyina Josefa bali ikumi bakainka kuyoosunza ku-Egepita.																									
Pele Benjamini mwanike wa-Josefa, Jakobo takamutumide ababunyina, nkaambo wakati, Ambweni bubi bulamujana.																									
Elyo bana ba-Israyeli bakasika kuyoosunza akati kabamwi basikusunza, nkaambo kakuli inzala munyika ya-Kanana.																									
Lino Josefa kali mweendelezi wacisi coonse. Ngonguwe iwakali kuuzizya bantu boonse banyika.																									
Aboobo babunyina Josefa bakeza, bamukotamina cakuvundama ansi. Nkabela Josefa naakabona babunyina wakabaziba,																									
elyo wakalifulunganya mbuli mweenzu, wabaambila cakuhalamuka.																									
Wakababuzya kuti, Mwazwa kuli? Bakati, Twazwa kunyika ya-Kanana kuzoosunza zyakulya.																									
Lino Josefa wakaziba bakulana bakwe, pele balo tabakamuzibide.																									
Elyo Josefa wakaibalukwa ziloto zyakwe nzyaakalota aambabo, nkabela wakabaambila kuti, Pe, muli basimutambatamba, mweza kuzoobona butete bwanyika.																									
Bakamuvwiila kuti, Pe, mwami, balanda bako beza kuzoosunza zyakulya.																									
Toonse biyo tuli bana bamuntu omwe. Tuli bantu baluleme. Balanda bako tabali basimutambatamba pe.																									
Wakati, Nee! mweza kuzoobona butete bwanyika. Bakati, Pe, swebo tobalanda bako tuli babunyina bali ikumi ababili,																									
bana bamuntu omwe munyika ya-Kanana, Muniini wasyaala kulitateesu, aumwi taciwo.																									
Pele Josefa wakabaambila kuti, Ncobeni makani ali mbubonya mbundaamba, Muli basimutambatamba.																									
Mbuboobu mbumuyoosolekwa. Ncobeni Farao mbali muumi, tamukoyooinka kuzwa okuno, cita mwanike wanu akasike okuno.																									
Amutume umwi wanu kuti akete mwanike wanu, pele nywebo mulaangwa.																									
Mbuboobo majwi aanu mbwaayoosolekwa, kuzibwe na ngaalusinizyo, Na takuli boobo, ncobeni Farao mbacili muumi, muli basimutambatamba.																									
Mpuwo wakabaanga muntolongo mazuba otatwe.																									
Lino buzuba bwatatu nebwakaca, Josefa wakabaambila kuti, Amucite obo, mupone, nkaambo mebo ndayoowa Leza.																									
Na muli bantu baluleme, umwi munyoko wanu asyaale muntolongo yanu, pele nywebo kamuya, mutolele maanda aanu zilyo zyabusunzi.																									
Lino amulete mwanike wanu kulindime, aboobo lusinizyo lwamajwi aanu luyoozibwa, kuti mutafwi. Mpawo bakacita obo.																									
Nkabela bakaamba umwi aumwi kumweenzinyina kuti, Ncobeni tulijisi mulandu mumakani aamwanike wesu,																									
nkaambo twakabona kunyonyongana kwamoyo wakwe naakali kutukombelezya, nekubaboobo twakakaka kuswiilila: Nciceeco mapenzi aya ncaasikila kulindiswe.																									
Lino Rubeni wakabaambila kuti, Sa teendakamwaambila kuti, Mutabisizyi mwana! Nekubaboobo mwakakaka kuswiilila.																									
Aboobo sunu twapegwa mulandu wabulowa bwakwe. Teebakaziba kuti Josefa ulamvwa, nkaambo bakali kwaambilana amutoloki.																									
Mpawo wakabafutatila, walila. Amane wakaboola alimwi kulimbabo, wabaambila, wagwisya Simeoni akati kabo, wamwaanga kumeso aabo.																									
Elyo Josefa wakalailila kuti inkomo zyabo zizuzigwe maila, amali aabo aboozegwe umwi																									
aumwi munkomo yakwe, alimwi bapegwe bulilu bwakulya munzila. Lino kwakacitwa obo.																									
Mpoonya awo bakabopa imbongolo zyabo amaila, bainka. Pele kucile, umwi wabo wakajula inkomo yakwe																									
kuti asanine imbongolo yakwe, elyo wakabona mali aakwe, mwaali mumulomo wasaka lyakwe.																									
Lino wakaambila beenzinyina kuti, Amubone! mali aangu apilusigwa, Mwaali mumulomo wasaka lyangu,																									
Bamvwe obo, myoyo yabo yakazwa, nkabela bakalangana umwi aumwi kumweenzinyina cakukankama, bati, Ino ncinzi eci Leza ncatucitila?																									
Lino nebakasika kuli-Jakobo wisaabo munyika ya-Kanana, bakamwaambila makani oonse aakabacitikila, bati,																									
Ulya muntu, mwami wacisi, wakatukalamukila, watwaambila kuti, Muli basimutambatamba banyika.																									
Pele twakaamwaambila kuti, Ne! Tuli bantu baluleme. Tatuli basimutambatamba pe.																									
Tuli babunyina bali ikumi ababili, bana bamuntu omwe, Umwi taciwo, amuniini wasyaala kuliwiseesu munyika ya-Kanana.																									
Elyo oyo muntu, mwami wacisi, wakatwaambila kuti, Mbuboobu mbunkonzya kuziba kuti muli balulami. Amusie munyoko umwi kulindime.																									
Lino amutole zilyo zyakusunza kumaanda aanu, mwiinke. Pele amundiletele munyoko muniini,																									
aboobo njooziba kuti tamuli basimutambatamba, muli bantu baluleme, Mwaakucita obo, njoomuboozezya munyoko, nkabela muyookonzya kusambala munyika.																									
Lino nebakali kutaula masaka aabo, bakajana umwi aumwi ciputizyo camali aakwe musaka lyakwe.																									
Mpawo nebakabona ziputizyo zyamali aabo, bakayoowa boonse awisaabo.																									
Nkabela Jakobo wisaabo wakabaambila kuti, Mwandilobya! Josefa taciwo, alakwe Simeoni taciwo,																									
lino mulayanda kutola Benjamini. Andilemena mapenzi! Mpawo Rubeni wakaambila wisi kuti, Ukajaye bana bangu bobile na ndabula kumuboozya kulinduwe.																									
Umubike mumaanza aangu, Ndamuboozya. Pele wakati, Nel Mwanaangu takooyooinka anywebo,																									
nkaambo mupati wakwe wakafwa, lino wasyaala alike. Na wasikilwa bubi mulweendo ndomutola, muyooselusya imvwi zyangu cabuusu mukabanda.																									
Lweendo lwabili lwakusunza. Lino inzala yakabija munyika.																									
Nkabela nebakamanisya kulya zilyo nzebakasunzide ku-Egepita, wisaabo wakabaambila kuti, Amubweede, mukatuulile alimwi tulyo tuniini.																									
Pele Juda wakabaambila kuti, Ncobeni ulya muntu wakatukonkezya kuti, Tamukooyoobona busyu bwangu limbi cita mwaletelela mwanike wanu.																									
Na wamuzumizya mwanike wesu kuti tuye awe, tulaya kuyookuulila zyakulya, pele na wakaka kumutuma tatukooinka pe,																									
nkaambo ulya muntu wakatwaambila kuti, Tamukooyoobona busyu bwangu cita mwaletelela amwanike wanu.																									
Elyo Israyeli wakati, Nkaambonzi mwakandibisizya kukulwiida muntu kuti mulijisi mwanike wanu?																									
Bakati, Muntu wakatubuzisisya makani aaluzubo lwesu, Wakatubuzya kuti, Sa wisi wanu mpaacili?																									
Sa mulijisi munyoko aumwi? Elyo twakamulwiida makani aya oonse. Sa twakalizi kuti ulaamba kuti, Amulete mwanike wanu?																									
Mpawo Juda wakaambila Israyeli wisi kuti, Tuma mulombe ambebo, lino tulanyamuka akwiinka, kuti tupone tutafwi, swebo ayebo atwana twesu.																									
Mebo nomususi; kujanza lyangu nkoelede kumulangawida. Na ndabula kumuboozya akumubika kubusyu bwako, mbe amulandu lyoonse akutamani.																									
Ncobeni nitwatakali kulinelezya netubweede kale alimwi.																									
Mpoonya awo Israyeli wisaabo wakabaambila kuti, Mbubo, kamuya, alimwi mbuboobu mbumweelede kucita,																									
Amutolelele micelo yanyika muzibwe zelo zyanu, mutolele muntu cipo.																									
Amutole tumabbona, atuci, atulisyo twanikoa, atununkilizyo twaladunu, andongo aminsomwa yamaalmondi.																									
Alimwi amubweze mali aamwi mumaanza aanu. Mali aakapilusigwa mumilomo yamasaka amwaapilusye mumaanza aanu; ambweni bakaaluba.																									
Amwanike wanu amumutole, munyamuke, mubweede kumuntu oyo.																									
Leza Singuzuzyoonse amu pe luzyalo mumeso aamuntu oyo, kuti aangunune munyoko wanu uusyeede antoomwe a-Benjamini. Na ndalobelwa bana bangu, ndaloba.																									
Mpawo bantu bakatolelela cipo eco, amali aambi mumaanza aabo a-Benjamini mwanike wabo, banyampuka, bainka kuEgepita, baakwiima kubusyu bwa-Josefa,																									
Nkabela Josefa naakabona kuti beza a-Benjamini, wakaambila mubambi waŋanda yakwe																									
kuti, Njizya aba bantu muŋanda, alimwi jaya munyama, utubambile, nkaambo bantu aba baleelede kulya kulindime ciindi casikati.																									
Lino oyo muntu wakacita mbubonya mbuli Josefa mbwaakalailila. Wakanjizya bantu muŋanda ya-Josefa.																									
Mpawo bantu bakayoowa nkaambo kakunjizigwa muŋanda ya-Josefa, bati, Nkaambo kamali aakaboozegwa mumasaka esu mulweendo lutaanzi, ncencico ncitwaletelwa.																									
Ulayanda kutupa mulandu akutwaanga, atutole mubuzike swebo ambongolo zyesu.																									
Lino bakaswena kufwaafwi kumubambi waŋanda ya-Josefa akwaambaula awe kumulyango waŋanda.																									
Bakati, Koswiilila, mwami. Ncobeni twakeza mulweendo lutaanzi kuzoosunza zilyo.																									
Elyo netwakasika kucilo, twakajalula masaka esu, twabona kuti mali esu mwaali, mali aaumwi aumwi kumulomo wasaka lyakwe, mali oonse buyo.																									
Lino sunu twaaboozya mumaanza esu. Alimwi twaleta mali aamwi mumaanza esu kuzooula zilyo. Tatuzi na nguni wakabika mali esu mumasaka esu.																									
Elyo wakabavwiila kuti, Amube aluumuno. Mutayoowi. Leza wanu a-Leza wabamausowanu nguwakamupa coolwe mumasaka aanu.																									
Ndakatambula mali aanu. Amane kwaamba obo, wakaleta Simeoni kulimbabo.																									
Lino oyo muntu naakanjizya bantu muŋanda ya-Josefa, wakaleta maanzi kuti basambe kumaulu, alimwi wakasanina imbongolo zyabo.																									
Nkabela bakabamba cipo kuti bape Josefa asika isikati, nkaambo bakamvwa kuti nkobazoolida insima ciindi casikati.																									
Lino Josefa naakasika kuŋanda, bakamuletela mumonya muŋanda cipo ncebakeza aco, nkabela bakamukotamina cakuvundama ansi.																									
Mpawo wakababuzya mbobapona, alimwi wababuzya kuti, Sa usowanu uli kabotu, munene ngomwakandaambila? Sa ucipona?																									
Bakamuvwiila kuti, Mulanda wako wiseesu uli kabotu, ucipona. Elyo bakasintama, bakotama.																									
Atambye meso aakwe, wakabona mwanike wakwe Benjamini, mwana wabanyina, nkabela wakababuzya kuti,																									
Sa Oyu ngomwanike wanu ngomwakandaambila? Alimwi wakati, Leza akupe coolwe, mwanaangu.																									
Mpawo Josefa wakafwambaana kuyandaula cilililo, nkaambo moyo wakwe wakali kuyandisya mwanike wakwe.																									
Wakanjila muŋanda yakoonena, walilila nkuko. Amane kulila, wakasamba kumeso, wazwa, walisimyasimya, wati, Amubike cakulya.																									
Nkabela bakamubikila cakwe alike, abalo cabo abalike, aba-Egepita mbaakali kulya abo balike,																									
nkaambo ba-Egepita tabakonzyi kulya insima mucilido comwe aba-Hebrayo, nkaambo kucita obo kulatondwa kuba-Egepita.																									
Nkabela bakakazikwa kunembo lyakwe, mupati mbuli bupati bwakwe, muniini mbuli buniini bwakwe. Lino bantu bakali kulangana cakugamba.																									
Lino bakabikilwa zipampwido kubusyu bwakwe, pele cipampwido ca-Benjamini cakainda zipampwido zyabo zyoonse zyeelelo zyosanwe. Elyo bakanywa akunywisya awe.																									
Josefa mbwaakasunka bananyina. Lino wakalailila mupati waŋanda yakwe kuti,																									
Zuzya masaka aabantu zilyo, mbubonya mbobakonzya kunyampula, alimwi bika mali aamuntu umwi aumwi mumulomo wasaka lyakwe.																									
Ayalo inkomeki yangu, inkomeki yansiliva koibika mumulomo wasaka lyamuniini, antoomwe amali aakwe aazilyo.																									
Nkabela wakacita mbubonya mbuli Josefa mbwaakalailila­. Buce biyo, bantu bakasungulwa kuti beende balo ambongolo zyabo.																									
Lino kabatana kuya kule kuzwa kumunzi Josefa wakaambila mupati waŋanda yakwe kuti, Nyamuka, ubatobele bantu.																									
Wabeenzya, uleelede kubaambila kuti, Ino nkaambonzi mwandiboozezya bubi mucimanga cabubotu? Nkaambonzi mwabba inkomeki yangu yansiliva?																									
Sa teensi njiyo mwami wangu mwaanywida? Sa teensi njiyo njasondya? Mwabisya kukucita obo.																									
Wabeenzya, wabaambila majwi ayo. Lino bakamubuzya kuti, Ino nkaambonzi mwami wesu ulaamba majwi aya? Swebo tobalanda bako cilatondwa kulindiswe kucita obo.																									
Mwabona kuti mali ayo ngetwakajana mumilomo yankomo zyesu twakaaboozya kulinduwe kuzwa kunyika ya-­Kanana,																									
Ino inga twabba buti insiliva na ingolida muŋanda yamwami wako? Kufumbwa muntu akati kesu tobalanda bako uujanwa kuti uli ankomeki, afwe,																									
Aswebo toonse tulaba bazike bamwami wesu. Wakavuwa kuti, Kube mbubonya obo mboamba.																									
Kufumbwa uujanwa kuti uli ankomeki abe mulanda wangu, pele bamwi banu tabakooyooba amulandu.																									
Mpoonya awo bakafwambaana kwaangununa umwi aumwi isaka lyakwe, batula ansi, bajalula umwi aumwi isaka lyakwe.																									
Nkabela wakayandaula moonse moonse, watalikila kumupati, wasyaalizya kumuniini, nkabela inkomeki yakajanwa munkomo ya-Benjamini.																									
Mpawo bakadelaula zyakusama zyabo, babopa umwi aumwi imbongolo zyakwe, bapilukila kumunzi.																									
Lino Juda abeenzinyina nebakasika kuŋanda ya-Josefa, bajana kuti mpacili, nkabela bakamuvundamina ansi.																									
Elyo Josefa wakabaambila kuti, Ino ncinzi eco neemwacita? Sa tamuzi kuti muntu uuli mbuli ndime ncobeni ulikuzi kusonda?																									
Mpawo Juda wakati, Twaambenzi kumwami wangu? Twaambenzi? Tulilulamike buti? Leza ngowajana milandu yesu tobalanda bako,																									
Toonse tuli bazike bamwami wangu, aswebo ayooyo moyajanwa inkomeki mujanza lyakwe.																									
Pele wakati, Nee! Kulindime cilatondwa kucita obo, Muntu wajanwa kuti uli ankomeki mujanza lyakwe, ngonguwe alike uuelede kuba muzike wangu.																									
Pele inywe nobamwi kamuya aluumuno kuli usowanu,																									
Mpawo Juda wakaswena afwaafwi kulinguwe, wati, Wence simalelaangu, ndemulanda wako Ŋambe ijwi mumatwi aasimalelaangu.																									
Bukali bwako butabukili mulanda wako, nkaambo uli mbubonya mbuli Farao.																									
Simalelaangu wakatubuzya swebo tobalanda bakwe kuti, Sa mulijisi uso na munyoko?																									
Nkabela twakaambila simalelo wesu kuti, Tulijisi wiseesu munene, amwanike wesu mwana wabucembele bwakwe,																									
Mukulana wakwe wakafwa, lino kwakasyaala nguwe alike mulibanyina, nkabela wisi ulamuyandisya.																									
Lino yebo wakatwaambila tobalanda bako kuti, Amumulete kulindime, nkamu bone.																									
Twakaambila mwami wesu kuti, Musankwa takonzyi kusia wisi pe. Asia wisi, wisi ulafwa.																									
Pele yebo wakatwaambila tobalanda bako kuti, Na mwanike wanu tasiki anywebo, tamukooyoobona limbi busyu bwangu.																									
Aboobo netwakapiluka kuliwiseesu mulanda wako, twakamulwiida majwi aamwami wangu.																									
Nkabela tateesu naakaamba kuti, Amupiluke, mukatuulile tulyo, twakati, Tatukonzyi kuya pe,																									
cita mwanike wesu alakwe kali wo, lino tulaya, nkaambo tatukonzyi kubona busyu bwamuntu oyo na mwanike wesu tawo.																									
Amvwe obo, wiseesu mulanda wako wakatwaambila kuti, Mulizi kuti mwanakazi wangu wakandizyalila bana bobile.																									
Umwi wakandisia, Ndakati, Ncobeni ulikwamwiidwe, Nsimubwene limbi mane kusikila sunu.																									
Lino na mwatola oyu alakwe kuzwa kulindime, alimwi bubi bwamujana, muyooselusya imvwi zyangu abuusu mukabanda.																									
Lino na ndasika kulitaata mulanda wako, alimwi musankwa tawo, —moyo wakwe ulisukeme musankwa,																									
aboobo naayoobona kuti musankwa tawo, uyoofwa, Tobalanda bako tuyooselusya imvwi zyatateesu mulanda wako cabuusu mukabanda.																									
Nkaambo mebo ndemulanda wako ndimususi musankwa kuti aye kulitaata. Ndakati, Na ndabula kumuboozya kulinduwe, njooba amulandu kulitaata mazuba oonse.																									
Wence nsyaale, mebo ndemulanda wako, mucibaka camulombe, mbe muzike wamwami wangu, lino musankwa ainke abeenzinyina.																									
Nkaambo nsikonzyi kupiluka kulitaata na mulombe tawo. Ndayoowa kubona bubi buti sikile taata.																									
Josefa mbwaakalilubulula kubananyina. Mpoonya awo Josefa wakakacilwa kulisimya-simya kumeso aabakwabo ibakaimvwi awe,																									
nkabela wakapolopota kuti, Amubagwisye bantu bonse kulindime. Aboobo katakwe muntu naba omwe ngwaakaimvwi awe Josefa naakalilubulula kulibabunyina,																									
Elyo wakalila loko, mane ba-Egepita bakamvwa, abalo basiŋanda ba-Farao bakamvwa.																									
Josefa wakaambila bananyina kuti, Ndime Josefa. Sa taata ucipona? Nkabela babunyina bakakacilwa kumuvwiila, nkaambo bakali kukankama kubusyu bwakwe.																									
Mpawo Josefa wakaambila babunyina kuti, Amuze kufwafwi kulindime. Bakaswena afwaafwi.																									
Lino wakati, Ndime Josefa mwanike wanu ngomwakasambala kuti atolwe ku-Egepita.																									
Lino mutapengi nekuba kulikalalila nkaambo kakundisambazya okuno, nkaambo Leza ngowakandituma kunembo lyanu kuti aponye bantu.																									
Myaka yobile inzala yakataazya munyika, alimwi myaka yosanwe iciza iitakooyooba akulima nanka kutebula.																									
Leza nguwakandituma kunembo lyanu kuti amusiile lunyungu akumuyobweda bafutusi banji.																									
Teensi ndinywe mwakandituma okuno pe, nguLeza. Wandibika kuti mbe wisi Farao amwami waŋanda yakwe yoonse amweendelezi wanyika yoonse ya-Egepita.																									
Amufwambaane kwiinka kulitaata, mumwaambile kuti, Mbuboobu mbwaamba mwanaako Josefa,																									
Leza wandibika kuti mbe mwami wacisi coonse ca-Egepita. Boola kulindime. Utaneeleli pe.																									
Uzookala mucisi ca-Goseni aboobo uzooba kufwaafwi kulindime yebo abana bako abazukulu bako anibelele zyako aŋombe zyako azyoonse nzojisi.																									
Lino njookulela nkuko oko, nkaambo kuciza myaka yosanwe yanzala, kuti utalobi yebo abasiŋanda bako azyoonse nzojisi,																									
Amulange! Meso aanu alabona, aalo meso aamwanike wangu Benjamini alabona, kuti ncobeni mulomo wangu nguuambaula anywe.																									
Muleelede kulwiida taata makani aabulemu bwangu bwaku-Egepita amakani oonse ngemubwene. Amufwambaane kuleta taata okuno.																									
Mpawo wakawida ansingo yamwanike wakwe Benjamini, walila, alakwe Benjamini wakalila ansingo yakwe.																									
Abalo bakulana bakwe boonse wakabamyonta akulila alimbabo. Amane obo, bakulana bakwe bakaambaula awe.																									
Lino impuo neyakamvwigwa kuŋanda ya-Farao, yakuti, Babuuyina Josefa basika, makani akabotela Farao abalanda bakwe.																									
Nkabela Farao wakaambila Josefa kuti, Ambila bakulana bako kuti, Kamucita obu. Amubope imbongolo zyanu, mwiinke kunyika ya-Kanana.																									
Mwasika, amulete usowanu abamaanda aanu boonse, muboole kulindime. Njoomupa bubotu bwanyika ya-Egepita, mulye bunono bwanyika.																									
Alimwi kobalailila kuti, Mbuboobu mbumweelede kucita. Amutole iŋola kuzwa kucisi ca-Egepita zibe zyakubwezela bacece banu abanakazi banu,																									
alimwi amunyampule usowanu, muboole. Mutalikataazyi ambono zyanu pe, nkaambo bubotu bwanyika yoonse ya-Egepita buyooba bwanu.																									
Lino bana ba-Israyeli bakacita obo. Josefa wakabapa ŋola, mbubonya mbwaakaamba Farao, abulilu boonse wabapa.																									
Alimwi boonse buyo wakabapa umwi aumwi zyakuzwaata, a-Benjamini mwanike wakwe wakamupa mali aansiliva aali myanda yotatwe azyakuzwaata zyosanwe.																									
Alakwe wisi, nzeezi nzyaakamutumina: imbongolo zili ikumi ziyumwide zintu zibotu																									
zyaku-Egepita, ambongolo inzyazi zili ikumi ziyumwide maila azilyo abulilu bwawisi.																									
Elyo wakatuma babunyina, bainka. Nkabela wakabaambila kuti, Mutakalazyanyi munzila.																									
Mpawo bakazwa kucisi caEgepita, basika kucisi ca-Kanana nkwaakabede Jakobo wisaabo.																									
Nkabela bakamwaambila kuti, Josefa ucipona, alimwi ngonguwe uuendelezya mucisi coonse ca-Egepita, Amvwe obo, moyo wakwe wakalebuluka, nkaambo takwakazumina.																									
Pele nebakamulwiida majwi oonse aa-Josefa ngaakamwaambila, alimwi naakabona ŋola Josefa nzyaakatuma kukumubweza, moyo wa-Jakobo wisaabo wakabukuluka,																									
Israyeli wakati, Mbubo, mwanaangu Josefa ucipona, Njiinke kuyoomubona nkentanafwa.																									
Ba-Israyeli mbubakalongela ku-Egepita. Lino Israyeli wakanyampuka azyoonse nzyaakajisi,																									
wasika ku-Beereseba, watuula zipaizyo kuli-Leza wa-Izaka wisi.																									
Nkabela Leza wakaambaula a-Israyeli muzilengano zyamasiku, wati, Jakobo, Jakobo. Wakati, Mpondi.																									
Wakati, Ndime Leza, Leza wauso. Utayoowi kwiinka ku-Egepita, nkaambo njoocita kuti ukabe musyobo mupati nkuko.																									
Njooinka ayebo ku-Egepita, alimwi njookuboozya kuzwa nkuko. Alakwe Josefa uyoobika ijanza lyakwe ameso aako.																									
Mpawo Jakobo wakanyampuka kuzwa ku-Beereseba, nkabela bana ba-Israyeli bakanyampula																									
Jakobo wisaabo abacece babo abanakazi babo munola Farao nzyaakatumide kukubabweza.																									
Azyalo iŋombe zyabo ambono zyabo zyoonse nzibakajene munyika ya-Kana na bakazitola aboobo bakasika ku-Egepita, Jakobo alunyungu lwakwe loonse.																									
Bana bakwe balombe, abazukulu bakwe, abana bakwe basimbi, abana basimbi babana bakwe, amuzukulu wakwe woonse, boonse buyo wakeza abo kunyika ya-Egepita.																									
Ngaaya mazina aabana ba-Israyeli ibakasika ku-Egepita, nkukuti Jakobo abana bakwe, Mwana mutaanzi wa-Jakobo kali Rubeni.																									
Bantu boonse Jakobo mbaakeza abo ku-Egepita, nkokuti bantu ibakazwa mucikungu cakwe, kutabala banakazi babana bakwe, bakali makumi aali musanu alimwi amusanu aumwi.																									
Abana ba-Josefa mbaakazyalilwa ku-Egepita bakali babili, Bantu boonse baluzubo lwa-Jakobo ibakeza ku-Egepita bakali makumi aali musanu aabili.																									
Nkabela wakatuma Juda kunembo lyakwe kuli-Josefa kuti babonanine ku-Goseni, elyo bakasika kucisi ca-Goseni.																									
Mpawo Josefa wakabopa inkalaki yakwe, wainka kuyooswanaana a-Israyeli wisi ku-Goseni. Babonane biyo, wakawida ansingo yakwe, walila ansingo yakwe ciindi cilamfulamfu.																									
Lino Israyeli wakaambila Josefa kuti, Mbubo, mfwe, nkaambo ndabona busyu bwako, ndabona kuti ucipona.																									
Mpoonya awo Josefa wakaambila bananyina aluzubo lwawisi kuti, Ndainka kuyooambila Farao makani,																									
Nkamulwiide kuti, Bakulana bangu aluzubo lwataara ibakakede munyika ya-Kanana basika kulindime.																									
Baalumi abo mbeembeli, mbavubi baŋombe, alimwi baletelela imbelele zyabo aŋombe zyabo azyoonse nzebajisi.																									
Lino Farao naayoomwiita akumubuzya kuti, Muli basimilimonzi? muleelede kuvuwa kuti, Swebo tobalanda bako tuli beembeli.																									
Njemilimo yesu kuzwa kubwanike bwesu akusikila asunu, swebo abamatateesu boonse, Amuvuwe obo,																									
kuti mukakale munyika ya-Goseni, nkaambo beembeli boonse balisulidwe kuba-Egepita.																									
Jakobo mbwaakabonesegwa kuli-Farao. Elyo Josefa wakasika kuli-Farao, wamwaambila kuti,																									
Taata abakulana bangu ambelele zyabo aŋombe zyabo ambono zyabo zyoonse basika kuzwa kunyika ya-Kanana. Nkobali kunyika ya-Goseni.																									
Nkabela wakasala bantu hosanwe akati kabakulana bakwe, wabaimikizya kubusyu bwa-Farao.																									
Lino Farao wakabuzya bakulana bakwe kuti, Muli basimilimonzi? Bakavwiila Farao kuti, Swebo tobalanda bako tuli basikweembela imbelele, swebo abamatateesu boonse.																									
Alimwi bakaambila Farao kuti, Tweza kuzookala-kala munyika, nkaambo tacikwe mani aakucezya matanga esu, nkaambo ipamba lyalema mucisi ca-Kanana.																									
Twakumbila tobalanda bako kuti tukale munyika ya-Goseni. Alimwi Farao wakaambila Josefa kuti, Uso abakulana bako basika kulinduwe.																									
Nyika yoonse ya-Egepita ili kunembo lyako. Kazika uso abakulana bako mububotu bwanyika. Bakale munyika ya-Goseni.																									
Alimwi na ulizi bantu bacenjede akati kabo, kobabika kuti babambe matanga aangu.																									
Lino Josefa wakanjizya Jakobo wisi, wamwiimikizya kubusyu bwaFarao, nkabela Jakobo wakalongezya Farao.																									
Elyo Farao wakabuzya Jakobo kuti, Mazuba aamyaka yabuumi bwako ali buti?																									
Jakobo wakavwiila Farao kuti, Myaka yakweendeenda kwangu ili mwanda amakumi otatwe.																									
Mazuba aamyaka yabuumi bwangu mace buyo, alimwi mabi, taana kweelana amazuba aamyaka yabuumi bwabamataata kuciindi cakweendeenda kwabo.																									
Mpawo Jakobo wakalongezya Farao, wazwa omo Farao mwaakabede, Nkabela Josefa wakakazika wisi abakulana bakwe,																									
wabapa civubilo munyika ya-Egepita, munyika imbotu, munyika ya-Ramese, mbubonya mbwaakalailila Farao.																									
Alimwi Josefa wakasanizya wisi abakulana bakwe aluzubo lwawisi zilyo mbubonya mbuli mweelwe wabasiŋanda babo,																									
Amwi makani aapamba lyaku-Egepita. Lino kwakabulika zilyo munyika yoonse,																									
nkaambo ipamba lyakakomena loko, Nyika ya-Egepita anyika ya-Kanana yoonse zyakawizuka nkaambo kapamba.																									
Nkabela Josefa wakabungika mali oonse aakajanwa munyika ya-Egepita amunyika ya-Kanana nkaambo kazilyo nzibakali kuula; mali ayo Josefa wakaaleta muŋanda ya-Farao,																									
Lino mali oonse naakamaninina munyika ya-Egepita amunyika ya-Kanana, ba-Egepita																									
boonse bakeza kuliJosefa, bati, Utwaabile zilyo. Sa ncibotu kuti tufwe mumeso aako? Nkaambo tacikwe mali.																									
Elyo Josefa wakabaambila kuti, Amundipe iŋombe zyanu. Ndamuuzizya zilyo aŋombe zyanu na tacikwe mali.																									
Mpawo bakaletela Josefa matanga aabo, nkabela Josefa wakabapa zilyo cakuulana ambizi amatanga aambelele aŋombe ambongolo.																									
Wakabauzizya zilyo aŋombe zyabo zyoonse. Mwaka oyo umane, bakasika kulinguwe																									
mumwaka wabili, bati, Tatukonzyi kusisa makani kumwami wesu, Mali amaninina, aalo matanga aŋombe aba aamwami wesu.																									
Taakwe cintu cicisyeede kumeso aako O mwami wesu cita mibili yesu amyuunda yesu.																									
Sa ncibotu kuti tufwe kumeso aako, swebo amyuunda yesu? Kotuula swebo amyuunda yesu, utupe zilyo.																									
Tulaba bazike ba-Farao, swebo amyuunda yesu. Utupe imbuto, kuti tupone, tutafwi, ayalo nyika itanyonyooki.																									
Aboobo Josefa wakaulila Farao nyika yoonse ya-Egepita, nkaambo baEgepita bakaulisya umwi aumwi muunda wakwe,																									
nkaambo ipamba lyakabakataazya loko, Nyika yakaba ya-Farao, abalo bantu wakabanjizya mubuzike kuzwa kumagolelo amwi aa-Egepita kusikila kumagolelo amwi.																									
Nyika yabapaizi luzutu taakwe naakaiula, nkaambo bapaizi bakalipedwe caabilo kuzwa kuli-Farao,																									
nkabela bakali kulya caabilo cabo Farao ncaakabapa, aboobo teebakauzya nyika yabo.																									
Lino Josefa wakaambila bantu kuti, Amubone! Sunu ndamuula, nywebo anyika zyanu, mube ba-Farao. Nzeezi imbuto, Amubyale myuunda.																									
Lino casika ciindi cakutebula, muleelede kupa Farao cipanzi casanu, azipanzi zyone ziyooba zyanu, zibe zyakubyazya azilyo zyakusanizya basiŋanda banu atwana twanu.																									
Bakati, Watuponya. Atujane buuya mumeso aamwami wesu, lino tuyooba bazike ba-Farao.																									
Mbuboobo Josefa mbwaakacita mulao munyika ya-Egepita, mbuucibede asunu, wakuti Farao apegwe cipanzi casanu. Nyika yabapaizi luzutu njiitali ya-Farao.																									
Bucembele bwa-Jakobo. Aboobo Israyeli wakalikede munyika ya-Egepita, mucisi ca-Goseni.																									
Nkabela bakajana imbono mulinjiyo, alimwi bakazyalisya mane bavula loko.																									
Lino Jakobo wakakala munyika ya-Egepita myaka iili ikumi amusanu aibili. Mazuba oonse aa-Jakobo,																									
nkokuti myaka yoonse yabuumi bwakwe, akasika kumyaka iili mwanda amakumi one amusanu aibili.																									
Elyo ciindi cakufwa kwa-Israyeli nicakasika kufwaafwi, wakaita mwanaakwe Josefa, wamwaambila kuti,																									
Na ncobeni ndijene luzyalo mumeso aako, bika ijanza lyako kunsi lyacibelo cangu, undicitile caluzyalo acakusyomeka, Utandizikili mucisi ca-Egepita pe.																									
Njanda koona mucooneno cabamatata. Uleelede kunditola kuzwa ku-Egepita, ukandivwike mumavwikilo aabo. Wakati, Njoocita mbubonya mboamba.																									
Wakati, Ndikonka. Mpawo wakamukonka. Elyo Israyeli wakalikotamika amusego wabulo bwakwe.																									
Jakobo mbwaakalongezya bana ba-Josefa. Lino kusule lyayaaya Josefa wakaambilwa kuti, Sa tobwene kuti uso waciswa?																									
Mpawo wakatolelela bana bakwe bobile Manase a-Efrai­ mu. Elyo Jakobo wakalwiidwa kuti,																									
Mwanaako Josefa wasika kuzookubona. Amvwe obo, Israyeli wakaliyumya-yumya, wanongomana abule.																									
Nkabela Jakobo wakaambila Josefa kuti, Leza Singuzuzyoonse wakalibonya kulindime ku-Luzi munyika ya-Kanana, wandilongezya,																									
wandaambila kuti, Ncobeni njookuzyazya loko, ube banji; njoocita kuti ube misyobo misyobo yabantu, alimwi nyika eyi njooipa lunyungu lwako, kuti lwiivube lyoonse alyoonse.																									
Lino aba bana bako bobile mbowakazyala munyika ya-Egepita, nkentanasika kulinduwe okuno ku-Egepita, mbibangu, Efraimu a-Manase mbibangu mbubonya mbuli Rubeni aSimeoni.																									
Alunyungu lwako ndoyoozyala musule lyabo ndolwako. Bayooulikwa mbuli mazina aabakulana babo.																									
Nkaambo ciindi eco nindakazwa ku-Padani, ndakafwidwa Rakele munyika ya-Kanana,																									
nitwakacili munzila, nikwakacisyeede kasinzo kusika ku-Efrata, nkabela ndakamuzika nkukonya oko munzila yakuya ku-Efrata (ngonguwo Betelehemu).																									
Elyo Israyeli naakabona bana ba-Josefa, wakabuzya kuti, Ino mbani aba?																									
Nkabela Josefa wakavwiila wisi kuti, Mbombabo bana bangu Leza mbaakandipa okuno.																									
Wakati, Wence balete kulindime, mbalongezye. Nkabela meso aa-Israyeli akali agubi nkaambo kakucembaala, katakonzya kubona.																									
Elyo Josefa wakabaswenya afwiifwi, nkabela wakabamyonta, wabakumbata. Mpawo Israyeli																									
wakaambila Josefa kuti, Teendakali kuyeeya kubona busyu bwako, pele Leza wandibonya alunyungu lwako.																									
Lino Josefa wakabagwisya kumazwi aakwe, walikotamika ansi cakuvundama.																									
Nkabela Josefa wakabeenzya boonse bobile, Efraimu mujanza lyakwe lyalulyo kuya																									
kucimwensi cakwe ca-Israyeli, a-Manase mujanza lyakwe lyacimwensi kuya kululyo lwa-Israyeli, wabaswenya afwiifwi kulinguwe.																									
Mpawo Israyeli wakatandabika ijanza lyakwe lyalulyo, wajata amutwe wa-Efraimu, ngonguwe mwanike, alyalo ijanza lyakwe lyacimwensi wakalijatya amutwe wa-Manase,																									
aboobo wakapinganya maanza aakwe, nkaambo Manase kali mutaanzi, Lino wakalongezya Josefa, wati,																									
Leza ngubakabelekela bamataata Abrahamu a-Izaka, Leza iwakandeembela kuzwa kubwanike bwangu akusikila sunu,																									
Angelo iwakandivuna kububi boonse,longezye balombe,																									
Kuti izina lyangu azina lyamatata Abrahamu a-Izaka likalilile mulimbabo
