Ulawisya buyumu bwaŋanda njebakali kusyoma. Uubamba kabotu mulomo wakwe alulimi lwakwe Ulalivuna kumapenzi.
Sikulisumpula uulikankaizya, izina lyakwe ngusikasampusampu; Ulacita cabukali acakulisumpula.
Cisusi camutolo cilamujaya, Nkaambo maanza aakwe alakaka kubeleka,
Ciindi coonse sizibi uleemuzya, Pele mululami ula pa, takasyi pe.
Cipaizyo casizibi cilasesemya, Kwaambisya na wacileta amoyo wabubi.
Kamboni sikubeja ulanyonyooka, Pele majwi aamuntu uuswiilila alakalilila,
Muntu sizibi ulayumya busyu bwakwe, Pele uululeme ulayeeya kabotu inzila zyakwe.
Taakwe busongo, taakwe luzibo, Taakwe lulayo lukonzya kubisizya Jehova.
Ibbiza lilabambilwa buzuba bwa nkondo, Pele Jehova nguupa lufutuko.
Izina bbotu lilayandika kwiinda buvubi bunji, Aluzyalo ndubotu kwiinda insiliva angolida.
Batengwana abavubi balaswanaana; Jehova ngumulengi wabo boonse.
Muntu uucenjede, abona mapenzi, ulayuba, Pele bataiyide balaindilila aboobo balapenga.
Kulibombya akuyoowa Jehova Kulaleta buvubi abulemu abuumi.
Mamvwa atukole, zyoonse mozili munzila yabapilingene, Pele uulibamba kabotu uli kule kulinzizyo.
Iyisya mwana aende munzila iielede, Lino akomena takooyooleya mulinjiyo.
Muvubi uleendelezya mutengwana; Sizikoloto ngumuzike wasikukolotya.
Uubyala zitaluleme ulatebula mapenzi; Musako wabukali bwakwe ulamaninina.
Syacaaba ulajana coolwe, Nkaambo ulaabana zilyo zyakwe abatengwana.
Tanda sikasampusampu, lino inkondo ilamana; Kukazyanya akulwana zyoonse zilaleka.
Uuyandisya kusalala kwamoyo, alimwi uli amwaambo waluzyalo, Mwami ulaba muzwalani wakwe,
Meso aa-Jehova alalanga luzibo, Pele ulanyonyoona majwi aabasilweeno,
Mutolo ulaamba kuti, Kuli mulavu anze! Njoojayilwa mumigwagwa. Mulomo wamwanakazi mweenzu ncilindi cilamfu;
Uukalalilwa Jehova ulawida mulincico. Bufubafuba bulaangidwe mumoyo wamwana, Pele musako wakukomya ulabutanda,
Uupenzya bacete kuti alivuzizye imbono, Ayooyo uupa bavubi, ulasikilwa kubula buyo.
Tusimpi atumwi twamisyobo misyobo. Cenjeka kutwi kwako, ukaswiilile majwi aabasongo;
Bika moyo wako kuluzibo lwangu; Nkaambo cilabota na wabamba makani mukati kako,
Alimwi oonse alibambidwe kumilomo yako. Kuti usyome Jehova, Ncencico ncindakuzibisya makani aya ayebo sunu.
Sa nsina kukulembela makani aali makumi otatwe, Makani aalulayo aluzibo, Kuti nkuzibye ciluleme acalusinizyo,
Uvuwe majwi aalusinizyo kulibaabo bakutuma. Utabbidi mucete, nkaambo mutengwana, Nekuba kuuma bapengede mumulyango,
Nkaambo Jehova uyoobeteka makani nabo. Akunyanzya basikubanyanzya buumi. Utatangi buzwalani amuntu mukati,
Nekuba kweenda amuntu silunyemo, Kuti utaiyi inzila zyakwe, Akulyaanga mukakole.
Utabi umwi wabaabo bapa zitondezyo, Basyomezya kuliyila basizikoloto. Na wabula cakuliya,
Sa ncibotu kunyanzigwa bulo bwako? Utasunzululi munyinza wakale Ngobakabika bamauso,
Sa ulibwene muntu uusungwaala mumilimo yakwe? Oyo muntu ulaima kunembo lyabami, Takooyooima kunembo lyabantu buyo pe.
Na wakala kukulya amweendelezi, Yeeya kabotu cilyo ncowabikilwa; Lino utaingani, Na uli sindya;
Utasukami zilyo zyakwe zilweela, Nkaambo nzilyo zyalweeno. Utalikataazyi kuti ube muvubi;
Leka mubusongo bwako, Imbono zyabonwa buyo, zilamana ndilyonya, Zilalicitila mababa,
Zilauluka mbuli sikwaze uuya kujulu, Utalyi zilyo zyasyacivulamwangu; Utasukami zilyo zyakwe zilweela;
Nkaambo ulayeeya-yeeya mumoyo wakwe, Ulaamba kuti, Kolya akunywa, Nekubaboobo moyo wakwe tuuli ayebo.
Minsuma njowalya ulailuka, Alimwi ulasowa buyo majwi aako mabotu, Utaambi mumatwi aamufubafuba,
Nkaambo ulasampaula busongo bwamajwi aako, Utasunzululi munyinza wakale, Nekuba kunjila mumyuunda yabamucaala,
Nkaambo Munununi wabo ngusinguzu, Ulabeteka makani aabo kulinduwe, Bika moyo wako kululayo,
Akucenjeka kutwi kwako kumajwi aaluzibo, Utakaki kukoma mwana; Na wamuuma amusako, takoofwa pe;
Na wamuuma amusako, Ulavuna buumi bwakwe kulufu. Mwanaangu, na moyo wako uli abusongo,
Moyo wangu ambebo ulakondwa. Njookondwa mukati kansa zyangu, Na milomo yako ilaamba ziluleme.
Moyo wako utafwidi basizibi ibbivwe, Pele kaka tila kukuyoowa Jehova buzuba boonse,
Nkaambo mamanino ayooboneka, Nkabela bulangizi bwako tabukooyooloba,
Swiilila, mwanaangu, ujate busongo; Enzya moyo wako munzila, Utakali akati kabacakolwa,
Nanka akati kamadyanyama, Nkaambo mukolwi asindya bayoosikilwa bucete, Alimwi butolo bulasamika muntu madeludelu.
Swiilila uso iwakakuzyala, Alimwi utasampauli banyoko na bacembaala. Koula lusinizyo, utaluulisyi pe;
Koula busongo alulayo abupampu. Wisi mululami ulasekelela loko; Uuzyala musongo ulajana kukondwa mulinguwe,
Uso abanyoko basekelele; lwakakuzyala akondwe. Mwanaangu, undipe moyo wako; Meso aako alange inzila zyangu,
Nkaambo mwanakazi muvuule ncilindi cilamfu; Mwanakazi uuzwakule mugodi uusyanikide,
Ulalindila mbuli sikubba, Ulavuzya batasyomeki akati kabantu. Ngwani uuli abuusu? Ngwani uuli amapenzi?
Ngwani uuli ankondo? Ngwani uuli akutongauka? Ngwani uuli amibunda katakwe kaambo?
Ngwani uuli ameso aasalala pyu? Mbembabo bakala ciindi cilamfu kukunywa, Baya kukuyandaula waini uuvwelene,
Utalangi waini ciindi naasalala, Naanjoloma munkomeki, Naatelemuka kabotu. Kumamanino ulaluma mbuli inzoka,
Ulazapula mbuli cipile. Meso aako alabona zintu ziyoosya, Amoyo wako ulaamba makani aapilingene.
Ulaba mbuli muntu uulala mukati kalwizi, Na mbuli muntu uulala akasamu kandembela.
Ulati, Bakanduuma pele teendakaciswa, Bakandiyasa pele teendakamvwa, Nsinsimuke lili? Nkayandaule cakunywa alimwi.
Tusimpi twa-Solomoni ntubakalembulula bantu ba-Hezekiya.
Ntootu tusimpi atumwi twa-Solomoni ntubakalembulula bantu baHezekiya mwami wa-Juda.
Kusisa makani nkokulemeka Leza, Pele kuyubununa makani nkokulemeka bantu,
Kujulu nkulamfu, ayalo nyika yalampa ansi; Mbubonya obo myoyo yabami tiiyubunuki.
Na wagwisya mankwisila munsiliva, Mulazwa cibelesyo camufuzi; Na wagwisya basizibi kumeso aamwami,
Cuuno cakwe cilaimikwa nji mubululami, Utalilemeki kubusyu bwamwami, Nekuba kwiima mubusena bwabalemu,
Nkaambo ncibotu kwaambilwa kuti, Swena okuno, Kwiinda kufwinsigwa kumeso aamweendelezi.
Ncaabwene meso aako, Utafwambaani kucileta kunkuta; Nkaambo ulacitanzi kumamanino,
Na mweenzinyoko wakuusya bweeme? Buzyanya makani amweenzinyoko mwini;
Utayubununi makani aasisidwe aamuntu umbi; Ambweni uukuswiilila ulakuusya insoni,
Nkabela bweeme bwako tabukooyoomana. Mbuli micelo yangolida mucisuwo cansiliva,
Mbwaabede majwi aambwa kuciindi ceelede. Mbuli bunono bwangolida nanka cilisakatizyo cangolida loko,
Mbwabede sikutapatila musongo kukutwi kuswiilila, Mbuli caanda citontola kuciindi cakutebula,
Mbwabede mutumwa uusyomeka kulibaabo bamutuma; Ulabusya myoyo yabami bakwe.
Mbuli mayoba amuuwo uutakwe imvula, Mbwabede muntu uulisumpwida cipo cakweena.
Kukazika moyo nkoongelezya mweendelezi; Lulimi Iutete lulabombya zifuwa.
Na wajana buci, kolya mbokweelede; Atene ulakutisya, ulaluka. Maulu aako ateendi lyoonse kuŋanda yamweezinyoko,
Kuti atakucimwi akukusula, Mbuli inkoli na ipanga na muvwi uubosya, Mbwabede muntu uulengelela mweenzinyina kaambo cakubeja.
Kusyoma muntu silweeno kuciindi camapenzi, Kuli mbuli lino ibbi nanka mweendo uutezemuka.
Mbuli muntu uusamununa cikobela mubuzuba bwampeyo, Na mbuli ndulwe acilonda,
Mbwabede uuimbila moyo uusa. Anooli sinkondonyoko wafwa inzala, umusanine; Afwa nyota, umunywisye;
Nkaambo kukucita obo ulalundika makala aamulilo amutwe wakwe, Nkabela Jehova uyookulumbula.
Muuwo wakunyika ulaleta imvula; Lulimi luvwiya lulaleta busyu bukali. Kukala acooko calululi lwaŋanda nkubotu
Kwiinda kukala amwanakazi silwaambwe muŋanda impati, Mbuli maanzi aatontola kumuntu uukateede,
Mbwaabede makani mabotu aazwa kucisi cakule. Mbuli kalonga kasofwaazigwa na kasensa kali antimba,
Mbwabede muntu uululeme uuzumizya basizibi. Tacili cibotu kulya buci bunji; Utalemezyi bantu loko.
Mbuli munzi uumwayidwe uubula bulambo, Mbwabede muntu uuteendelezyi moyo wakwe.
Mbuli caanda kuciindi cacilimo nanka imvula kuciindi cakutebula, Bulemu tabweelede mufubafuba.
Mbuli kayuni kapembelela, na mbuli sikamembya mukuuluka kwakwe, Mbulubede lutuko lwabuyo; talusiki pe,
Ciswepu cileelede ibbiza, lubulo luleelede mukanwa lyambongolo, Amusako uleelede musana wamufubafuba.
Utavuwi mufubafuba mbuli bufubafuba bwakwe, Kuti uteelani awe ayebo. Vuwa mufubafuba mbuli bufubafuba bwakwe,
Kuti atasongwaali mumeso aakwe mwini. Uutuma makani kumulomo wamufubafuba Ulakosola zituta zyakwe, alimwi ulanywa lunyonyongano.
Maulu aacilema alalengelela buyo; Mbukabede kasimpi mumilomo yabafubafuba. Mbuli muntu uuanga ibbwe munkwilipo,
Mbwabede uupa mufubafuba bulemu, Mbuli bumvwa buyasa ijanza lyamukolwi, Mbukabede kasimpi mumilomo yabafubafuba,
Mbuli simata uuyasa boonse buyo, Mbwabede muntu uubelesya mufubafuba ayooyo uubelesya mweendanzila.
Mbuli mubwa uuboola kubulusi bwakwe, Mbwabede mufubafuba uuindulula bufubafuba bwakwe,
Sa ulibwene muntu musongo mumeso aakwe mwini? Mufubafuba ulasyomeka kwiinda nguwe.
Mutolo ulaamba kuti, Kuli mulavu munzila, Kuli butambo mumigwagwa! Mbuli ikoma mbolizumuka,
Mbwabede mutolo abulo bwakwe, Mutolo ulanjizya ijanza lyakwe mumbede, Pele cilamukataazya kuliboozya kumulomo wakwe,
Mutolo musongo mumeso aakwe mwini Kwiinda bantu bali musanu ababili bezi kuvuwa kabotu,
Uukazyanya munkondo iitali yakwe Uli mbuli uujata mubwa kumatwi uuinda. Mbuli sicinsondo uuwaala-waala zisisi amivwi alufu,
Mbwabede muntu uuena mweenzinyina Akwaamba kuti, Ndasekana buyo. Na taakwe inkuni, mulilo ulazima;
Na taakwe sikuvwiya, inkondo ilamana. Mbuli masizi kumakala aayaka, ambuli inkuni kumulilo, Mbwabede sikukazyanya kukubusya inkondo.
Majwi aasikuvwiya ali mbuli zilyo zinono, Alanjila mukati kabula. Mbuli cibelesyo cabulongo cizilulwidwe ansiliva,
Mbwiibede milomo myuuba antoomwe amoyo mubi. Uusula akuupaupa amilomo Akusisa lweeno mumoyo wakwe,
Nekuba kuti ulaamba cabuuya, utamusyomi, Nkaambo muli zisesemyo zili musanu azibili mumoyo wakwe;
Nekuba kuti lusulo lwakwe lulisisidwe alweeno, Bubi bwakwe bulayubununwa mumbungano yabantu,
Uusya cilindi ulawida mulincico; Uukunkulisya ibbwe, lilamupilukila. Lulimi lubeja lulisulide abo mbolupwayide; Amulomo muuba ulaleta lunyonyooko.
Utalikankaizizyi zyajunza, Nkaambo tozi na buzuba bulaleta nzi. Muntu umbi akutembaule, mulomo wako omwini pe;
Mweenzu, kutali kumilomo yako, Ibbwe ndidemu, awalo musee ulalema, Pele bukali bwamufubafuba mbulemu kwiinda zyoonse.
Bukali bulayoosya, lunyemo lulakataazya; Pele ibbivwe, ngwani uukonzya kwiima kulindilyo?
Kutapatila kaanzambwene Nkubotu kwiinda luyando lusisidwe. Kuyasa kwamuzwalani kulasyomeka,
Pele imyonto zyasinkondonyoko zilavula. Muntu uukutide ulasesemwa buci, Pele kulisinzala zintu zilula zyoonse nzinono,
Mbuli kayuni kaswekede kuciteente cako, Mbwabede muntu uuswekede kuzwa kulinguwe,
Mafuta atununkilizyo zilabotezya moyo; Mbulubede lulayo lwamweenzinyoko uuyandika.
Mweenzinyoko, amweenzinyina uso, utabalekelezyi; Alimwi utayi kuŋanda yamunyoko mubuzuba bwamapenzi.
Mweenzinyoko uuli kufwaafwi mubotu Kwiinda munyoko uuli kule. Songwaala, mwanaangu, ukondezye moyo wangu,
Kuti mbe aluvwiilo kuliyooyo uundisampaula. Muntu uucenjede, abona mapenzi, ulayuba,
Pele bataiyide balaindilila aboobo balapenga, Nyanzya muntu cikobela cakwe na wasyomezya kuliyila mweenzu;
Umujate na walisyomezya mumwanakazi muzwakule. Muntu uufuma akulongezya mweenzinyina ajwi ipati, Cilaambwa kuti ulatuka buyo,
Mbuli mandomondomo mubuzuba bwamvula,Mbwabede mwanakazi sikukazyanya; Uumukasya ulakasya muuwo,
Uli mbuli mafuta mumaanza aakwe. Lubulo lulanona lubulonyina, Mbubonya obo muntu ulanona busyu bwamweenzinyina,
Uubamba mukuyu ulalya micelo yawo, Ayooyo uubamba simalelaakwe ulalemekwa, Mbuli busyu mbububoneka mumaanzi,
Mbubonya obo moyo wamuntu mbuuboneka kumuntunyina. Kwacimvumwe alufu tazikuti;
Aalo meso aamuntu taakuti, Cuumpilo ncansiliva, ceengelo ncangolida, Pele muntu ulasunkwa kumpuwo yakwe,
Nekuba kuti watwa mufubafuba muncili amunsi antoomwe amaila, Bufubafuba bwakwe tabumani pe,
Ncobeni uleelede kuziba imbelele zyako mbozibede, Akubika moyo wako kumatanga aako;
Nkaambo imbono tazikalilili lyoonse, Amunsini tuuli kumazyalani oonse. Bwizu bwamana kuligwa, mweemvwe ulamena,
Azisyu zyakuzilundu zyacelwa, Tubelele tulakupa zyakusama, Ampongo zilaleta muulo wamuunda;
Malili aampongo alakuvulila, Alaba zilyo zyabasiŋanda bako. Akulela bana bako basimbi,
Basizibi balacija nekuba kuti taakwe uubatanda, Pele baluleme balaima mbuli mulavu.
Na cisi cabisya, cilijisi beendelezi banji, Pele mumaanza aabantu basongo abasiluzibo cilakalilila,
Mutengwana uupenzya mucetenyina Uli mbuli imvula yamucobocobo litapi zilyo.
Basowa mulao balatembaula basizibi, Pele basikubamba mulao balakazyanya abo.
Bantu babi tabamvwisyi kubeteka, Pele basikuyandaula Jehova balamvwisya.
Muntu mutengwana uuenda cakululama. Mubotu kwiinda muntu muvubi uupilingene.
Uubamba mulao mwana musongo, Pele uuenda abasindya ulausya wisi insoni.
Uuvuzya imbono zyakwe kukujana impindu zyazikwelete. Ulaziyobweda sikufwida bacete luzyalo.
Na muntu wasinka matwi aakwe kukumvwa mulao, Acikombyo cakwe cilaba cisesemyo.
Uuongelezya baluleme kubatola muzibi, Ulawida mumonya mucilindi ncaakasya, Pele baluleme balajana lukono lubotu,
Muntu muvubi musongo mumeso aakwe mwini, Pele mutengwana uucenjede ulamvwisya mbwabede.
Na baluleme bazunda, bulemu bulavula, Pele na basizibi babuka, bantu balayuba, Uusisa milandu yakwe takooyooba acoolwe pe,
Pele oyo uulyaambawida akuleka ulafwidwa luzyalo. Uli acoolwe muntu uuyoowa lyoonse,
Pele oyo uuyumya moyo wakwe ulawida mumapenzi. Mbuli mulavu uuvuluma na masekese uulwisya,
Mbwabede muntu mubi uuendelezya bacete. Silutwe uubula busongo ulapenzya loko,
Pele oyo uusula impindu iitaluleme uloongola. Muntu uuli amulandu wabulowa bwamweenzinyina,
Acije akusikila kulufu; Kutabi muntu uumugwasya, Uuenda cakululama ulafutulwa, Pele uupilingene munzila zyakwe ulawida mucilindi.
Uulima nyika yakwe ulakuta cilyo, Pele uutobela zintu zyabuyo ulakuta bucete. Muntu uusyomeka ulaba azyoolwe zinji,
Pele uufwaamba kuvuba ulajana mulandu. Tacili cibotu kulanga ziimo zyabantu; Muntu ulabisya kuti ajane kalyo,
Syacivulamwangu ulafwamba kujana imbono, Pele tezi kuti kubula kulamusikila, Uutapatila muntu, kumamanino ulayandwa,
Kwiinda oyo uubombeka-bombeka alulimi lwakwe, Kufumbwa uubbida wisi abanyina,
Akwaamba kuti, Taakwe mulandu, Oyo ngumweenzinyina sikunyonyoona, Syacivulamwangu ulabusya inkondo,
Pele uusyoma Jehova ulaneneesegwa, Uusyoma moyo wakwe mwini mufubafuba, Pele oyo uuenda mubusongo ulavunwa,
Uuabila batengwana takooyoobula, Pele uusisa meso aakwe ulajana intuko zinji, Na basizibi babuka, bantu balayuba, Pele na banyonyooka, baluleme balavula.
